## 2003: Jesus Christ, qualities of (id: 2003)

* 2006: God, the Son
* **Associated Articles:** 2006: God, the Son (ID: `2006@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 2006: God, the Son (id: 2006)

The co\-equal and co\-eternal Son of the Father, who became incarnate in Jesus Christ for the redemption of the world. Scripture stresses both the divinity and the humanity of the incarnate Son of God, and the necessity and total sufficiency of his atoning death for human redemption. Through his resurrection and ascension, he interecedes for believers at the right hand of God.

* **Associated Articles:** 2009: Jesus Christ, anger of (ID: `2009@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2012: Jesus Christ, authority of (ID: `2012@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2015: Jesus Christ, compassion of (ID: `2015@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2018: Jesus Christ, divinity of (ID: `2018@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2021: Jesus Christ, faithfulness of (ID: `2021@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2024: Jesus Christ, glory of (ID: `2024@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2027: Jesus Christ, grace and mercy of (ID: `2027@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2030: Jesus Christ, holiness of (ID: `2030@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2033: Jesus Christ, humanity of (ID: `2033@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2036: Jesus Christ, humility of (ID: `2036@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2039: Jesus Christ, joy of (ID: `2039@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2042: Jesus Christ, justice of (ID: `2042@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2045: Jesus Christ, knowledge of (ID: `2045@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2048: Jesus Christ, love of (ID: `2048@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2051: Jesus Christ, majesty of (ID: `2051@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2054: Jesus Christ, mind of (ID: `2054@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2057: Jesus Christ, obedience of (ID: `2057@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2060: Jesus Christ, patience of (ID: `2060@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2063: Jesus Christ, perfection of (ID: `2063@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2066: Jesus Christ, power of (ID: `2066@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2069: Jesus Christ, pre-eminence of (ID: `2069@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2072: Jesus Christ, righteousness of (ID: `2072@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2075: Jesus Christ, sinlessness of (ID: `2075@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2078: Jesus Christ, sonship of (ID: `2078@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2081: Jesus Christ, wisdom of (ID: `2081@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 2009: Jesus Christ, anger of (id: 2009)

Jesus Christ's controlled emotion arising from his unswerving opposition to evil and his determination to eradicate it.

Causes of Jesus Christ's anger
------------------------------

### Petty legalism in religious observance

[MAT 15:3](https://ref.ly/Matt15:3), [MAT 23:1–23:4](https://ref.ly/Matt23:1-Matt23:4); ; [MRK 3:4–3:5](https://ref.ly/Mark3:4-Mark3:5)

### Attempts to prevent access to him

[MRK 10:14](https://ref.ly/Mark10:14)

### People leading others into sin

[MAT 18:6–18:7](https://ref.ly/Matt18:6-Matt18:7) parallels [MRK 9:42](https://ref.ly/Mark9:42), [LUK 17:1–17:2](https://ref.ly/Luke17:1-Luke17:2)

Demonstrations of Jesus Christ's anger
--------------------------------------

### Purging the temple

[MAT 21:12–21:13](https://ref.ly/Matt21:12-Matt21:13) parallels [MRK 11:15–11:17](https://ref.ly/Mark11:15-Mark11:17), [LUK 19:45–19:46](https://ref.ly/Luke19:45-Luke19:46); ; [JHN 2:14–2:16](https://ref.ly/John2:14-John2:16)

### Cursing the fig\-tree

[MRK 11:14](https://ref.ly/Mark11:14) parallel [MAT 21:19](https://ref.ly/Matt21:19)

Jesus Christ's words in anger
-----------------------------

### Against demons

**[MAT 17:18](https://ref.ly/Matt17:18)** parallels [MRK 9:25](https://ref.ly/Mark9:25), [LUK 9:42](https://ref.ly/Luke9:42) *See also* [MRK 1:25–1:26](https://ref.ly/Mark1:25-Mark1:26) parallel [LUK 4:35](https://ref.ly/Luke4:35)

### Against disciples

**[LUK 9:55–9:56](https://ref.ly/Luke9:55-Luke9:56)** *See also* [MAT 16:23](https://ref.ly/Matt16:23) parallel [MRK 8:33](https://ref.ly/Mark8:33)

### Against Pharisees

**[MAT 23:13](https://ref.ly/Matt23:13)** *See also* [MAT 12:34](https://ref.ly/Matt12:34), [MAT 15:7–15:9](https://ref.ly/Matt15:7-Matt15:9) parallel [MRK 7:6–7:8](https://ref.ly/Mark7:6-Mark7:8); [MAT 23:15–23:16](https://ref.ly/Matt23:15-Matt23:16), [MAT 23:23–23:33](https://ref.ly/Matt23:23-Matt23:33); [LUK 11:42–11:44](https://ref.ly/Luke11:42-Luke11:44), [LUK 13:15](https://ref.ly/Luke13:15); [JHN 8:44](https://ref.ly/John8:44)

### Against unbelief

**[MAT 17:17](https://ref.ly/Matt17:17)** parallels [MRK 9:19](https://ref.ly/Mark9:19), [LUK 9:41](https://ref.ly/Luke9:41) *See also* [MAT 12:39–12:45](https://ref.ly/Matt12:39-Matt12:45) parallel [LUK 11:29–11:32](https://ref.ly/Luke11:29-Luke11:32); [MRK 8:38](https://ref.ly/Mark8:38); [LUK 11:50–11:51](https://ref.ly/Luke11:50-Luke11:51)

### Against false prophets

**[MAT 7:15](https://ref.ly/Matt7:15)**

### Against the rich

**[LUK 6:24–6:26](https://ref.ly/Luke6:24-Luke6:26)**

### Against unrepentant cities

**[MAT 11:20](https://ref.ly/Matt11:20)** *See also* [MAT 11:21–11:24](https://ref.ly/Matt11:21-Matt11:24) parallel [LUK 10:13–10:15](https://ref.ly/Luke10:13-Luke10:15)

Jesus Christ reflects the anger of God
--------------------------------------

**[JHN 3:36](https://ref.ly/John3:36)** *See also* [MAT 5:21–5:22](https://ref.ly/Matt5:21-Matt5:22), [MAT 5:29](https://ref.ly/Matt5:29), [MAT 22:7](https://ref.ly/Matt22:7), [MAT 22:13](https://ref.ly/Matt22:13), [MAT 25:30](https://ref.ly/Matt25:30), [MAT 25:46](https://ref.ly/Matt25:46); [LUK 21:23](https://ref.ly/Luke21:23)

The anger of the glorified Christ
---------------------------------

### Against the unbelieving world

**[REV 6:16](https://ref.ly/Rev6:16)**

### Against the wayward church

**[REV 2:16](https://ref.ly/Rev2:16)** *See also* [REV 2:5](https://ref.ly/Rev2:5), [REV 2:22–2:23](https://ref.ly/Rev2:22-Rev2:23), [REV 3:3](https://ref.ly/Rev3:3), [REV 3:16](https://ref.ly/Rev3:16)

* **Associated Passages:** Matthew 15:3; Matthew 23:1-4; Mark 3:4-5; Mark 10:14; Matthew 18:6-7; Mark 9:42; Luke 17:1-2; Matthew 21:12-13; Mark 11:15-17; Luke 19:45-46; John 2:14-16; Mark 11:14; Matthew 21:19; Matthew 17:18; Mark 9:25; Luke 9:42; Mark 1:25-26; Luke 4:35; Luke 9:55-56; Matthew 16:23; Mark 8:33; Matthew 23:13; Matthew 12:34; Matthew 15:7-9; Mark 7:6-8; Matthew 23:15-16; Matthew 23:23-33; Luke 11:42-44; Luke 13:15; John 8:44; Matthew 17:17; Mark 9:19; Luke 9:41; Matthew 12:39-45; Luke 11:29-32; Mark 8:38; Luke 11:50-51; Matthew 7:15; Luke 6:24-26; Matthew 11:20; Matthew 11:21-24; Luke 10:13-15; John 3:36; Matthew 5:21-22; Matthew 5:29; Matthew 22:7; Matthew 22:13; Matthew 25:30; Matthew 25:46; Luke 21:23; Revelation 6:16; Revelation 2:16; Revelation 2:5; Revelation 2:22-23; Revelation 3:3; Revelation 3:16

## 2012: Jesus Christ, authority of (id: 2012)

The right of Jesus Christ to speak and act on his Father's behalf in forgiving sin, pronouncing judgment and promising eternal life to those who believe in him.

Jesus Christ's authority underlines his divine status
-----------------------------------------------------

**[JHN 8:28](https://ref.ly/John8:28)** *See also* [JHN 8:58](https://ref.ly/John8:58), [JHN 14:6](https://ref.ly/John14:6); [1CO 1:24](https://ref.ly/1Cor1:24); [COL 2:10](https://ref.ly/Col2:10)

The origin of Jesus Christ's authority
--------------------------------------

### It is given by God the Father

**[JHN 3:35](https://ref.ly/John3:35)** *See also* [MAT 28:18](https://ref.ly/Matt28:18); [LUK 10:22](https://ref.ly/Luke10:22); [JHN 5:26–5:27](https://ref.ly/John5:26-John5:27), [JHN 7:16](https://ref.ly/John7:16), [JHN 10:18](https://ref.ly/John10:18), [JHN 12:49–12:50](https://ref.ly/John12:49-John12:50), [JHN 17:2](https://ref.ly/John17:2)

### It is limited by the Father

**[MRK 10:40](https://ref.ly/Mark10:40)** *See also* [MAT 24:36](https://ref.ly/Matt24:36) parallel [MRK 13:32](https://ref.ly/Mark13:32); [PHP 2:6–2:8](https://ref.ly/Phil2:6-Phil2:8)

### It is questioned by others

**[MAT 12:24–12:28](https://ref.ly/Matt12:24-Matt12:28)** parallels [MRK 3:22–3:26](https://ref.ly/Mark3:22-Mark3:26), [LUK 11:15–11:20](https://ref.ly/Luke11:15-Luke11:20) *See also* [MAT 21:23–21:27](https://ref.ly/Matt21:23-Matt21:27) parallels [MRK 11:27–11:33](https://ref.ly/Mark11:27-Mark11:33), [LUK 20:1–20:8](https://ref.ly/Luke20:1-Luke20:8); [JHN 2:18](https://ref.ly/John2:18)

The authority of Jesus Christ is seen in his works
--------------------------------------------------

### He has authority over nature

[MAT 8:23–8:27](https://ref.ly/Matt8:23-Matt8:27) parallels [MRK 4:36–4:41](https://ref.ly/Mark4:36-Mark4:41), [LUK 8:22–8:25](https://ref.ly/Luke8:22-Luke8:25); ; [MAT 14:22–14:33](https://ref.ly/Matt14:22-Matt14:33) parallels [MRK 6:45–6:51](https://ref.ly/Mark6:45-Mark6:51), [JHN 6:15–6:21](https://ref.ly/John6:15-John6:21); ; [MAT 21:18–21:22](https://ref.ly/Matt21:18-Matt21:22) parallels [MRK 11:12–11:14](https://ref.ly/Mark11:12-Mark11:14), [MRK 11:20–11:24](https://ref.ly/Mark11:20-Mark11:24)

### He has authority over sin

[MAT 9:1–9:8](https://ref.ly/Matt9:1-Matt9:8) parallels [MRK 2:3–2:12](https://ref.ly/Mark2:3-Mark2:12), [LUK 5:18–5:26](https://ref.ly/Luke5:18-Luke5:26); ; [LUK 7:37–7:38](https://ref.ly/Luke7:37-Luke7:38), [LUK 7:44–7:50](https://ref.ly/Luke7:44-Luke7:50)

### He has authority over sickness

[MAT 8:14–8:15](https://ref.ly/Matt8:14-Matt8:15) parallels [MRK 1:30–1:31](https://ref.ly/Mark1:30-Mark1:31), [LUK 4:38–4:39](https://ref.ly/Luke4:38-Luke4:39); ; [MAT 20:29–20:34](https://ref.ly/Matt20:29-Matt20:34) parallels [MRK 10:46–10:52](https://ref.ly/Mark10:46-Mark10:52), [LUK 18:35–18:43](https://ref.ly/Luke18:35-Luke18:43); ; [ACT 3:16](https://ref.ly/Acts3:16), [ACT 4:30](https://ref.ly/Acts4:30)

### He has authority over evil

[MRK 1:23–1:27](https://ref.ly/Mark1:23-Mark1:27) parallel [LUK 4:33–4:36](https://ref.ly/Luke4:33-Luke4:36); ; [LUK 10:17](https://ref.ly/Luke10:17)

### He has authority over death

[MAT 9:18–9:25](https://ref.ly/Matt9:18-Matt9:25) parallels [MRK 5:22–5:42](https://ref.ly/Mark5:22-Mark5:42), [LUK 8:40–8:55](https://ref.ly/Luke8:40-Luke8:55); ; [MAT 28:1–28:7](https://ref.ly/Matt28:1-Matt28:7) parallels [MRK 16:1–16:6](https://ref.ly/Mark16:1-Mark16:6), [LUK 24:1–24:8](https://ref.ly/Luke24:1-Luke24:8), [JHN 20:1–20:17](https://ref.ly/John20:1-John20:17); ; [LUK 7:11–7:16](https://ref.ly/Luke7:11-Luke7:16); ; [JHN 11:38–11:44](https://ref.ly/John11:38-John11:44)

The authority of Jesus Christ is seen in his teaching
-----------------------------------------------------

### Jesus Christ claims authority for his own words

**[LUK 4:18](https://ref.ly/Luke4:18)** *See also* [MAT 5:21–5:22](https://ref.ly/Matt5:21-Matt5:22), [MAT 5:27–5:28](https://ref.ly/Matt5:27-Matt5:28), [MAT 12:41–12:42](https://ref.ly/Matt12:41-Matt12:42), [MAT 17:5](https://ref.ly/Matt17:5) parallels [MRK 9:7](https://ref.ly/Mark9:7), [LUK 9:35](https://ref.ly/Luke9:35); [MRK 2:5](https://ref.ly/Mark2:5), [MRK 2:10](https://ref.ly/Mark2:10), [MRK 8:38](https://ref.ly/Mark8:38), [MRK 10:15](https://ref.ly/Mark10:15) *The use of the phrase “I tell you the truth” emphasises Jesus Christ's authority*; [MRK 13:26](https://ref.ly/Mark13:26), [MRK 13:31](https://ref.ly/Mark13:31); [JHN 4:24–4:26](https://ref.ly/John4:24-John4:26), [JHN 6:63](https://ref.ly/John6:63), [JHN 7:15–7:18](https://ref.ly/John7:15-John7:18), [JHN 12:48–12:50](https://ref.ly/John12:48-John12:50), [JHN 13:13](https://ref.ly/John13:13), [JHN 14:6](https://ref.ly/John14:6) *The “I am” sayings in John's Gospel emphasise the divine nature of Jesus Christ's authority*; [JHN 15:3](https://ref.ly/John15:3)

### His authority is recognised by others

**[MAT 7:28–7:29](https://ref.ly/Matt7:28-Matt7:29)** *See also* [MAT 22:33](https://ref.ly/Matt22:33), [MAT 22:46](https://ref.ly/Matt22:46); [MRK 1:22](https://ref.ly/Mark1:22), [MRK 1:27](https://ref.ly/Mark1:27) parallel [LUK 4:32](https://ref.ly/Luke4:32)

### His authority is questioned and opposed by others

[MAT 26:65–26:68](https://ref.ly/Matt26:65-Matt26:68); ; [LUK 4:28–4:30](https://ref.ly/Luke4:28-Luke4:30)

Jesus Christ delegates his authority to others
----------------------------------------------

### His followers preach in his name

[MAT 10:7](https://ref.ly/Matt10:7), [MAT 28:18–28:20](https://ref.ly/Matt28:18-Matt28:20)

### His followers continue his works

[MAT 10:1](https://ref.ly/Matt10:1) parallels [MRK 6:7](https://ref.ly/Mark6:7), [LUK 9:1–9:2](https://ref.ly/Luke9:1-Luke9:2); ; [MAT 10:8](https://ref.ly/Matt10:8); ; [MRK 3:15](https://ref.ly/Mark3:15), [MRK 6:13](https://ref.ly/Mark6:13), [MRK 16:17–16:18](https://ref.ly/Mark16:17-Mark16:18); ; [LUK 10:1–10:12](https://ref.ly/Luke10:1-Luke10:12); ; [JHN 14:12](https://ref.ly/John14:12); ; [ACT 3:6](https://ref.ly/Acts3:6), [ACT 3:16](https://ref.ly/Acts3:16)

### His followers pronounce his forgiveness and judgment

[MAT 18:18](https://ref.ly/Matt18:18); ; [MRK 6:11](https://ref.ly/Mark6:11); ; [LUK 22:28–22:30](https://ref.ly/Luke22:28-Luke22:30); ; [JHN 20:22–20:23](https://ref.ly/John20:22-John20:23); ; [1CO 6:2–6:3](https://ref.ly/1Cor6:2-1Cor6:3)

The results of Jesus Christ's authority
---------------------------------------

### He receives honour and glory

**[JHN 5:22–5:23](https://ref.ly/John5:22-John5:23)** *See also* [JHN 11:4](https://ref.ly/John11:4), [JHN 17:5](https://ref.ly/John17:5)

### He arouses amazement

[MAT 9:33](https://ref.ly/Matt9:33), [MAT 12:23](https://ref.ly/Matt12:23)

### He is opposed

[MAT 12:14](https://ref.ly/Matt12:14) parallels [MRK 3:6](https://ref.ly/Mark3:6), [LUK 6:11](https://ref.ly/Luke6:11)

### He is feared

[LUK 8:37](https://ref.ly/Luke8:37) parallel [MAT 8:34](https://ref.ly/Matt8:34)

### His disciples are opposed

[ACT 16:16–16:24](https://ref.ly/Acts16:16-Acts16:24)

The authority of the exalted Christ
-----------------------------------

### He is Lord

[EPH 1:20](https://ref.ly/Eph1:20); ; [PHP 2:9–2:11](https://ref.ly/Phil2:9-Phil2:11); ; [COL 3:1](https://ref.ly/Col3:1); ; [1PE 3:22](https://ref.ly/1Pet3:22); ; [REV 3:21](https://ref.ly/Rev3:21)

### He is Lord of creation

[COL 1:16–1:17](https://ref.ly/Col1:16-Col1:17)

### He is Lord of the church

[EPH 1:22](https://ref.ly/Eph1:22), [EPH 5:23](https://ref.ly/Eph5:23); ; [COL 1:18](https://ref.ly/Col1:18)

### He is judge

[ACT 10:42](https://ref.ly/Acts10:42), [ACT 17:31](https://ref.ly/Acts17:31)

### He is Saviour

[JHN 3:15](https://ref.ly/John3:15), [JHN 14:3](https://ref.ly/John14:3); ; [COL 1:19–1:20](https://ref.ly/Col1:19-Col1:20); ; [TIT 2:13](https://ref.ly/Titus2:13); ; [HEB 7:24–7:25](https://ref.ly/Heb7:24-Heb7:25), [HEB 9:28](https://ref.ly/Heb9:28)

### He is interceder

[ROM 8:34](https://ref.ly/Rom8:34); ; [HEB 7:25](https://ref.ly/Heb7:25), [HEB 9:24](https://ref.ly/Heb9:24); ; [1JN 2:1](https://ref.ly/1John2:1)

## 2015: Jesus Christ, compassion of (id: 2015)

Jesus Christ's pity and loving concern for the lowly and the needy. His words and deeds show God's merciful and gracious nature in action.

Jesus Christ shows the compassion of God
----------------------------------------

**[2CO 1:3](https://ref.ly/2Cor1:3)** *See also* [2CH 36:15](https://ref.ly/2Chr36:15); [PSA 86:15](https://ref.ly/Ps86:15); [HOS 11:4](https://ref.ly/Hos11:4), [HOS 11:8–11:9](https://ref.ly/Hos11:8-Hos11:9); [LUK 1:72](https://ref.ly/Luke1:72), [LUK 1:78](https://ref.ly/Luke1:78), [LUK 15:20](https://ref.ly/Luke15:20)

The compassion of Jesus Christ is the basis of Christian confidence
-------------------------------------------------------------------

**[HEB 4:14–4:16](https://ref.ly/Heb4:14-Heb4:16)** *The Greek word here translated “sympathise” has the sense of “be compassionate towards”.*

The demonstration of Jesus Christ's compassion
----------------------------------------------

### In supporting the weak

**[MAT 12:20](https://ref.ly/Matt12:20)** *See also* [ISA 42:3](https://ref.ly/Isa42:3); [MAT 19:14](https://ref.ly/Matt19:14) parallels [MRK 10:14](https://ref.ly/Mark10:14), [LUK 18:16](https://ref.ly/Luke18:16)

### In healing the sick

**[MAT 14:14](https://ref.ly/Matt14:14)** parallel [LUK 9:11](https://ref.ly/Luke9:11) *See also* [MAT 20:34](https://ref.ly/Matt20:34) parallels [MRK 10:52](https://ref.ly/Mark10:52), [LUK 18:42–18:43](https://ref.ly/Luke18:42-Luke18:43); [MRK 1:41](https://ref.ly/Mark1:41) parallels [MAT 8:3](https://ref.ly/Matt8:3), [LUK 5:13](https://ref.ly/Luke5:13); [LUK 13:12](https://ref.ly/Luke13:12)

### In comforting the bereaved

**[LUK 7:13](https://ref.ly/Luke7:13)** *See also* [LUK 8:50](https://ref.ly/Luke8:50) parallel [MRK 5:36](https://ref.ly/Mark5:36); [JHN 11:33–11:35](https://ref.ly/John11:33-John11:35), [JHN 19:25–19:27](https://ref.ly/John19:25-John19:27), [JHN 20:14–20:16](https://ref.ly/John20:14-John20:16)

### In feeding the hungry

**[MAT 15:32](https://ref.ly/Matt15:32)** parallel [MRK 8:2–8:3](https://ref.ly/Mark8:2-Mark8:3) *See also* [MAT 14:16](https://ref.ly/Matt14:16) parallels [MRK 6:37](https://ref.ly/Mark6:37), [LUK 9:13](https://ref.ly/Luke9:13), [JHN 6:5–6:6](https://ref.ly/John6:5-John6:6)

### In finding and forgiving lost sinners

**[MAT 9:36](https://ref.ly/Matt9:36)** parallel [MRK 6:34](https://ref.ly/Mark6:34) *See also* [ISA 40:11](https://ref.ly/Isa40:11); [MAT 18:14](https://ref.ly/Matt18:14), [MAT 23:37–23:38](https://ref.ly/Matt23:37-Matt23:38) parallel [LUK 13:34–13:35](https://ref.ly/Luke13:34-Luke13:35); [LUK 7:47–7:48](https://ref.ly/Luke7:47-Luke7:48); [JHN 8:10–8:11](https://ref.ly/John8:10-John8:11)

### In giving rest to those who are burdened or abandoned

**[MAT 11:28–11:29](https://ref.ly/Matt11:28-Matt11:29)** *See also* [MRK 1:40–1:41](https://ref.ly/Mark1:40-Mark1:41) parallels [MAT 8:1–8:3](https://ref.ly/Matt8:1-Matt8:3), [LUK 5:12–5:13](https://ref.ly/Luke5:12-Luke5:13); [LUK 11:46](https://ref.ly/Luke11:46), [LUK 15:1–15:2](https://ref.ly/Luke15:1-Luke15:2), [LUK 17:12–17:14](https://ref.ly/Luke17:12-Luke17:14)

## 2018: Jesus Christ, divinity of (id: 2018)

The equality and identity of Jesus Christ as God is clearly stated in the NT, and is also implied by the words and deeds of Jesus Christ. The OT prophecies also point to the divinity of the coming Messiah.

The NT writers affirm Jesus Christ's divinity
---------------------------------------------

**[HEB 1:8](https://ref.ly/Heb1:8)** *See also* [PSA 45:6](https://ref.ly/Ps45:6); [JHN 1:1–1:2](https://ref.ly/John1:1-John1:2), [JHN 1:18](https://ref.ly/John1:18); [ROM 9:5](https://ref.ly/Rom9:5) *NIV footnote has alternative translations: “Christ who is over all. God be for ever praised!” Or: “Christ. God who is over all be for ever praised!”*; [PHP 2:6](https://ref.ly/Phil2:6); [TIT 2:13](https://ref.ly/Titus2:13); [2PE 1:1](https://ref.ly/2Pet1:1)

Statements which imply Jesus Christ's divinity
----------------------------------------------

**[MAT 1:23](https://ref.ly/Matt1:23)** *See also* [ISA 7:14](https://ref.ly/Isa7:14); [LUK 1:35](https://ref.ly/Luke1:35); [COL 1:15](https://ref.ly/Col1:15), [COL 2:2](https://ref.ly/Col2:2), [COL 2:9](https://ref.ly/Col2:9); [1TI 1:17](https://ref.ly/1Tim1:17); [1JN 5:20](https://ref.ly/1John5:20)

Jesus Christ's unity with the Father and the Holy Spirit in the Godhead
-----------------------------------------------------------------------

**[MAT 28:19](https://ref.ly/Matt28:19)** *See also* [JHN 14:16](https://ref.ly/John14:16); [2CO 13:14](https://ref.ly/2Cor13:14); [EPH 1:13–1:14](https://ref.ly/Eph1:13-Eph1:14), [EPH 2:18](https://ref.ly/Eph2:18), [EPH 2:22](https://ref.ly/Eph2:22), [EPH 3:14–3:17](https://ref.ly/Eph3:14-Eph3:17), [EPH 4:4–4:6](https://ref.ly/Eph4:4-Eph4:6)

Jesus Christ's eternal nature indicates his divinity
----------------------------------------------------

### Jesus Christ precedes creation

**[COL 1:17](https://ref.ly/Col1:17)** *See also* [MIC 5:2](https://ref.ly/Mic5:2); [JHN 17:5](https://ref.ly/John17:5), [JHN 17:24](https://ref.ly/John17:24); [2TI 1:9](https://ref.ly/2Tim1:9); [1PE 1:20](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:20); [1JN 1:1](https://ref.ly/1John1:1), [1JN 2:13](https://ref.ly/1John2:13)

### Jesus Christ is everlasting

**[JHN 8:58](https://ref.ly/John8:58)** *See also* [HEB 1:12](https://ref.ly/Heb1:12); [PSA 102:27](https://ref.ly/Ps102:27); [HEB 7:3](https://ref.ly/Heb7:3), [HEB 7:24](https://ref.ly/Heb7:24), [HEB 13:8](https://ref.ly/Heb13:8); [REV 1:8](https://ref.ly/Rev1:8), [REV 5:13](https://ref.ly/Rev5:13), [REV 22:13](https://ref.ly/Rev22:13)

Jesus Christ's pre\-existence indicates his divinity
----------------------------------------------------

**[JHN 6:62](https://ref.ly/John6:62)** *See also* [JHN 3:13](https://ref.ly/John3:13), [JHN 3:31](https://ref.ly/John3:31), [JHN 6:41–6:42](https://ref.ly/John6:41-John6:42), [JHN 13:3](https://ref.ly/John13:3), [JHN 16:28](https://ref.ly/John16:28)

Jesus Christ's manifestation of God's glory indicates his divinity
------------------------------------------------------------------

**[HEB 1:3](https://ref.ly/Heb1:3)** *See also* [MAT 17:2](https://ref.ly/Matt17:2) parallels [MRK 9:2–9:3](https://ref.ly/Mark9:2-Mark9:3), [LUK 9:29](https://ref.ly/Luke9:29); [JHN 1:14](https://ref.ly/John1:14); [1CO 2:8](https://ref.ly/1Cor2:8); [2CO 4:4](https://ref.ly/2Cor4:4); [JAS 2:1](https://ref.ly/Jas2:1)

Jesus Christ's divinity in the OT
---------------------------------

### The divinity of the coming Messiah

[ISA 9:6](https://ref.ly/Isa9:6), [ISA 40:3](https://ref.ly/Isa40:3); ; [JER 23:6](https://ref.ly/Jer23:6); ; [MAL 3:1](https://ref.ly/Mal3:1)

### NT passages which apply OT passages about God to Jesus Christ

**[ROM 10:13](https://ref.ly/Rom10:13)** *See also* [JOL 2:32](https://ref.ly/Joel2:32); [JHN 12:40–12:41](https://ref.ly/John12:40-John12:41); [ISA 6:10](https://ref.ly/Isa6:10); [ROM 9:33](https://ref.ly/Rom9:33); [ISA 8:14](https://ref.ly/Isa8:14); [EPH 4:8](https://ref.ly/Eph4:8); [PSA 68:18](https://ref.ly/Ps68:18)

Jesus Christ's claims to divinity
---------------------------------

### He claimed to be one with the Father

**[JHN 5:17–5:18](https://ref.ly/John5:17-John5:18)** *See also* [JHN 10:30–10:33](https://ref.ly/John10:30-John10:33), [JHN 10:36–10:38](https://ref.ly/John10:36-John10:38), [JHN 12:45](https://ref.ly/John12:45), [JHN 14:7](https://ref.ly/John14:7), [JHN 14:9–14:11](https://ref.ly/John14:9-John14:11), [JHN 17:11](https://ref.ly/John17:11), [JHN 17:21](https://ref.ly/John17:21)

### He demonstrated his authority to forgive sin

**[LUK 5:20–5:24](https://ref.ly/Luke5:20-Luke5:24)** parallels [MAT 9:2–9:6](https://ref.ly/Matt9:2-Matt9:6), [MRK 2:5–2:10](https://ref.ly/Mark2:5-Mark2:10) *See also* [LUK 7:47–7:48](https://ref.ly/Luke7:47-Luke7:48)

Jesus Christ's actions imply his divinity
-----------------------------------------

**[MAT 8:26–8:27](https://ref.ly/Matt8:26-Matt8:27)** parallels [MRK 4:39–4:41](https://ref.ly/Mark4:39-Mark4:41), [LUK 8:24–8:25](https://ref.ly/Luke8:24-Luke8:25) *See also* [MAT 12:8](https://ref.ly/Matt12:8) parallels [MRK 2:28](https://ref.ly/Mark2:28), [LUK 6:5](https://ref.ly/Luke6:5); [LUK 8:39](https://ref.ly/Luke8:39) parallel [MRK 5:19–5:20](https://ref.ly/Mark5:19-Mark5:20)

Jesus Christ's resurrection confirms his divinity
-------------------------------------------------

**[ACT 2:36](https://ref.ly/Acts2:36)** *See also* [ROM 1:4](https://ref.ly/Rom1:4); [PHP 2:9–2:11](https://ref.ly/Phil2:9-Phil2:11)

Jesus Christ's names and titles point to his divinity
-----------------------------------------------------

### Jesus Christ as judge

**[JHN 5:27](https://ref.ly/John5:27)** *In the OT, final responsibility for judgment is assigned to God.* *See also* [MAT 25:31–25:33](https://ref.ly/Matt25:31-Matt25:33); [MRK 8:38](https://ref.ly/Mark8:38) parallels [MAT 16:27](https://ref.ly/Matt16:27), [LUK 9:26](https://ref.ly/Luke9:26); [ACT 17:31](https://ref.ly/Acts17:31); [ROM 2:16](https://ref.ly/Rom2:16); [2CO 5:10](https://ref.ly/2Cor5:10)

### Jesus Christ as \`\`I am''

**[JHN 11:25](https://ref.ly/John11:25)** *“I am” is the meaning of God's name in the OT (see [Ex 3:14](https://ref.ly/Exod3:14)).* *See also* [JHN 6:35](https://ref.ly/John6:35), [JHN 8:12](https://ref.ly/John8:12), [JHN 10:7](https://ref.ly/John10:7), [JHN 10:11](https://ref.ly/John10:11), [JHN 14:6](https://ref.ly/John14:6), [JHN 15:1](https://ref.ly/John15:1), [JHN 18:5–18:6](https://ref.ly/John18:5-John18:6)

### Jesus Christ as Saviour

**[ACT 5:31](https://ref.ly/Acts5:31)** *According to the OT, God alone can save.* *See also* [ACT 4:12](https://ref.ly/Acts4:12); [EPH 5:23](https://ref.ly/Eph5:23); [HEB 7:25](https://ref.ly/Heb7:25)

### Jesus Christ as Lord

**[ROM 10:9](https://ref.ly/Rom10:9)** *“Lord” was equivalent to God's name in the OT.* *See also* [LUK 1:43](https://ref.ly/Luke1:43), [LUK 2:11](https://ref.ly/Luke2:11); [JHN 13:13](https://ref.ly/John13:13); [1CO 12:3](https://ref.ly/1Cor12:3); [2CO 4:5](https://ref.ly/2Cor4:5); [REV 19:16](https://ref.ly/Rev19:16)

### Jesus Christ as creator

**[COL 1:16](https://ref.ly/Col1:16)** *See also* [JHN 1:3](https://ref.ly/John1:3), [JHN 1:10](https://ref.ly/John1:10); [ACT 3:15](https://ref.ly/Acts3:15); [ROM 11:36](https://ref.ly/Rom11:36); [1CO 8:6](https://ref.ly/1Cor8:6); [HEB 1:2](https://ref.ly/Heb1:2), [HEB 1:10](https://ref.ly/Heb1:10); [PSA 102:25](https://ref.ly/Ps102:25)

### Jesus Christ as shepherd

**[HEB 13:20](https://ref.ly/Heb13:20)** *“Shepherd” was a well\-known OT name for God.* *See also* [JHN 10:11–10:16](https://ref.ly/John10:11-John10:16); [1PE 2:25](https://ref.ly/1Pet2:25), [1PE 5:4](https://ref.ly/1Pet5:4)

Those who recognised Jesus Christ's divinity
--------------------------------------------

### The disciples

**[JHN 20:28](https://ref.ly/John20:28)** *See also* [MAT 16:16](https://ref.ly/Matt16:16) parallels [MRK 8:29](https://ref.ly/Mark8:29), [LUK 9:20](https://ref.ly/Luke9:20)

### The demons

[MRK 3:11](https://ref.ly/Mark3:11); ; [LUK 4:41](https://ref.ly/Luke4:41) parallel [MRK 1:34](https://ref.ly/Mark1:34)

-------------------------------------------------------

## 2021: Jesus Christ, faithfulness of (id: 2021)

The total reliability and constancy of Jesus Christ is shown in his personal character, and made known by his words and works.

Jesus Christ's faithfulness is seen in his character
----------------------------------------------------

### He is faithful by nature

**[REV 19:11](https://ref.ly/Rev19:11)** *A description of the exalted Christ.* *See also* [REV 1:5](https://ref.ly/Rev1:5), [REV 3:14](https://ref.ly/Rev3:14)

### The promised Messiah is faithful

**[ISA 11:5](https://ref.ly/Isa11:5)** *See also* [ISA 42:3](https://ref.ly/Isa42:3)

### Jesus Christ is faithful because he never changes

**[HEB 13:8](https://ref.ly/Heb13:8)** *See also* [HEB 1:11–1:12](https://ref.ly/Heb1:11-Heb1:12); [PSA 102:26–102:27](https://ref.ly/Ps102:26-Ps102:27)

### Jesus Christ is faithful because he is the truth

**[JHN 1:14](https://ref.ly/John1:14)** *“grace” and “truth” are often associated in Hebrew with love and faithfulness.* *See also* [JHN 1:17](https://ref.ly/John1:17), [JHN 14:6](https://ref.ly/John14:6)

Jesus Christ's faithfulness demonstrated in his obedience
---------------------------------------------------------

### He is faithful to his Father

**[HEB 3:6](https://ref.ly/Heb3:6)** *See also* [LUK 2:49](https://ref.ly/Luke2:49); [JHN 5:30](https://ref.ly/John5:30), [JHN 6:38](https://ref.ly/John6:38), [JHN 8:29](https://ref.ly/John8:29), [JHN 14:31](https://ref.ly/John14:31); [HEB 3:2](https://ref.ly/Heb3:2)

### He kept faithfully to his work

**[LUK 4:43](https://ref.ly/Luke4:43)** parallel [MRK 1:38](https://ref.ly/Mark1:38) *See also* [JHN 4:34](https://ref.ly/John4:34), [JHN 9:4](https://ref.ly/John9:4), [JHN 12:27](https://ref.ly/John12:27), [JHN 17:4](https://ref.ly/John17:4), [JHN 19:30](https://ref.ly/John19:30); [HEB 2:17–2:18](https://ref.ly/Heb2:17-Heb2:18)

Jesus Christ's faithfulness is seen in his words
------------------------------------------------

### In his predictions about events

**[MAT 16:28](https://ref.ly/Matt16:28)** parallels [LUK 9:27](https://ref.ly/Luke9:27), [MRK 9:1](https://ref.ly/Mark9:1) *This prediction could refer to either Jesus Christ's transfiguration or his ascension*; **[MAT 24:2](https://ref.ly/Matt24:2)** parallels [MRK 13:2](https://ref.ly/Mark13:2), [LUK 21:6](https://ref.ly/Luke21:6) *This prediction was fulfilled in A.D. 70 when the Romans destroyed Jerusalem and the temple.* *See also* [MAT 21:2](https://ref.ly/Matt21:2) parallels [MRK 11:2](https://ref.ly/Mark11:2), [LUK 19:30](https://ref.ly/Luke19:30) *finding a donkey and her colt*; [MAT 26:21](https://ref.ly/Matt26:21) parallels [MRK 14:18](https://ref.ly/Mark14:18), [LUK 22:21](https://ref.ly/Luke22:21), [JHN 13:21](https://ref.ly/John13:21) *Jesus Christ's betrayer*; [MAT 26:34](https://ref.ly/Matt26:34) parallels [MRK 14:30](https://ref.ly/Mark14:30), [LUK 22:34](https://ref.ly/Luke22:34), [JHN 13:38](https://ref.ly/John13:38) *Peter's denial*; [JHN 16:20](https://ref.ly/John16:20), [JHN 21:18–21:19](https://ref.ly/John21:18-John21:19)

### In his promises about eternal life

**[JHN 5:24](https://ref.ly/John5:24)** *See also* [MAT 19:28–19:29](https://ref.ly/Matt19:28-Matt19:29) parallels [MRK 10:29–10:30](https://ref.ly/Mark10:29-Mark10:30), [LUK 18:29–18:30](https://ref.ly/Luke18:29-Luke18:30); [LUK 23:43](https://ref.ly/Luke23:43); [JHN 6:47](https://ref.ly/John6:47), [JHN 6:53–6:54](https://ref.ly/John6:53-John6:54), [JHN 8:51](https://ref.ly/John8:51)

### In his promise of authority for believers

**[MAT 17:20](https://ref.ly/Matt17:20)** *See also* [MAT 16:19](https://ref.ly/Matt16:19), [MAT 18:18](https://ref.ly/Matt18:18), [MAT 21:21](https://ref.ly/Matt21:21) parallel [MRK 11:23](https://ref.ly/Mark11:23); [MAT 28:18–28:19](https://ref.ly/Matt28:18-Matt28:19); [LUK 10:19](https://ref.ly/Luke10:19)

### In his promise about the Holy Spirit

## 2024: Jesus Christ, glory of (id: 2024)

Jesus Christ's radiance and splendour reflects the glory of the Father, and is both revealed to and reflected in the lives of believers.

Jesus Christ's glory existed before the incarnation
---------------------------------------------------

**[JHN 17:5](https://ref.ly/John17:5)** *See also* [JHN 1:14](https://ref.ly/John1:14), [JHN 17:24](https://ref.ly/John17:24)

Jesus Christ's glory is God's glory
-----------------------------------

### God's glory is reflected in Jesus Christ

**[HEB 1:3](https://ref.ly/Heb1:3)** *See also* [JHN 12:41](https://ref.ly/John12:41) *John makes no distinction between God's glory revealed in [Isa 6:3](https://ref.ly/Isa6:3) and the glory of Jesus Christ*; [JHN 13:32](https://ref.ly/John13:32); [2CO 4:4](https://ref.ly/2Cor4:4), [2CO 4:6](https://ref.ly/2Cor4:6)

### Jesus Christ brings glory to his Father

**[JHN 14:13](https://ref.ly/John14:13)** *See also* [JHN 13:31](https://ref.ly/John13:31), [JHN 17:1](https://ref.ly/John17:1), [JHN 17:4](https://ref.ly/John17:4); [ROM 16:27](https://ref.ly/Rom16:27); [EPH 1:12](https://ref.ly/Eph1:12); [JUD 1:25](https://ref.ly/Jude1:25)

### The Holy Spirit glorifies Jesus Christ

**[JHN 16:14](https://ref.ly/John16:14)**

Jesus Christ's glory is revealed on earth
-----------------------------------------

### Through his miracles

## 2027: Jesus Christ, grace and mercy of (id: 2027)

The qualities of Jesus Christ by which he is compassionate, accepting and generous. In his ministry, Christ demonstrates these qualities towards those whom he encounters. Believers should model themselves upon Jesus Christ in this respect.

The grace and mercy of God made known in Jesus Christ
-----------------------------------------------------

**[JHN 1:14](https://ref.ly/John1:14), [JHN 1:16–1:17](https://ref.ly/John1:16-John1:17)** *See also* [LUK 2:40](https://ref.ly/Luke2:40), [LUK 2:52](https://ref.ly/Luke2:52); [2CO 8:9](https://ref.ly/2Cor8:9); [TIT 2:11](https://ref.ly/Titus2:11) *Jesus Christ shows the grace of God in his life.*

Grace and mercy in the ministry of Jesus Christ
-----------------------------------------------

### Jesus Christ responds to pleas for mercy

**[MAT 9:27–9:30](https://ref.ly/Matt9:27-Matt9:30)** *See also* [MAT 15:22](https://ref.ly/Matt15:22), [MAT 20:29–20:34](https://ref.ly/Matt20:29-Matt20:34) parallels [MRK 10:46–10:52](https://ref.ly/Mark10:46-Mark10:52), [LUK 18:35–18:42](https://ref.ly/Luke18:35-Luke18:42)

### His teaching reflects his grace and mercy

**[LUK 6:35–6:36](https://ref.ly/Luke6:35-Luke6:36)** *See also* [HOS 6:6](https://ref.ly/Hos6:6); [MAT 6:12–6:15](https://ref.ly/Matt6:12-Matt6:15) parallel [LUK 11:4](https://ref.ly/Luke11:4); [MAT 9:10–9:13](https://ref.ly/Matt9:10-Matt9:13) parallels [MRK 2:15–2:17](https://ref.ly/Mark2:15-Mark2:17), [LUK 5:29–5:32](https://ref.ly/Luke5:29-Luke5:32); [MAT 18:21–18:35](https://ref.ly/Matt18:21-Matt18:35) *the parable of the unmerciful servant*; [LUK 10:30–10:37](https://ref.ly/Luke10:30-Luke10:37) *the parable of the good Samaritan*; [EPH 4:32](https://ref.ly/Eph4:32)

----------------------------------------

### The grace of Jesus Christ

**[ACT 15:11](https://ref.ly/Acts15:11)** *See also* [ROM 3:24](https://ref.ly/Rom3:24), [ROM 5:15](https://ref.ly/Rom5:15); [EPH 2:4–2:5](https://ref.ly/Eph2:4-Eph2:5), [EPH 2:8](https://ref.ly/Eph2:8); [2TI 1:9](https://ref.ly/2Tim1:9)

## 2030: Jesus Christ, holiness of (id: 2030)

The holiness of Jesus Christ is seen in his divine nature and work, as he stands apart from and above the created world with divine power, authority and purity. Recognition of the holiness of Jesus Christ leads both to a realisation of sin and unworthiness and to worship and adoration.

The holy character of Jesus Christ
----------------------------------

### Its divine origin

**[LUK 1:35](https://ref.ly/Luke1:35)** *See also* [JHN 1:1–1:2](https://ref.ly/John1:1-John1:2), [JHN 3:31](https://ref.ly/John3:31), [JHN 8:23](https://ref.ly/John8:23), [JHN 13:3](https://ref.ly/John13:3), [JHN 17:14](https://ref.ly/John17:14), [JHN 17:16](https://ref.ly/John17:16)

### Its divine nature

**[COL 2:9](https://ref.ly/Col2:9)** *See also* [JHN 1:14](https://ref.ly/John1:14), [JHN 10:30](https://ref.ly/John10:30), [JHN 10:38](https://ref.ly/John10:38), [JHN 14:10](https://ref.ly/John14:10); [PHP 2:6](https://ref.ly/Phil2:6); [HEB 1:3](https://ref.ly/Heb1:3)

### Its divine purity

**[HEB 7:26](https://ref.ly/Heb7:26)** *See also* [2CO 5:21](https://ref.ly/2Cor5:21); [HEB 4:15](https://ref.ly/Heb4:15); [1PE 1:19](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:19), [1PE 2:22](https://ref.ly/1Pet2:22); [1JN 3:3](https://ref.ly/1John3:3), [1JN 3:5](https://ref.ly/1John3:5)

### Its divine power

**[ACT 4:30](https://ref.ly/Acts4:30)** *See also* [ACT 10:38](https://ref.ly/Acts10:38)

The holy work of Jesus Christ
-----------------------------

### He is set apart as God's servant

**[ACT 4:27](https://ref.ly/Acts4:27)** *See also* [MRK 10:45](https://ref.ly/Mark10:45) parallel [MAT 20:28](https://ref.ly/Matt20:28); [JHN 14:31](https://ref.ly/John14:31); [ACT 3:26](https://ref.ly/Acts3:26); [PHP 2:7–2:8](https://ref.ly/Phil2:7-Phil2:8); [HEB 10:7](https://ref.ly/Heb10:7)

### His life is consecrated to the will and purpose of God

**[MAT 26:39](https://ref.ly/Matt26:39)** parallels [MRK 14:35–14:36](https://ref.ly/Mark14:35-Mark14:36), [LUK 22:42](https://ref.ly/Luke22:42) *See also* [MAT 26:42](https://ref.ly/Matt26:42); [JHN 12:49–12:50](https://ref.ly/John12:49-John12:50), [JHN 14:31](https://ref.ly/John14:31)

### He is appointed as the judge of sinners

[JHN 5:22](https://ref.ly/John5:22), [JHN 5:26–5:27](https://ref.ly/John5:26-John5:27); ; [ACT 17:31](https://ref.ly/Acts17:31); ; [2CO 5:10](https://ref.ly/2Cor5:10)

### He makes God's people holy

**[HEB 13:12](https://ref.ly/Heb13:12)** *See also* [JHN 17:19](https://ref.ly/John17:19); [EPH 5:25–5:27](https://ref.ly/Eph5:25-Eph5:27); [HEB 2:11](https://ref.ly/Heb2:11), [HEB 10:10](https://ref.ly/Heb10:10), [HEB 10:14](https://ref.ly/Heb10:14); [1PE 2:4–2:5](https://ref.ly/1Pet2:4-1Pet2:5), [1PE 2:9–2:10](https://ref.ly/1Pet2:9-1Pet2:10)

--------------------------------------------

## 2033: Jesus Christ, humanity of (id: 2033)

Scripture stresses the total humanity of Jesus Christ. Although sinless, Christ shared in the general condition of humanity, including suffering and death.

Jesus Christ was a man
----------------------

### By his own claims

**[JHN 8:40](https://ref.ly/John8:40)** *See also* [MAT 8:20](https://ref.ly/Matt8:20) parallel [LUK 9:58](https://ref.ly/Luke9:58)

### In statements made by others

**[JHN 19:5](https://ref.ly/John19:5)** *See also* [MAT 8:27](https://ref.ly/Matt8:27); [MRK 15:39](https://ref.ly/Mark15:39) parallel [LUK 23:47](https://ref.ly/Luke23:47) *the centurion*; [LUK 15:2](https://ref.ly/Luke15:2) *the Pharisees and teachers of the law*; [LUK 23:18](https://ref.ly/Luke23:18); [JHN 1:33](https://ref.ly/John1:33), [JHN 4:42](https://ref.ly/John4:42), [JHN 7:12](https://ref.ly/John7:12), [JHN 7:15](https://ref.ly/John7:15) *some Jews*; [JHN 7:27](https://ref.ly/John7:27), [JHN 9:33](https://ref.ly/John9:33), [JHN 11:47](https://ref.ly/John11:47); [ACT 2:22–2:23](https://ref.ly/Acts2:22-Acts2:23)

Jesus Christ shared in the general condition of humanity
--------------------------------------------------------

### He assumed human nature

**[JHN 1:14](https://ref.ly/John1:14)** *“flesh” here speaks not only of a material body but also of human nature.* *See also* [PHP 2:7–2:8](https://ref.ly/Phil2:7-Phil2:8); [HEB 2:14](https://ref.ly/Heb2:14); [1JN 4:2](https://ref.ly/1John4:2)

### He had a soul

**[MAT 26:38](https://ref.ly/Matt26:38)** parallel [MRK 14:34](https://ref.ly/Mark14:34) *See also* [ISA 53:11](https://ref.ly/Isa53:11)

**[MAT 27:50](https://ref.ly/Matt27:50)** parallels [MRK 15:37](https://ref.ly/Mark15:37), [LUK 23:46](https://ref.ly/Luke23:46), [JHN 19:30](https://ref.ly/John19:30) *Jesus Christ most closely identified with the rest of humanity through his death. However Jesus Christ is distinct from human beings in that his death was an act of free will and not the inevitable consequence of sin (see [Jn 10:17–18](https://ref.ly/John10:17-John10:18)).* *See also* [HEB 2:9](https://ref.ly/Heb2:9), [HEB 2:14](https://ref.ly/Heb2:14)

--------------------------------------

## 2036: Jesus Christ, humility of (id: 2036)

The obedient submission of Jesus Christ to his Father, seen in his willingness to become a human being for humanity's sake, his freedom from self\-interest and his willingness to serve others.

Jesus Christ's willingness to become a human being
--------------------------------------------------

**[PHP 2:6–2:7](https://ref.ly/Phil2:6-Phil2:7)** *“human likeness” is not mere similarity to but identity with humanity.* *See also* [ROM 8:3](https://ref.ly/Rom8:3); [2CO 8:9](https://ref.ly/2Cor8:9)

Jesus Christ's humility predicted in the OT
-------------------------------------------

[MAT 12:19–12:20](https://ref.ly/Matt12:19-Matt12:20); ; [ISA 42:2–42:3](https://ref.ly/Isa42:2-Isa42:3), [ISA 50:4–50:6](https://ref.ly/Isa50:4-Isa50:6); [MAT 8:17](https://ref.ly/Matt8:17); ; [ACT 8:32–8:33](https://ref.ly/Acts8:32-Acts8:33); ; [ISA 53:2–53:7](https://ref.ly/Isa53:2-Isa53:7); ; [1PE 2:22](https://ref.ly/1Pet2:22); ; [ISA 53:9](https://ref.ly/Isa53:9); ; [1PE 2:24](https://ref.ly/1Pet2:24); [MAT 21:5](https://ref.ly/Matt21:5) parallel [JHN 12:15](https://ref.ly/John12:15); ; [ZEC 9:9](https://ref.ly/Zech9:9); [ZEC 12:10](https://ref.ly/Zech12:10); [MAT 26:31](https://ref.ly/Matt26:31) parallel [MRK 14:27](https://ref.ly/Mark14:27); ; [ZEC 13:7](https://ref.ly/Zech13:7)

## 2039: Jesus Christ, joy of (id: 2039)

Jesus Christ brings joy to his people, who are able to rejoice at the coming of their Saviour and Lord, and all the benefits which he brings to them.

Jesus Christ's joy originates in God
------------------------------------

### From his intimate relationship with his Father and the Spirit

**[LUK 10:21](https://ref.ly/Luke10:21)** parallel [MAT 11:25–11:26](https://ref.ly/Matt11:25-Matt11:26) *See also* [ISA 11:2–11:3](https://ref.ly/Isa11:2-Isa11:3); [MAT 3:16–3:17](https://ref.ly/Matt3:16-Matt3:17) parallels [MRK 1:10–1:11](https://ref.ly/Mark1:10-Mark1:11), [LUK 3:22](https://ref.ly/Luke3:22); [MAT 12:18](https://ref.ly/Matt12:18); [ISA 42:1](https://ref.ly/Isa42:1); [ACT 2:28](https://ref.ly/Acts2:28); [PSA 16:11](https://ref.ly/Ps16:11)

### From his awareness of God's purposes

**[HEB 12:2](https://ref.ly/Heb12:2)** *See also* [JHN 8:29](https://ref.ly/John8:29)

Jesus Christ's coming brings great joy
--------------------------------------

### His birth

## 2042: Jesus Christ, justice of (id: 2042)

The teaching and lifestyle of Jesus Christ show him to be just and impartial in his judgments and dealings with people. At the end of the age, God has appointed Jesus Christ to judge and rule with justice.

Justice was a quality displayed in Jesus Christ's life
------------------------------------------------------

**[MAT 12:18–12:21](https://ref.ly/Matt12:18-Matt12:21)** *See also* [ISA 42:1–42:4](https://ref.ly/Isa42:1-Isa42:4)

Jesus Christ was just and impartial in his dealings with people
---------------------------------------------------------------

[JHN 4:9](https://ref.ly/John4:9) *with Samaritans*; ; [JHN 4:27](https://ref.ly/John4:27) *with women*; ; [MAT 9:10–9:12](https://ref.ly/Matt9:10-Matt9:12) parallels [MRK 2:15–2:17](https://ref.ly/Mark2:15-Mark2:17), [LUK 5:29–5:31](https://ref.ly/Luke5:29-Luke5:31) *with tax collectors and those classed as “sinners”*; ; [MAT 15:21–15:28](https://ref.ly/Matt15:21-Matt15:28) parallel [MRK 7:24–7:29](https://ref.ly/Mark7:24-Mark7:29) *with the Gentiles*

Justice in the teaching of Jesus Christ
---------------------------------------

**[MAT 23:23](https://ref.ly/Matt23:23)** parallel [LUK 11:42](https://ref.ly/Luke11:42) *See also* [MAT 5:17–5:48](https://ref.ly/Matt5:17-Matt5:48), [MAT 7:1–7:5](https://ref.ly/Matt7:1-Matt7:5) parallel [LUK 6:37–6:42](https://ref.ly/Luke6:37-Luke6:42); [LUK 12:58–12:59](https://ref.ly/Luke12:58-Luke12:59), [LUK 14:13–14:14](https://ref.ly/Luke14:13-Luke14:14); [JHN 7:24](https://ref.ly/John7:24), [JHN 8:7](https://ref.ly/John8:7)

----------------------------

------------------------------------------------

## 2045: Jesus Christ, knowledge of (id: 2045)

Jesus Christ has perfect insight into God's purposes and into human nature by reason of his intimate relationship with the Father, but he has accepted limited knowledge as a consequence of his humanity.

Jesus Christ's knowledge of his Father
--------------------------------------

**[MAT 11:27](https://ref.ly/Matt11:27)** parallel [LUK 10:22](https://ref.ly/Luke10:22) *See also* [JHN 7:29](https://ref.ly/John7:29), [JHN 8:26](https://ref.ly/John8:26), [JHN 8:55](https://ref.ly/John8:55), [JHN 10:15](https://ref.ly/John10:15), [JHN 11:41–11:42](https://ref.ly/John11:41-John11:42), [JHN 15:15](https://ref.ly/John15:15), [JHN 17:25](https://ref.ly/John17:25)

Jesus Christ's complete knowledge
---------------------------------

**[JHN 16:30](https://ref.ly/John16:30)** *See also* [JHN 21:17](https://ref.ly/John21:17)

--------------------------------------

## 2048: Jesus Christ, love of (id: 2048)

Jesus Christ's total giving of himself, shown supremely in his obedient suffering and death on the cross, reveals God's amazing love for sinners. It continues to motivate and inspire Christians today.

The supreme quality of Jesus Christ's love
------------------------------------------

**[EPH 3:17–3:19](https://ref.ly/Eph3:17-Eph3:19)** *See also* [ROM 8:35](https://ref.ly/Rom8:35), [ROM 8:38–8:39](https://ref.ly/Rom8:38-Rom8:39)

### He loves sinners

## 2051: Jesus Christ, majesty of (id: 2051)

The glorious splendour of Jesus Christ's royal authority belongs to him by right and is reaffirmed through his exaltation to the Father's right hand.

Jesus Christ shared in God's majesty before time began
------------------------------------------------------

**[JHN 17:5](https://ref.ly/John17:5)** *See also* [JHN 17:24](https://ref.ly/John17:24); [COL 1:15](https://ref.ly/Col1:15); [HEB 1:3](https://ref.ly/Heb1:3); [REV 22:13](https://ref.ly/Rev22:13)

Jesus Christ renounced his majesty to become a human being
----------------------------------------------------------

**[PHP 2:6–2:8](https://ref.ly/Phil2:6-Phil2:8)** *See also* [ISA 53:2–53:3](https://ref.ly/Isa53:2-Isa53:3); [MAT 20:28](https://ref.ly/Matt20:28) parallel [MRK 10:45](https://ref.ly/Mark10:45); [JHN 13:3–13:5](https://ref.ly/John13:3-John13:5); [2CO 8:9](https://ref.ly/2Cor8:9)

---------------------------------------------------

### At the transfiguration

**[2PE 1:16](https://ref.ly/2Pet1:16)** *See also* [MAT 17:2](https://ref.ly/Matt17:2) parallels [MRK 9:2–9:3](https://ref.ly/Mark9:2-Mark9:3), [LUK 9:29](https://ref.ly/Luke9:29)

### At the entry into Jerusalem

**[MAT 21:9–21:10](https://ref.ly/Matt21:9-Matt21:10)** parallels [MRK 11:9–11:10](https://ref.ly/Mark11:9-Mark11:10), [LUK 19:37–19:38](https://ref.ly/Luke19:37-Luke19:38), [JHN 12:13](https://ref.ly/John12:13) *See also* [MAT 21:5](https://ref.ly/Matt21:5) parallel [JHN 12:15](https://ref.ly/John12:15); [ZEC 9:9](https://ref.ly/Zech9:9)

-----------------------------------------------------------

### Jesus Christ is exalted to the throne of God's majesty

### Jesus Christ's is majestic in his absolute pre\-eminence

### Jesus Christ's majesty is shown by his authority as judge of all

**[MAT 25:31](https://ref.ly/Matt25:31)** *See also* [ACT 17:31](https://ref.ly/Acts17:31); [2TI 4:1](https://ref.ly/2Tim4:1)

All humanity will see Jesus Christ's majesty
--------------------------------------------

## 2054: Jesus Christ, mind of (id: 2054)

The centre of Jesus Christ's thought, understanding and motivation, characterised by a total dedication to God. Christians are called upon to have the same mind as Christ.

The intellectual capacity of Jesus Christ's mind
------------------------------------------------

### In childhood

**[LUK 2:47](https://ref.ly/Luke2:47)** *See also* [LUK 2:40](https://ref.ly/Luke2:40), [LUK 2:52](https://ref.ly/Luke2:52)

### In adulthood

**[JHN 7:15](https://ref.ly/John7:15)** *See also* [MAT 7:28](https://ref.ly/Matt7:28), [MAT 13:54](https://ref.ly/Matt13:54) parallel [MRK 6:2](https://ref.ly/Mark6:2); [MRK 1:22](https://ref.ly/Mark1:22) parallel [LUK 4:32](https://ref.ly/Luke4:32); [MRK 11:18](https://ref.ly/Mark11:18)

Jesus Christ's mind was pure
----------------------------

**[HEB 7:26](https://ref.ly/Heb7:26)** *The purity of Jesus Christ's mind is declared by his words and actions and by his oneness with God.* *See also* [LUK 1:35](https://ref.ly/Luke1:35); [JHN 10:30](https://ref.ly/John10:30); [HEB 4:15](https://ref.ly/Heb4:15)

Examples of Jesus Christ's use of his mind
------------------------------------------

### In overcoming temptation

[MAT 4:4](https://ref.ly/Matt4:4) parallel [LUK 4:4](https://ref.ly/Luke4:4); ; [DEU 8:3](https://ref.ly/Deut8:3); ; [MAT 27:42](https://ref.ly/Matt27:42) parallels [MRK 15:32](https://ref.ly/Mark15:32), [LUK 23:37](https://ref.ly/Luke23:37)

### Against opposition

[MAT 22:18–22:22](https://ref.ly/Matt22:18-Matt22:22) parallels [MRK 12:15–12:17](https://ref.ly/Mark12:15-Mark12:17), [LUK 20:22–20:26](https://ref.ly/Luke20:22-Luke20:26)

Jesus Christ's mind is more than intellect
------------------------------------------

### His thinking is supported by prayer

**[LUK 6:12–6:13](https://ref.ly/Luke6:12-Luke6:13)** *See also* [LUK 5:16](https://ref.ly/Luke5:16), [LUK 22:41–22:43](https://ref.ly/Luke22:41-Luke22:43) parallels [MAT 26:39](https://ref.ly/Matt26:39), [MRK 14:35–14:36](https://ref.ly/Mark14:35-Mark14:36)

Jesus Christ's mind is extraordinary
------------------------------------

## 2057: Jesus Christ, obedience of (id: 2057)

The selfless obedience of Jesus Christ to the will of God his Father, through which the redemption of humanity is accomplished. Christ also shows himself willing to submit to earthly authorities and sets an example which believers are called to imitate.

Jesus Christ was totally obedient to his Father's will
------------------------------------------------------

### Obedience was central to Jesus Christ's life and thought

**[JHN 4:34](https://ref.ly/John4:34)**; **[HEB 10:9](https://ref.ly/Heb10:9)** *See also* [MAT 3:15](https://ref.ly/Matt3:15), [MAT 8:9–8:10](https://ref.ly/Matt8:9-Matt8:10) parallel [LUK 7:8–7:9](https://ref.ly/Luke7:8-Luke7:9); [JHN 5:30](https://ref.ly/John5:30), [JHN 6:38](https://ref.ly/John6:38), [JHN 14:31](https://ref.ly/John14:31); [HEB 10:7](https://ref.ly/Heb10:7); [PSA 40:7–40:8](https://ref.ly/Ps40:7-Ps40:8)

### Jesus Christ's obedience meant ultimate personal cost

**[MAT 26:39](https://ref.ly/Matt26:39)** parallels [MRK 14:36](https://ref.ly/Mark14:36), [LUK 22:42](https://ref.ly/Luke22:42)**[PHP 2:8](https://ref.ly/Phil2:8)** *See also* [ISA 50:5–50:6](https://ref.ly/Isa50:5-Isa50:6), [ISA 53:10–53:12](https://ref.ly/Isa53:10-Isa53:12); [MAT 16:21](https://ref.ly/Matt16:21) parallels [MRK 8:31](https://ref.ly/Mark8:31), [LUK 9:22](https://ref.ly/Luke9:22); [JHN 10:18](https://ref.ly/John10:18), [JHN 13:1](https://ref.ly/John13:1); [HEB 5:8](https://ref.ly/Heb5:8)

### Jesus Christ's obedience was necessary for God's salvation plan

**[ROM 5:18–5:19](https://ref.ly/Rom5:18-Rom5:19)** *See also* [MAT 27:40–27:42](https://ref.ly/Matt27:40-Matt27:42) parallels [MRK 15:30–15:31](https://ref.ly/Mark15:30-Mark15:31), [LUK 23:35–23:37](https://ref.ly/Luke23:35-Luke23:37); [LUK 24:26](https://ref.ly/Luke24:26); [JHN 17:2–17:4](https://ref.ly/John17:2-John17:4), [JHN 17:26](https://ref.ly/John17:26), [JHN 19:30](https://ref.ly/John19:30)

Jesus Christ's obedience was shown in his human relationships
-------------------------------------------------------------

### He was obedient to his parents

**[LUK 2:51](https://ref.ly/Luke2:51)**

### He was obedient to secular authorities

*See also* [MAT 17:24–17:27](https://ref.ly/Matt17:24-Matt17:27), [MAT 22:17–22:21](https://ref.ly/Matt22:17-Matt22:21) parallels [MRK 12:15–12:17](https://ref.ly/Mark12:15-Mark12:17), [LUK 20:22–20:25](https://ref.ly/Luke20:22-Luke20:25)

### He was obedient to the Jewish law

[MAT 5:17–5:18](https://ref.ly/Matt5:17-Matt5:18), [MAT 22:37–22:40](https://ref.ly/Matt22:37-Matt22:40) parallels [MRK 12:29–12:31](https://ref.ly/Mark12:29-Mark12:31), [LUK 10:26–10:28](https://ref.ly/Luke10:26-Luke10:28); ; [MRK 2:23–2:28](https://ref.ly/Mark2:23-Mark2:28); ; [JHN 7:19](https://ref.ly/John7:19), [JHN 10:37–10:38](https://ref.ly/John10:37-John10:38) *Jesus Christ's obedience and commitment were to the spirit of God's law; his attitudes to Jewish legalism were often seen as disobedience. Disputes over the Sabbath are one example.*

Believers should follow Jesus Christ's example of obedience
-----------------------------------------------------------

### Obedience to God's will is paramount

**[MAT 19:17](https://ref.ly/Matt19:17)** *See also* [MAT 7:21](https://ref.ly/Matt7:21), [MAT 12:50](https://ref.ly/Matt12:50) parallels [MRK 3:35](https://ref.ly/Mark3:35), [LUK 8:21](https://ref.ly/Luke8:21); [JHN 15:10](https://ref.ly/John15:10); [EPH 6:6](https://ref.ly/Eph6:6)

### Christlike obedience expresses love for God

**[2JN 1:6](https://ref.ly/2John1:6)** *See also* [JHN 14:15](https://ref.ly/John14:15), [JHN 14:20–14:21](https://ref.ly/John14:20-John14:21), [JHN 15:12](https://ref.ly/John15:12)

### Obedience should characterise believers' lives

**[ROM 1:5](https://ref.ly/Rom1:5)** *“obedience” refers to a whole lifestyle arising from a relationship with God through Jesus Christ.* *See also* [ACT 5:29](https://ref.ly/Acts5:29); [2CO 2:9](https://ref.ly/2Cor2:9)

## 2060: Jesus Christ, patience of (id: 2060)

Jesus Christ supremely displays God's patient character in his work of salvation. The patience of Jesus Christ is seen in his relationships with people and in his perseverance through trial and suffering to death. Followers of Christ are called to demonstrate patience in all their relationships and circumstances.

The patience of Jesus Christ in his earthly ministry
----------------------------------------------------

### His patience with people

**[LUK 22:32–22:34](https://ref.ly/Luke22:32-Luke22:34)** *See also* [MAT 20:20–20:28](https://ref.ly/Matt20:20-Matt20:28) parallel [MRK 10:35–10:45](https://ref.ly/Mark10:35-Mark10:45); [MAT 26:69–26:75](https://ref.ly/Matt26:69-Matt26:75) parallels [MRK 14:66–14:72](https://ref.ly/Mark14:66-Mark14:72), [LUK 22:55–22:62](https://ref.ly/Luke22:55-Luke22:62), [JHN 18:16–18:27](https://ref.ly/John18:16-John18:27); [MRK 4:13–4:20](https://ref.ly/Mark4:13-Mark4:20); [LUK 23:33–23:34](https://ref.ly/Luke23:33-Luke23:34); [JHN 21:15–21:19](https://ref.ly/John21:15-John21:19)

### His patience with God's timing of events

**[JHN 12:27](https://ref.ly/John12:27)** *Jesus Christ's life was lived under the shadow of the cross. He was concerned that people should understand his ministry and therefore he exercised great patience, being directed by the Father in the priorities and timing of his ministry.* *See also* [MRK 1:34](https://ref.ly/Mark1:34) parallel [LUK 4:41](https://ref.ly/Luke4:41); [MRK 7:36](https://ref.ly/Mark7:36), [MRK 8:30](https://ref.ly/Mark8:30), [MRK 9:9](https://ref.ly/Mark9:9); [JHN 2:4](https://ref.ly/John2:4), [JHN 7:6](https://ref.ly/John7:6), [JHN 7:30](https://ref.ly/John7:30), [JHN 12:23](https://ref.ly/John12:23), [JHN 13:1](https://ref.ly/John13:1), [JHN 16:32](https://ref.ly/John16:32), [JHN 17:1](https://ref.ly/John17:1)

### His patience in suffering

**[MAT 26:39–26:42](https://ref.ly/Matt26:39-Matt26:42)** parallels [MRK 14:35–14:36](https://ref.ly/Mark14:35-Mark14:36), [LUK 22:42](https://ref.ly/Luke22:42) *See also* [MAT 26:59–26:68](https://ref.ly/Matt26:59-Matt26:68), [MAT 27:28–27:50](https://ref.ly/Matt27:28-Matt27:50); [2TH 3:5](https://ref.ly/2Thess3:5); [HEB 5:7–5:9](https://ref.ly/Heb5:7-Heb5:9), [HEB 12:2–12:3](https://ref.ly/Heb12:2-Heb12:3); [1PE 2:21–2:25](https://ref.ly/1Pet2:21-1Pet2:25)

-------------------------------------------------

**[1TI 1:16](https://ref.ly/1Tim1:16)** *See also* [ROM 2:4](https://ref.ly/Rom2:4); [2PE 3:15](https://ref.ly/2Pet3:15)

## 2063: Jesus Christ, perfection of (id: 2063)

Jesus Christ perfectly radiates the glory of God, exactly representing his Father's likeness. Christ's work is complete and he is free from all impurity.

Jesus Christ represents perfection and absoluteness
---------------------------------------------------

### His perfection was established through obedient suffering

**[HEB 5:8–5:9](https://ref.ly/Heb5:8-Heb5:9)** *See also* [HEB 2:10](https://ref.ly/Heb2:10), [HEB 7:28](https://ref.ly/Heb7:28)

### All things find fulfilment in Christ

**[EPH 1:22–1:23](https://ref.ly/Eph1:22-Eph1:23)** *See also* [EPH 1:9–1:10](https://ref.ly/Eph1:9-Eph1:10), [EPH 4:13](https://ref.ly/Eph4:13), [EPH 4:15–4:16](https://ref.ly/Eph4:15-Eph4:16); [COL 1:17–1:18](https://ref.ly/Col1:17-Col1:18)

Jesus Christ radiates God's glory
---------------------------------

**[HEB 1:3](https://ref.ly/Heb1:3)** *See also* [MAT 17:2](https://ref.ly/Matt17:2) parallels [MRK 9:3](https://ref.ly/Mark9:3), [LUK 9:29](https://ref.ly/Luke9:29) *At the transfiguration Jesus Christ's face mirrors God's glory and purity*; [JHN 1:14](https://ref.ly/John1:14); [2CO 4:4](https://ref.ly/2Cor4:4), [2CO 4:6](https://ref.ly/2Cor4:6); [2PE 1:17](https://ref.ly/2Pet1:17); [REV 1:14–1:16](https://ref.ly/Rev1:14-Rev1:16)

Jesus Christ exactly represents the Father's likeness
-----------------------------------------------------

**[HEB 1:3](https://ref.ly/Heb1:3)** *See also* [JHN 1:18](https://ref.ly/John1:18), [JHN 12:44–12:45](https://ref.ly/John12:44-John12:45), [JHN 14:7](https://ref.ly/John14:7), [JHN 14:9–14:10](https://ref.ly/John14:9-John14:10); [PHP 2:6](https://ref.ly/Phil2:6); [COL 1:15](https://ref.ly/Col1:15)

### The fulness of God dwells in Jesus Christ

**[COL 1:19](https://ref.ly/Col1:19)** *See also* [COL 2:9](https://ref.ly/Col2:9)

Jesus Christ's work is totally complete
---------------------------------------

**[HEB 12:2](https://ref.ly/Heb12:2)** *See also* [HEB 7:25](https://ref.ly/Heb7:25)

### Christians will finally participate in Christ's perfection

**[2CO 3:18](https://ref.ly/2Cor3:18)** *See also* [1CO 13:9–13:12](https://ref.ly/1Cor13:9-1Cor13:12)

Jesus Christ is without impurity
--------------------------------

**[1JN 3:5](https://ref.ly/1John3:5)** *See also* [JHN 8:46](https://ref.ly/John8:46); [2CO 5:21](https://ref.ly/2Cor5:21); [HEB 4:15](https://ref.ly/Heb4:15), [HEB 7:26](https://ref.ly/Heb7:26); [1PE 1:19](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:19), [1PE 2:22](https://ref.ly/1Pet2:22); [ISA 53:9](https://ref.ly/Isa53:9); [1JN 3:3](https://ref.ly/1John3:3), [1JN 3:7](https://ref.ly/1John3:7)

## 2066: Jesus Christ, power of (id: 2066)

The historical and ongoing effective authority of Jesus Christ over natural elements, over human life and ultimately over sin, forces of evil, Satan and death.

Jesus Christ's power is from God
--------------------------------

**[ACT 10:38](https://ref.ly/Acts10:38)**

### God's creative power is exercised through Jesus Christ

**[JHN 1:3](https://ref.ly/John1:3)** *See also* [1CO 8:6](https://ref.ly/1Cor8:6); [COL 1:16](https://ref.ly/Col1:16); [HEB 1:2](https://ref.ly/Heb1:2)

### God's infinite power is given to Jesus Christ

**[MAT 28:18](https://ref.ly/Matt28:18)** *See also* [MAT 9:6](https://ref.ly/Matt9:6) parallels [MRK 2:10](https://ref.ly/Mark2:10), [LUK 5:24](https://ref.ly/Luke5:24); [MAT 19:26](https://ref.ly/Matt19:26) parallel [LUK 1:37](https://ref.ly/Luke1:37); [LUK 1:35](https://ref.ly/Luke1:35); [JHN 3:34–3:35](https://ref.ly/John3:34-John3:35), [JHN 5:19–5:20](https://ref.ly/John5:19-John5:20), [JHN 13:3](https://ref.ly/John13:3); [PHP 2:9](https://ref.ly/Phil2:9)

Jesus Christ's power is revealed on earth
-----------------------------------------

### Jesus Christ's power over nature

**[MAT 8:26–8:27](https://ref.ly/Matt8:26-Matt8:27)** parallels [MRK 4:39–4:41](https://ref.ly/Mark4:39-Mark4:41), [LUK 8:24–8:25](https://ref.ly/Luke8:24-Luke8:25) *See also* [MAT 14:25](https://ref.ly/Matt14:25) parallels [MRK 6:48](https://ref.ly/Mark6:48), [JHN 6:19](https://ref.ly/John6:19); [MAT 21:19](https://ref.ly/Matt21:19) parallel [MRK 11:14](https://ref.ly/Mark11:14); [MRK 11:21](https://ref.ly/Mark11:21)

### Jesus Christ's power over sickness

**[MAT 4:23](https://ref.ly/Matt4:23)** *See also* [MAT 8:2–8:3](https://ref.ly/Matt8:2-Matt8:3) parallels [MRK 1:40–1:42](https://ref.ly/Mark1:40-Mark1:42), [LUK 5:12–5:13](https://ref.ly/Luke5:12-Luke5:13); [MRK 5:27–5:30](https://ref.ly/Mark5:27-Mark5:30) parallels [MAT 9:21–9:22](https://ref.ly/Matt9:21-Matt9:22), [LUK 8:44–8:46](https://ref.ly/Luke8:44-Luke8:46); [LUK 5:17](https://ref.ly/Luke5:17); [ACT 10:38](https://ref.ly/Acts10:38)

### Jesus Christ's power over human life

**[MAT 11:5](https://ref.ly/Matt11:5)** parallel [LUK 7:22](https://ref.ly/Luke7:22) *See also* [MAT 9:18–9:25](https://ref.ly/Matt9:18-Matt9:25) parallels [MRK 5:22–5:42](https://ref.ly/Mark5:22-Mark5:42), [LUK 8:41–8:55](https://ref.ly/Luke8:41-Luke8:55); [JHN 11:43–11:44](https://ref.ly/John11:43-John11:44)

### Jesus Christ's power over his own life

**[JHN 10:18](https://ref.ly/John10:18)** *See also* [HEB 7:16](https://ref.ly/Heb7:16)

### Jesus Christ's power over human behaviour

**[MAT 4:20](https://ref.ly/Matt4:20)** parallel [LUK 5:11](https://ref.ly/Luke5:11) *See also* [MAT 9:9](https://ref.ly/Matt9:9) parallels [MRK 2:14](https://ref.ly/Mark2:14), [LUK 5:27–5:28](https://ref.ly/Luke5:27-Luke5:28); [MRK 15:5](https://ref.ly/Mark15:5); [JHN 11:29](https://ref.ly/John11:29), [JHN 19:10–19:11](https://ref.ly/John19:10-John19:11)

### Jesus Christ's power over forces of evil

**[MAT 8:16](https://ref.ly/Matt8:16)** parallels [MRK 1:32–1:34](https://ref.ly/Mark1:32-Mark1:34), [LUK 4:40–4:41](https://ref.ly/Luke4:40-Luke4:41) *See also* [MAT 4:10–4:11](https://ref.ly/Matt4:10-Matt4:11) parallels [MRK 1:13](https://ref.ly/Mark1:13), [LUK 4:12–4:13](https://ref.ly/Luke4:12-Luke4:13); [MAT 9:32–9:33](https://ref.ly/Matt9:32-Matt9:33), [MAT 12:22](https://ref.ly/Matt12:22), [MAT 17:18](https://ref.ly/Matt17:18) parallels [MRK 9:25](https://ref.ly/Mark9:25), [LUK 9:42](https://ref.ly/Luke9:42); [JHN 14:30](https://ref.ly/John14:30)

Jesus Christ has power over sin and death
-----------------------------------------

### Jesus Christ's crucifixion defeats the power of sin

**[ROM 6:6](https://ref.ly/Rom6:6)** *See also* [ISA 53:10–53:12](https://ref.ly/Isa53:10-Isa53:12); [MAT 9:6](https://ref.ly/Matt9:6); [JHN 15:13](https://ref.ly/John15:13); [1CO 15:3](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:3); [TIT 2:14](https://ref.ly/Titus2:14); [HEB 9:28](https://ref.ly/Heb9:28); [1PE 2:24](https://ref.ly/1Pet2:24); [REV 5:9](https://ref.ly/Rev5:9)

### Jesus Christ's power over sin and death remains effective

**[HEB 7:25](https://ref.ly/Heb7:25)** *See also* [JHN 6:40](https://ref.ly/John6:40); [ROM 8:2–8:3](https://ref.ly/Rom8:2-Rom8:3); [1CO 15:22](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:22); [HEB 7:26–7:28](https://ref.ly/Heb7:26-Heb7:28); [1PE 3:18](https://ref.ly/1Pet3:18)

Jesus Christ's power remains available in human experience
----------------------------------------------------------

### Jesus Christ's forgiving power is effective today

**[ACT 13:38–13:39](https://ref.ly/Acts13:38-Acts13:39)** *See also* [JHN 20:23](https://ref.ly/John20:23); [ACT 5:31](https://ref.ly/Acts5:31); [EPH 1:7](https://ref.ly/Eph1:7)

## 2069: Jesus Christ, pre-eminence of (id: 2069)

Jesus Christ excels over all of creation and reigns supreme over everthing in the created order.

The scope of Jesus Christ's pre\-eminence
-----------------------------------------

### Over all people

**[JHN 17:2](https://ref.ly/John17:2)** *See also* [MAT 25:31–25:32](https://ref.ly/Matt25:31-Matt25:32); [ROM 10:12](https://ref.ly/Rom10:12)

### Over his enemies

**[1CO 15:25–15:26](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:25-1Cor15:26)** *See also* [ACT 2:32–2:35](https://ref.ly/Acts2:32-Acts2:35); [PSA 110:1](https://ref.ly/Ps110:1); [EPH 4:8](https://ref.ly/Eph4:8) *Paul probably interpreted “captives” to refer to the spiritual enemies of Christ defeated at the cross.*

### Over every power and authority

**[COL 2:15](https://ref.ly/Col2:15)** *See also* [EPH 1:21](https://ref.ly/Eph1:21)

### Over all traditions and institutions

[MAT 12:8](https://ref.ly/Matt12:8) parallels [MRK 2:28](https://ref.ly/Mark2:28), [LUK 6:5](https://ref.ly/Luke6:5)

### Over all things

**[1CO 15:28](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:28)** *See also* [MAT 11:27](https://ref.ly/Matt11:27) parallel [LUK 10:22](https://ref.ly/Luke10:22); [MAT 28:18](https://ref.ly/Matt28:18); [JHN 3:35](https://ref.ly/John3:35), [JHN 13:3](https://ref.ly/John13:3), [JHN 16:33](https://ref.ly/John16:33); [ACT 10:36](https://ref.ly/Acts10:36); [PHP 3:21](https://ref.ly/Phil3:21); [HEB 2:8](https://ref.ly/Heb2:8)

The pre\-eminence of Jesus Christ in relation to others
-------------------------------------------------------

### To other prophets

[MAT 3:11](https://ref.ly/Matt3:11), [MAT 12:41](https://ref.ly/Matt12:41) parallel [LUK 11:32](https://ref.ly/Luke11:32); ; [JHN 1:26–1:27](https://ref.ly/John1:26-John1:27), [JHN 1:30](https://ref.ly/John1:30), [JHN 3:30](https://ref.ly/John3:30); ; [HEB 1:1–1:2](https://ref.ly/Heb1:1-Heb1:2)

### To the patriarchs

[JHN 1:17](https://ref.ly/John1:17), [JHN 8:52–8:58](https://ref.ly/John8:52-John8:58); ; [HEB 3:3–3:6](https://ref.ly/Heb3:3-Heb3:6)

### To Aaron and other high priests

**[HEB 8:1–8:6](https://ref.ly/Heb8:1-Heb8:6)** *See also* [HEB 4:14](https://ref.ly/Heb4:14), [HEB 6:20](https://ref.ly/Heb6:20), [HEB 7:23](https://ref.ly/Heb7:23), [HEB 7:26–7:28](https://ref.ly/Heb7:26-Heb7:28), [HEB 9:11–9:14](https://ref.ly/Heb9:11-Heb9:14), [HEB 9:24–9:26](https://ref.ly/Heb9:24-Heb9:26)

### To angels

**[1PE 3:22](https://ref.ly/1Pet3:22)** *See also* [HEB 1:4–1:14](https://ref.ly/Heb1:4-Heb1:14)

### To other lords and kings

**[REV 17:14](https://ref.ly/Rev17:14)** *See also* [1TI 6:15](https://ref.ly/1Tim6:15); [REV 19:16](https://ref.ly/Rev19:16)

Descriptions of Jesus Christ's pre\-eminence
--------------------------------------------

### He is the head

**[COL 2:10](https://ref.ly/Col2:10)** *See also* [EPH 1:9–1:10](https://ref.ly/Eph1:9-Eph1:10), [EPH 1:22](https://ref.ly/Eph1:22), [EPH 4:15](https://ref.ly/Eph4:15), [EPH 5:23–5:24](https://ref.ly/Eph5:23-Eph5:24); [COL 1:18](https://ref.ly/Col1:18)

### He is the capstone

**[MAT 21:42](https://ref.ly/Matt21:42)** parallels [MRK 12:10–12:11](https://ref.ly/Mark12:10-Mark12:11), [LUK 20:17](https://ref.ly/Luke20:17) *By so saying Jesus Christ applied this verse to himself. The capstone/cornerstone was the most significant stone of a building's structure.* *See also* [PSA 118:22](https://ref.ly/Ps118:22); [ACT 4:11](https://ref.ly/Acts4:11); [EPH 2:20](https://ref.ly/Eph2:20); [1PE 2:7](https://ref.ly/1Pet2:7)

### He is the Chief Shepherd

[JHN 10:11](https://ref.ly/John10:11); ; [HEB 13:20](https://ref.ly/Heb13:20); ; [1PE 5:4](https://ref.ly/1Pet5:4)

The reasons for Jesus Christ's pre\-eminence
--------------------------------------------

### His divine origin

**[JHN 3:31](https://ref.ly/John3:31)** *See also* [JHN 1:1–1:2](https://ref.ly/John1:1-John1:2), [JHN 17:24](https://ref.ly/John17:24)

### His equality with the Father

**[JHN 10:30](https://ref.ly/John10:30)** *See also* [COL 1:19](https://ref.ly/Col1:19), [COL 2:9](https://ref.ly/Col2:9)

### His authority derives from the Father

[JHN 5:22–5:27](https://ref.ly/John5:22-John5:27)

### He possesses the rights of the firstborn

**[COL 1:15–1:17](https://ref.ly/Col1:15-Col1:17)** *As the firstborn son has the rights and privileges of an heir, so Jesus Christ is heir of all things by virtue of his pre\-existence and sonship.* *See also* [ROM 8:29](https://ref.ly/Rom8:29); [HEB 1:6](https://ref.ly/Heb1:6)

### He has a superior name

**[PHP 2:9](https://ref.ly/Phil2:9)** *See also* [ACT 4:12](https://ref.ly/Acts4:12); [HEB 1:4](https://ref.ly/Heb1:4)

### He is the First and the Last

**[REV 1:17](https://ref.ly/Rev1:17)** *This title implies that all things are summed up in Christ and find their purpose in him.* *See also* [REV 2:8](https://ref.ly/Rev2:8), [REV 22:13](https://ref.ly/Rev22:13)

Examples of events whereby Jesus Christ's pre\-eminence is recognised
---------------------------------------------------------------------

### His entry into Jerusalem

[MAT 21:4–21:9](https://ref.ly/Matt21:4-Matt21:9) parallels [MRK 11:7–11:10](https://ref.ly/Mark11:7-Mark11:10), [LUK 19:35–19:38](https://ref.ly/Luke19:35-Luke19:38), [JHN 12:12–12:15](https://ref.ly/John12:12-John12:15); ; [ZEC 9:9](https://ref.ly/Zech9:9)

### His resurrection

[ROM 1:4](https://ref.ly/Rom1:4); ; [1CO 15:21–15:23](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:21-1Cor15:23); ; [REV 1:5](https://ref.ly/Rev1:5)

### His exaltation to the Father's right hand

**[ACT 5:31](https://ref.ly/Acts5:31)** *See also* [ACT 2:33](https://ref.ly/Acts2:33), [ACT 7:55](https://ref.ly/Acts7:55); [EPH 1:20–1:21](https://ref.ly/Eph1:20-Eph1:21), [EPH 4:8–4:10](https://ref.ly/Eph4:8-Eph4:10); [PHP 2:9–2:11](https://ref.ly/Phil2:9-Phil2:11); [COL 3:1](https://ref.ly/Col3:1); [HEB 8:1](https://ref.ly/Heb8:1), [HEB 10:12](https://ref.ly/Heb10:12); [1PE 3:22](https://ref.ly/1Pet3:22); [REV 3:21](https://ref.ly/Rev3:21)

## 2072: Jesus Christ, righteousness of (id: 2072)

Jesus Christ pleased his Father perfectly in his life on earth and in his death. He now gives believers a new status before God and a new power for living.

The promised Messiah will be righteous
--------------------------------------

**[ZEC 9:9](https://ref.ly/Zech9:9)** *See also* [PSA 45:7](https://ref.ly/Ps45:7); [ISA 53:11](https://ref.ly/Isa53:11); [JER 23:5–23:6](https://ref.ly/Jer23:5-Jer23:6), [JER 33:15](https://ref.ly/Jer33:15)

--------------------------------

## 2075: Jesus Christ, sinlessness of (id: 2075)

The complete absence of sin, only in Jesus Christ. Christ demonstrated complete obedience to God in spite of his human frailty, enabling him to be a perfect atoning sacrifice and to give his righteousness to sinners.

Jesus Christ fully experienced human weakness
---------------------------------------------

[PHP 2:7](https://ref.ly/Phil2:7); ; [HEB 2:14](https://ref.ly/Heb2:14), [HEB 2:17](https://ref.ly/Heb2:17)

## 2078: Jesus Christ, sonship of (id: 2078)

Jesus Christ is described as Son of David, Son of Man and Son of God. His sonship speaks of his divinity and humanity and is closely associated with his role as promised Messiah, suffering Saviour, risen Lord and coming judge and king. It also speaks of his intimate, obedient and unique relationship with his Father and of his mission to enable people to become children of God through faith in him.

Jesus Christ as the Son of David
--------------------------------

### He is physically descended from David

**[MAT 1:1](https://ref.ly/Matt1:1)** *See also* [MAT 1:2–1:20](https://ref.ly/Matt1:2-Matt1:20); [LUK 1:27](https://ref.ly/Luke1:27), [LUK 1:32](https://ref.ly/Luke1:32), [LUK 2:4](https://ref.ly/Luke2:4), [LUK 2:11](https://ref.ly/Luke2:11), [LUK 3:23–3:38](https://ref.ly/Luke3:23-Luke3:38); [ROM 1:3](https://ref.ly/Rom1:3); [2TI 2:8](https://ref.ly/2Tim2:8); [REV 22:16](https://ref.ly/Rev22:16)

### He is the promised royal Messiah of David's line

**[ISA 16:5](https://ref.ly/Isa16:5)** *See also* [2SA 7:12–7:16](https://ref.ly/2Sam7:12-2Sam7:16) parallel [1CH 17:11–17:14](https://ref.ly/1Chr17:11-1Chr17:14); [PSA 89:1–89:4](https://ref.ly/Ps89:1-Ps89:4), [PSA 132:11](https://ref.ly/Ps132:11), [PSA 132:17](https://ref.ly/Ps132:17); [ISA 9:7](https://ref.ly/Isa9:7), [ISA 11:1](https://ref.ly/Isa11:1); [JER 23:5–23:6](https://ref.ly/Jer23:5-Jer23:6), [JER 33:15–33:16](https://ref.ly/Jer33:15-Jer33:16); [EZK 34:23–34:24](https://ref.ly/Ezek34:23-Ezek34:24), [EZK 37:24–37:25](https://ref.ly/Ezek37:24-Ezek37:25)[ZEC 3:8](https://ref.ly/Zech3:8), [ZEC 6:12](https://ref.ly/Zech6:12)

### He is both the Son and Lord of David

**[MAT 22:41–22:45](https://ref.ly/Matt22:41-Matt22:45)** parallels [MRK 12:35–12:37](https://ref.ly/Mark12:35-Mark12:37), [LUK 20:41–20:44](https://ref.ly/Luke20:41-Luke20:44) *See also* [PSA 110:1](https://ref.ly/Ps110:1)

Jesus Christ as the Son of Man
------------------------------

**[MRK 2:10](https://ref.ly/Mark2:10)** parallels [MAT 9:6](https://ref.ly/Matt9:6), [LUK 5:24](https://ref.ly/Luke5:24)**[JHN 3:13](https://ref.ly/John3:13)** *See also* [DAN 7:13–7:14](https://ref.ly/Dan7:13-Dan7:14); [MRK 2:28](https://ref.ly/Mark2:28) parallels [MAT 12:8](https://ref.ly/Matt12:8), [LUK 6:5](https://ref.ly/Luke6:5); [JHN 1:51](https://ref.ly/John1:51), [JHN 6:27](https://ref.ly/John6:27), [JHN 8:28](https://ref.ly/John8:28)

### His knowledge of the Father's will

### His role as promised Messiah

**[MAT 16:16](https://ref.ly/Matt16:16)** parallel [LUK 9:20](https://ref.ly/Luke9:20) *See also* [2SA 7:12–7:14](https://ref.ly/2Sam7:12-2Sam7:14) parallel [1CH 17:11–17:13](https://ref.ly/1Chr17:11-1Chr17:13); [PSA 89:26–89:27](https://ref.ly/Ps89:26-Ps89:27); [ISA 9:6–9:7](https://ref.ly/Isa9:6-Isa9:7); [MAT 1:23](https://ref.ly/Matt1:23); [ISA 7:14](https://ref.ly/Isa7:14); [MAT 2:15](https://ref.ly/Matt2:15); [HOS 11:1](https://ref.ly/Hos11:1); [MAT 26:63–26:64](https://ref.ly/Matt26:63-Matt26:64) parallels [MRK 14:61–14:62](https://ref.ly/Mark14:61-Mark14:62), [LUK 22:70](https://ref.ly/Luke22:70); [LUK 4:41](https://ref.ly/Luke4:41), [LUK 22:29–22:30](https://ref.ly/Luke22:29-Luke22:30); [JHN 1:49](https://ref.ly/John1:49), [JHN 11:27](https://ref.ly/John11:27), [JHN 20:31](https://ref.ly/John20:31); [ACT 13:33](https://ref.ly/Acts13:33); [HEB 1:5](https://ref.ly/Heb1:5), [HEB 5:5](https://ref.ly/Heb5:5); [PSA 2:7](https://ref.ly/Ps2:7)

### His sharing the Father's character and being

**[HEB 1:3](https://ref.ly/Heb1:3)** *See also* [JHN 1:14](https://ref.ly/John1:14), [JHN 5:26](https://ref.ly/John5:26), [JHN 6:57](https://ref.ly/John6:57), [JHN 10:30](https://ref.ly/John10:30), [JHN 17:5](https://ref.ly/John17:5)

## 2081: Jesus Christ, wisdom of (id: 2081)

Jesus Christ's deep understanding of God, people and situations derived from his relationship with God his Father and from knowledge of his word. Christ's wisdom is seen in his words, actions and dealings with people.

The wisdom of Messiah was foretold and recognised in Jesus Christ
-----------------------------------------------------------------

**[ISA 11:2](https://ref.ly/Isa11:2)** *See also* [PRO 8:22–8:23](https://ref.ly/Prov8:22-Prov8:23); [ISA 52:13](https://ref.ly/Isa52:13); [JHN 1:1](https://ref.ly/John1:1), [JHN 4:29](https://ref.ly/John4:29); [1CO 1:24](https://ref.ly/1Cor1:24), [1CO 1:30](https://ref.ly/1Cor1:30); [COL 2:2–2:3](https://ref.ly/Col2:2-Col2:3)

-----------------------------------------------------

## 2206: Jesus, the Christ (id: 2206)

“Christ” means “Messiah” or “anointed one”. As the Christ, Jesus is the one who fulfils all OT expectations. Paul's phrase “in Christ” indicates the intimate relationship between Jesus Christ and his people.

The Christ as the anointed one
------------------------------

### The act of anointing in the OT

**[1SA 16:13](https://ref.ly/1Sam16:13)** *Anointing symbolises God's calling and being equipped by his Spirit.* *See also* [EXO 40:15](https://ref.ly/Exod40:15); [LEV 8:12](https://ref.ly/Lev8:12); [1SA 10:1](https://ref.ly/1Sam10:1); [1KI 1:39](https://ref.ly/1Kgs1:39)

### Anointed OT leaders

Priests: [EXO 29:7](https://ref.ly/Exod29:7); ; [LEV 4:3](https://ref.ly/Lev4:3), [LEV 4:5](https://ref.ly/Lev4:5), [LEV 6:20](https://ref.ly/Lev6:20), [LEV 16:32](https://ref.ly/Lev16:32); [1SA 24:6](https://ref.ly/1Sam24:6), [1SA 24:10](https://ref.ly/1Sam24:10), [1SA 26:9](https://ref.ly/1Sam26:9), [1SA 26:11](https://ref.ly/1Sam26:11), [1SA 26:16](https://ref.ly/1Sam26:16), [1SA 26:23](https://ref.ly/1Sam26:23); ; [PSA 18:50](https://ref.ly/Ps18:50), [PSA 20:6](https://ref.ly/Ps20:6), [PSA 132:10](https://ref.ly/Ps132:10)

### The OT promise of a future anointed leader

**[ISA 11:1–11:2](https://ref.ly/Isa11:1-Isa11:2)** *See also* [ISA 42:1](https://ref.ly/Isa42:1); [JER 23:5–23:6](https://ref.ly/Jer23:5-Jer23:6)

Jesus' own claims to be the Christ
----------------------------------

**[JHN 4:25–4:26](https://ref.ly/John4:25-John4:26)** *See also* [MAT 23:10](https://ref.ly/Matt23:10), [MAT 26:63–26:64](https://ref.ly/Matt26:63-Matt26:64) parallel [MRK 14:61–14:62](https://ref.ly/Mark14:61-Mark14:62); [JHN 10:24–10:25](https://ref.ly/John10:24-John10:25)

Jesus recognised as the Christ
------------------------------

**[MAT 16:16](https://ref.ly/Matt16:16)** parallels [MRK 8:29](https://ref.ly/Mark8:29), [LUK 9:20](https://ref.ly/Luke9:20) *See also* [LUK 2:26–2:32](https://ref.ly/Luke2:26-Luke2:32), [LUK 4:41](https://ref.ly/Luke4:41); [JHN 1:41–1:42](https://ref.ly/John1:41-John1:42), [JHN 11:27](https://ref.ly/John11:27)

Jesus' demand that his identity as the Christ should not be publicised
----------------------------------------------------------------------

**[MAT 16:20](https://ref.ly/Matt16:20)** parallels [MRK 8:30](https://ref.ly/Mark8:30), [LUK 9:21](https://ref.ly/Luke9:21) *Jesus' reluctance to be known as the Christ is probably due to Jewish misunderstandings of the Messiah's true role.* *See also* [MAT 12:16](https://ref.ly/Matt12:16); [LUK 4:41](https://ref.ly/Luke4:41)

Grounds for affirming Jesus as the Christ
-----------------------------------------

### Jesus Christ's birth in Bethlehem

**[MAT 2:4–2:6](https://ref.ly/Matt2:4-Matt2:6)** *See also* [MIC 5:2](https://ref.ly/Mic5:2); [LUK 2:4–2:7](https://ref.ly/Luke2:4-Luke2:7)

### Jesus Christ's spiritual anointing from God

**[ACT 10:38](https://ref.ly/Acts10:38)** *See also* [MAT 3:16](https://ref.ly/Matt3:16) parallels [MRK 1:10](https://ref.ly/Mark1:10), [LUK 3:22](https://ref.ly/Luke3:22); [JHN 3:34](https://ref.ly/John3:34); [ACT 4:27](https://ref.ly/Acts4:27)

### Jesus Christ's proclamation of Jubilee

**[LUK 4:17–4:21](https://ref.ly/Luke4:17-Luke4:21)** *See also* [ISA 61:1–61:2](https://ref.ly/Isa61:1-Isa61:2) *Isaiah's words are borrowed from the language of the Year of Jubilee (Leviticus chapter 25\), which was to be a time when true freedom was restored.*

### Jesus Christ's healing ministry

**[MAT 8:16–8:17](https://ref.ly/Matt8:16-Matt8:17)** *See also* [ISA 53:4](https://ref.ly/Isa53:4); [MAT 11:2–11:5](https://ref.ly/Matt11:2-Matt11:5) parallel [LUK 7:18–7:23](https://ref.ly/Luke7:18-Luke7:23); [JHN 7:31](https://ref.ly/John7:31)

### Jesus Christ's prophetic ministry

**[JHN 4:29](https://ref.ly/John4:29)** *See also* [MAT 21:45–21:46](https://ref.ly/Matt21:45-Matt21:46), [MAT 26:67–26:68](https://ref.ly/Matt26:67-Matt26:68); [JHN 4:19](https://ref.ly/John4:19), [JHN 7:26](https://ref.ly/John7:26)

### Jesus Christ's suffering, death and resurrection

**[LUK 24:26](https://ref.ly/Luke24:26)** *See also* [LUK 24:46](https://ref.ly/Luke24:46); [ACT 3:18](https://ref.ly/Acts3:18), [ACT 17:3](https://ref.ly/Acts17:3), [ACT 26:23](https://ref.ly/Acts26:23); [1PE 1:11](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:11)

### Jesus Christ's fulfilment of prophecy

**[2CO 1:20](https://ref.ly/2Cor1:20)** *See also* [MAT 1:22–1:23](https://ref.ly/Matt1:22-Matt1:23); [ISA 7:14](https://ref.ly/Isa7:14); [MAT 26:21–26:24](https://ref.ly/Matt26:21-Matt26:24) parallel [MRK 14:18–14:21](https://ref.ly/Mark14:18-Mark14:21); [PSA 41:9](https://ref.ly/Ps41:9); [MAT 21:4–21:7](https://ref.ly/Matt21:4-Matt21:7) parallel [JHN 12:14–12:15](https://ref.ly/John12:14-John12:15); [ZEC 9:9](https://ref.ly/Zech9:9); [MAT 21:8–21:9](https://ref.ly/Matt21:8-Matt21:9) parallels [MRK 11:9–11:10](https://ref.ly/Mark11:9-Mark11:10), [LUK 19:37–19:38](https://ref.ly/Luke19:37-Luke19:38), [JHN 12:12–12:13](https://ref.ly/John12:12-John12:13); [PSA 118:26](https://ref.ly/Ps118:26); [ACT 2:22–2:36](https://ref.ly/Acts2:22-Acts2:36)

### God's establishment of Jesus Christ as king

**[LUK 1:32–1:33](https://ref.ly/Luke1:32-Luke1:33)** *See also* [PSA 2:6–2:7](https://ref.ly/Ps2:6-Ps2:7); [ISA 9:6](https://ref.ly/Isa9:6); [LUK 22:29](https://ref.ly/Luke22:29)

------------------------------

-----------------------------------------

**[MRK 14:61–14:64](https://ref.ly/Mark14:61-Mark14:64)** parallel [MAT 26:63–26:66](https://ref.ly/Matt26:63-Matt26:66)

That Jesus is the Christ is a central Christian belief
------------------------------------------------------

**[JHN 20:31](https://ref.ly/John20:31)** *See also* [JHN 11:27](https://ref.ly/John11:27); [1JN 5:1](https://ref.ly/1John5:1)

--------------------------------------------------

-----------------------------------------------------

**[GAL 2:20](https://ref.ly/Gal2:20)** *See also* [ROM 6:8](https://ref.ly/Rom6:8), [ROM 8:1](https://ref.ly/Rom8:1), [ROM 16:7](https://ref.ly/Rom16:7); [1CO 1:30](https://ref.ly/1Cor1:30); [EPH 1:13](https://ref.ly/Eph1:13); [COL 3:1](https://ref.ly/Col3:1)
