## 2212: Jesus Christ, head of the church (id: 2212)

Jesus Christ rules and governs his people and directs them towards the fulfilment of God's purposes. All power and authority within the church derive from Jesus Christ as the head.

Jesus Christ rules the universe in the interest of the church
-------------------------------------------------------------

**[EPH 1:22–1:23](https://ref.ly/Eph1:22-Eph1:23)** *See also* [EPH 1:10](https://ref.ly/Eph1:10); [COL 1:18](https://ref.ly/Col1:18)

All power and authority within the church derive from Jesus Christ as the head
------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Jesus Christ is recognised as head of the church

**[EPH 4:15](https://ref.ly/Eph4:15)** *See also* [EPH 5:23](https://ref.ly/Eph5:23); [COL 2:19](https://ref.ly/Col2:19)

### Within the church Jesus Christ alone rules with authority

**[MAT 23:8–23:10](https://ref.ly/Matt23:8-Matt23:10)** *See also* [JHN 13:13](https://ref.ly/John13:13); [2CO 4:5](https://ref.ly/2Cor4:5)

### The church owes obedience to its head

**[JHN 14:15](https://ref.ly/John14:15)** *See also* [JHN 14:21](https://ref.ly/John14:21), [JHN 14:23](https://ref.ly/John14:23); [EPH 5:24](https://ref.ly/Eph5:24); [1JN 3:24](https://ref.ly/1John3:24)

### All human authority in the church derives from its head

**[EPH 4:11](https://ref.ly/Eph4:11)** *See also* [GAL 1:1](https://ref.ly/Gal1:1)

Jesus Christ is the cornerstone and builder of the church
---------------------------------------------------------

**[EPH 2:20–2:22](https://ref.ly/Eph2:20-Eph2:22)** *See also* [MAT 16:18](https://ref.ly/Matt16:18); [ACT 4:11](https://ref.ly/Acts4:11); [PSA 118:22](https://ref.ly/Ps118:22); [1PE 2:4–2:6](https://ref.ly/1Pet2:4-1Pet2:6)

Jesus Christ's role as head of the church
-----------------------------------------

### He loves the church

**[EPH 5:25](https://ref.ly/Eph5:25)** *See also* [JHN 10:11](https://ref.ly/John10:11); [EPH 5:2](https://ref.ly/Eph5:2), [EPH 5:23](https://ref.ly/Eph5:23); [1JN 3:16](https://ref.ly/1John3:16)

### He cares for the church

**[REV 7:17](https://ref.ly/Rev7:17)** *See also* [JHN 10:14–10:15](https://ref.ly/John10:14-John10:15), [JHN 10:27–10:28](https://ref.ly/John10:27-John10:28), [JHN 17:12](https://ref.ly/John17:12); [EPH 5:29–5:30](https://ref.ly/Eph5:29-Eph5:30)

### He provides for the growth of the church

**[COL 2:19](https://ref.ly/Col2:19)** *See also* [EPH 4:15–4:16](https://ref.ly/Eph4:15-Eph4:16)

### He prays for the church

[JHN 17:20–17:26](https://ref.ly/John17:20-John17:26); ; [ROM 8:34](https://ref.ly/Rom8:34); ; [HEB 7:25](https://ref.ly/Heb7:25)

### He judges the church

**[REV 2:23](https://ref.ly/Rev2:23)** *See also* [ROM 14:10–14:12](https://ref.ly/Rom14:10-Rom14:12); [2CO 5:10](https://ref.ly/2Cor5:10); [EPH 6:8](https://ref.ly/Eph6:8)

### He will present the church blameless before God

**[EPH 5:27](https://ref.ly/Eph5:27)** *See also* [2CO 4:14](https://ref.ly/2Cor4:14); [COL 1:22](https://ref.ly/Col1:22); [JUD 1:24](https://ref.ly/Jude1:24)

## 2215: Jesus Christ, Son of David (id: 2215)

A Messianic title. Jesus Christ comes as a descendant of David to fulfil God's promises in the OT of a future king who would establish the kingdom of God on earth.

OT promises of a future king from David's line
----------------------------------------------

**[2SA 7:12–7:14](https://ref.ly/2Sam7:12-2Sam7:14)** parallel [1CH 17:11–17:13](https://ref.ly/1Chr17:11-1Chr17:13) *These promises are known as “the Davidic covenant”*; **[ISA 16:5](https://ref.ly/Isa16:5)** *See also* [PSA 132:11–132:12](https://ref.ly/Ps132:11-Ps132:12), [PSA 132:17](https://ref.ly/Ps132:17); [ISA 9:7](https://ref.ly/Isa9:7), [ISA 11:1](https://ref.ly/Isa11:1); [JER 23:5](https://ref.ly/Jer23:5), [JER 33:15](https://ref.ly/Jer33:15); [EZK 34:23–34:24](https://ref.ly/Ezek34:23-Ezek34:24), [EZK 37:24–37:25](https://ref.ly/Ezek37:24-Ezek37:25); [JHN 7:42](https://ref.ly/John7:42)

NT statements verifying that Jesus Christ is descended from David
-----------------------------------------------------------------

**[MAT 1:1](https://ref.ly/Matt1:1)** *See also* [LUK 3:23](https://ref.ly/Luke3:23), [LUK 3:31](https://ref.ly/Luke3:31); [ROM 1:3](https://ref.ly/Rom1:3); [2TI 2:8](https://ref.ly/2Tim2:8); [REV 22:16](https://ref.ly/Rev22:16)

Jesus Christ inherits the throne of David
-----------------------------------------

**[LUK 1:32–1:33](https://ref.ly/Luke1:32-Luke1:33)** *See also* [LUK 1:69](https://ref.ly/Luke1:69); [JHN 1:49](https://ref.ly/John1:49), [JHN 18:37](https://ref.ly/John18:37); [MAT 27:37](https://ref.ly/Matt27:37) parallels [MRK 15:26](https://ref.ly/Mark15:26), [LUK 23:38](https://ref.ly/Luke23:38), [JHN 19:19](https://ref.ly/John19:19)

Jesus Christ is called \`\`Son of David''
-----------------------------------------

### By those seeking healing

**[MAT 20:30–20:31](https://ref.ly/Matt20:30-Matt20:31)** parallels [MRK 10:47–10:48](https://ref.ly/Mark10:47-Mark10:48), [LUK 18:38–18:39](https://ref.ly/Luke18:38-Luke18:39) *See also* [MAT 9:27](https://ref.ly/Matt9:27), [MAT 15:22](https://ref.ly/Matt15:22)

### At his triumphal entry into Jerusalem

**[MAT 21:9](https://ref.ly/Matt21:9)** parallel [MRK 11:10](https://ref.ly/Mark11:10) *See also* [MAT 21:15](https://ref.ly/Matt21:15)

Grounds for identifying Jesus Christ as the Son of David
--------------------------------------------------------

### His human descent

**[ROM 1:3](https://ref.ly/Rom1:3)** *See also* [MAT 1:1](https://ref.ly/Matt1:1)

### His birth in Bethlehem

[MIC 5:2](https://ref.ly/Mic5:2); ; [JHN 7:42](https://ref.ly/John7:42)

### His healing ministry

**[MAT 12:22–12:23](https://ref.ly/Matt12:22-Matt12:23)** *One of the signs of the Messianic age was the healing of the sick (see [Isa 35:5–6](https://ref.ly/Isa35:5-Isa35:6); [42:7](https://ref.ly/Isa42:7)).* *See also* [JHN 7:31](https://ref.ly/John7:31)

### His ultimate victory

[REV 5:5](https://ref.ly/Rev5:5)

Jesus Christ is more than a merely human king descended from David
------------------------------------------------------------------

**[MRK 12:35–12:37](https://ref.ly/Mark12:35-Mark12:37)** *Jesus Christ claim is that he is not simply a human or political king, he is the Lord, the Son of God.* *See also* [PSA 110:1](https://ref.ly/Ps110:1); [JHN 18:36](https://ref.ly/John18:36)

* **Associated Passages:** 2 Samuel 7:12-14; 1 Chronicles 17:11-13; Isaiah 16:5; Psalms 132:11-12; Psalms 132:17; Isaiah 9:7; Isaiah 11:1; Jeremiah 23:5; Jeremiah 33:15; Ezekiel 34:23-24; Ezekiel 37:24-25; John 7:42; Matthew 1:1; Luke 3:23; Luke 3:31; Romans 1:3; 2 Timothy 2:8; Revelation 22:16; Luke 1:32-33; Luke 1:69; John 1:49; John 18:37; Matthew 27:37; Mark 15:26; Luke 23:38; John 19:19; Matthew 20:30-31; Mark 10:47-48; Luke 18:38-39; Matthew 9:27; Matthew 15:22; Matthew 21:9; Mark 11:10; Matthew 21:15; Micah 5:2; Matthew 12:22-23; Isaiah 35:5-6; Isaiah 42:7; John 7:31; Revelation 5:5; Mark 12:35-37; Psalms 110:1; John 18:36

## 2218: Jesus Christ, Son of God (id: 2218)

A title emphasising Jesus Christ's deity, his office as Messiah and his pre\-eminence as the object of the church's faith and worship and as the content of its gospel.

\`\`Son of God'' in the OT
--------------------------

### Israel as God's son

**[EXO 4:22–4:23](https://ref.ly/Exod4:22-Exod4:23)** *See also* [JER 31:9](https://ref.ly/Jer31:9), [JER 31:20](https://ref.ly/Jer31:20); [HOS 11:1](https://ref.ly/Hos11:1)

### The future Messiah/king as God's Son

**[PSA 2:7](https://ref.ly/Ps2:7)** *See also* [PSA 89:27](https://ref.ly/Ps89:27); [ACT 13:33](https://ref.ly/Acts13:33); [HEB 1:5](https://ref.ly/Heb1:5), [HEB 5:5](https://ref.ly/Heb5:5) *Jesus Christ perfectly fulfils all the OT promises concerning God's son, whether referring originally to Israel or to the Messiah.*

Jesus Christ is the Son of God
------------------------------

### Jesus Christ affirms he is God's Son

**[JHN 10:36](https://ref.ly/John10:36)** *See also* [LUK 22:70](https://ref.ly/Luke22:70) parallels [MAT 26:63–26:64](https://ref.ly/Matt26:63-Matt26:64), [MRK 14:61–14:62](https://ref.ly/Mark14:61-Mark14:62); [JHN 19:7](https://ref.ly/John19:7); [REV 2:18](https://ref.ly/Rev2:18)

### The Father affirms Jesus Christ is his Son

**[MAT 3:17](https://ref.ly/Matt3:17)** parallels [MRK 1:11](https://ref.ly/Mark1:11), [LUK 3:22](https://ref.ly/Luke3:22) *See also* [MAT 17:5](https://ref.ly/Matt17:5) parallels [MRK 9:7](https://ref.ly/Mark9:7), [LUK 9:35](https://ref.ly/Luke9:35); [2PE 1:17](https://ref.ly/2Pet1:17)

### Others affirm Jesus Christ is God's Son

**[MAT 14:33](https://ref.ly/Matt14:33)** *See also* [MRK 15:39](https://ref.ly/Mark15:39) parallel [MAT 27:54](https://ref.ly/Matt27:54); [JHN 1:34](https://ref.ly/John1:34); [ROM 1:4](https://ref.ly/Rom1:4); [HEB 4:14](https://ref.ly/Heb4:14); [2JN 1:3](https://ref.ly/2John1:3)

### Demons affirm Jesus Christ is God's Son

**[MRK 5:7](https://ref.ly/Mark5:7)** parallels [MAT 8:29](https://ref.ly/Matt8:29), [LUK 8:28](https://ref.ly/Luke8:28) *See also* [MRK 3:11](https://ref.ly/Mark3:11); [LUK 4:41](https://ref.ly/Luke4:41)

\`\`Son of God'' as a taunt
---------------------------

By the devil in the wilderness: [MAT 4:3](https://ref.ly/Matt4:3) parallel [LUK 4:3](https://ref.ly/Luke4:3); ; [MAT 4:6](https://ref.ly/Matt4:6) parallel [LUK 4:9](https://ref.ly/Luke4:9); [MAT 27:40](https://ref.ly/Matt27:40), [MAT 27:43](https://ref.ly/Matt27:43)

\`\`Son of God'' stresses Jesus Christ's deity
----------------------------------------------

### Jesus Christ is the Son of God the Father

**[JHN 3:35](https://ref.ly/John3:35)** *In John's Gospel in particular, the terms Son/Father are used many times to speak of Jesus Christ's unique relationship with God.* *See also* [MAT 11:27](https://ref.ly/Matt11:27) parallel [LUK 10:22](https://ref.ly/Luke10:22); [MAT 24:36](https://ref.ly/Matt24:36) parallel [MRK 13:32](https://ref.ly/Mark13:32); [JHN 5:20–5:22](https://ref.ly/John5:20-John5:22); [HEB 1:1–1:2](https://ref.ly/Heb1:1-Heb1:2); [1JN 1:3](https://ref.ly/1John1:3), [1JN 2:22–2:23](https://ref.ly/1John2:22-1John2:23); [2JN 1:9](https://ref.ly/2John1:9)

**[JHN 5:18](https://ref.ly/John5:18)** *See also* [JHN 5:23](https://ref.ly/John5:23), [JHN 10:30](https://ref.ly/John10:30), [JHN 10:33](https://ref.ly/John10:33), [JHN 14:9–14:10](https://ref.ly/John14:9-John14:10)

\`\`Son of God'' implies Jesus Christ's obedience to the Father
---------------------------------------------------------------

**[JHN 5:19](https://ref.ly/John5:19)** *See also* [MAT 26:39](https://ref.ly/Matt26:39) parallels [MRK 14:36](https://ref.ly/Mark14:36), [LUK 22:42](https://ref.ly/Luke22:42); [MAT 26:42](https://ref.ly/Matt26:42); [JHN 8:28](https://ref.ly/John8:28), [JHN 12:49](https://ref.ly/John12:49), [JHN 14:31](https://ref.ly/John14:31), [JHN 15:10](https://ref.ly/John15:10); [ROM 5:19](https://ref.ly/Rom5:19); [HEB 5:8](https://ref.ly/Heb5:8), [HEB 10:9](https://ref.ly/Heb10:9)

Jesus Christ as \`\`Son of God'' is the Messiah
-----------------------------------------------

### \`\`Son of God'' as a Messianic title for Jesus Christ

**[MAT 26:63–26:64](https://ref.ly/Matt26:63-Matt26:64)** parallels [MRK 14:61–14:62](https://ref.ly/Mark14:61-Mark14:62), [LUK 22:70–23:2](https://ref.ly/Luke22:70-Luke23:2) *See also* [MAT 16:16](https://ref.ly/Matt16:16); [MRK 1:1](https://ref.ly/Mark1:1); [LUK 1:32](https://ref.ly/Luke1:32), [LUK 4:41](https://ref.ly/Luke4:41); [JHN 1:49](https://ref.ly/John1:49), [JHN 11:27](https://ref.ly/John11:27)

**[GAL 4:4](https://ref.ly/Gal4:4)** *See also* [MAT 21:37](https://ref.ly/Matt21:37) parallels [MRK 12:6](https://ref.ly/Mark12:6), [LUK 20:13](https://ref.ly/Luke20:13); [JHN 3:16–3:17](https://ref.ly/John3:16-John3:17); [ROM 8:3](https://ref.ly/Rom8:3), [ROM 8:32](https://ref.ly/Rom8:32); [1JN 4:9](https://ref.ly/1John4:9)

## 2221: Jesus Christ, Son of Man (id: 2221)

Jesus Christ's preferred title for himself. The term points to the humanity and servanthood of Christ, but also reflects Daniel's vision of the son of man as a coming figure of judgment and authority.

Jesus Christ as the Son of Man in his human nature
--------------------------------------------------

### OT use of `son of man'' to mean`human being''

**[NUM 23:19](https://ref.ly/Num23:19)** *See also* [JOB 25:6](https://ref.ly/Job25:6), [JOB 35:8](https://ref.ly/Job35:8); [PSA 8:4](https://ref.ly/Ps8:4), [PSA 80:17](https://ref.ly/Ps80:17), [PSA 144:3](https://ref.ly/Ps144:3)

### Jesus Christ describes himself as Son of Man to stress his humanity

**[MAT 8:20](https://ref.ly/Matt8:20)** parallel [LUK 9:58](https://ref.ly/Luke9:58) *See also* [MAT 11:19](https://ref.ly/Matt11:19) parallel [LUK 7:34](https://ref.ly/Luke7:34); [MAT 16:13](https://ref.ly/Matt16:13), [MAT 16:15](https://ref.ly/Matt16:15); [LUK 6:22](https://ref.ly/Luke6:22); [JHN 9:35](https://ref.ly/John9:35)

### Blasphemy against the Son of Man is forgivable

**[MAT 12:32](https://ref.ly/Matt12:32)** *See also* [LUK 12:10](https://ref.ly/Luke12:10)

Jesus Christ as the Son of Man in his prophetic ministry
--------------------------------------------------------

### The OT use of \`\`son of man'' as a title for Ezekiel

[EZK 2:1](https://ref.ly/Ezek2:1)

### Jesus Christ preaches God's word

**[MAT 13:37–13:43](https://ref.ly/Matt13:37-Matt13:43)**

### Jesus Christ offers the words of eternal life

**[JHN 6:27](https://ref.ly/John6:27)** *See also* [JHN 6:53](https://ref.ly/John6:53), [JHN 6:63](https://ref.ly/John6:63), [JHN 6:68](https://ref.ly/John6:68)

Jesus Christ as the Son of Man in his suffering and death
---------------------------------------------------------

### Jesus Christ as a servant

**[MAT 20:28](https://ref.ly/Matt20:28)** parallel [MRK 10:45](https://ref.ly/Mark10:45)

### Jesus Christ came to suffer, die and be raised

**[LUK 24:6–24:7](https://ref.ly/Luke24:6-Luke24:7)** *See also* [MAT 12:40](https://ref.ly/Matt12:40) parallel [LUK 11:30](https://ref.ly/Luke11:30) *the sign of Jonah*; [MAT 17:9](https://ref.ly/Matt17:9) parallel [MRK 9:9](https://ref.ly/Mark9:9) *the transfiguration*[MAT 17:22–17:23](https://ref.ly/Matt17:22-Matt17:23) parallels [MRK 9:31](https://ref.ly/Mark9:31), [LUK 9:44](https://ref.ly/Luke9:44); [MAT 20:18](https://ref.ly/Matt20:18) parallels [MRK 10:33](https://ref.ly/Mark10:33), [LUK 18:31](https://ref.ly/Luke18:31); [MAT 26:24](https://ref.ly/Matt26:24) parallels [MRK 14:21](https://ref.ly/Mark14:21), [LUK 22:22](https://ref.ly/Luke22:22); [MRK 8:31](https://ref.ly/Mark8:31) parallel [LUK 9:22](https://ref.ly/Luke9:22); [JHN 3:14](https://ref.ly/John3:14), [JHN 12:23](https://ref.ly/John12:23), [JHN 13:31](https://ref.ly/John13:31)

Jesus Christ as the Son of Man in his authority and dominion
------------------------------------------------------------

### The vision of the son of man

**[DAN 7:13–7:14](https://ref.ly/Dan7:13-Dan7:14)** *This passage provides the main OT background to Jesus Christ's understanding of himself as the “Son of Man”. His main uses of the title emphasise his dominion and authority, and also paradoxically that this glory will be attained through the humiliation of the cross.*

### Son of man meaning \`\`son of Adam''

**[GEN 1:26](https://ref.ly/Gen1:26)** *Jesus Christ as Son of Man (in the Hebrew “son of Adam”) inherits the promise originally given to Adam of dominion over creation, which Adam forfeited because of his fall into sin.* *See also* [ROM 5:14](https://ref.ly/Rom5:14); [1CO 15:45](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:45); [HEB 2:6–2:9](https://ref.ly/Heb2:6-Heb2:9); [PSA 8:4–8:6](https://ref.ly/Ps8:4-Ps8:6)

### Jesus Christ had authority on earth

**[MAT 9:6](https://ref.ly/Matt9:6)** parallels [MRK 2:10](https://ref.ly/Mark2:10), [LUK 5:24](https://ref.ly/Luke5:24) *Authority to forgive sins.* *See also* [MAT 12:8](https://ref.ly/Matt12:8) parallels [MRK 2:28](https://ref.ly/Mark2:28), [LUK 6:5](https://ref.ly/Luke6:5) *authority over the Sabbath*

### Jesus Christ is now ascended into glory

**[ACT 7:55–7:56](https://ref.ly/Acts7:55-Acts7:56)** *See also* [REV 1:13](https://ref.ly/Rev1:13), [REV 14:14](https://ref.ly/Rev14:14)

### Jesus Christ will come to judge and reign over all

**[MAT 16:27–16:28](https://ref.ly/Matt16:27-Matt16:28)** parallels [MRK 8:38](https://ref.ly/Mark8:38), [LUK 9:26](https://ref.ly/Luke9:26) *See also* [MAT 10:23](https://ref.ly/Matt10:23), [MAT 24:30](https://ref.ly/Matt24:30) parallels [MRK 13:26](https://ref.ly/Mark13:26), [LUK 21:27](https://ref.ly/Luke21:27) *the second coming*; [MAT 24:44](https://ref.ly/Matt24:44) parallel [LUK 12:40](https://ref.ly/Luke12:40) *the day and hour unknown*; [MAT 26:64](https://ref.ly/Matt26:64) parallels [MRK 14:62](https://ref.ly/Mark14:62), [LUK 22:69](https://ref.ly/Luke22:69) *Jesus Christ before the Sanhedrin*; [LUK 18:8](https://ref.ly/Luke18:8), [LUK 21:36](https://ref.ly/Luke21:36); [JHN 5:27](https://ref.ly/John5:27)

* **Associated Passages:** Numbers 23:19; Job 25:6; Job 35:8; Psalms 8:4; Psalms 80:17; Psalms 144:3; Matthew 8:20; Luke 9:58; Matthew 11:19; Luke 7:34; Matthew 16:13; Matthew 16:15; Luke 6:22; John 9:35; Matthew 12:32; Luke 12:10; Ezekiel 2:1; Matthew 13:37-43; John 6:27; John 6:53; John 6:63; John 6:68; Matthew 20:28; Mark 10:45; Luke 24:6-7; Matthew 12:40; Luke 11:30; Matthew 17:9; Mark 9:9; Matthew 17:22-23; Mark 9:31; Luke 9:44; Matthew 20:18; Mark 10:33; Luke 18:31; Matthew 26:24; Mark 14:21; Luke 22:22; Mark 8:31; Luke 9:22; John 3:14; John 12:23; John 13:31; Daniel 7:13-14; Genesis 1:26; Romans 5:14; 1 Corinthians 15:45; Hebrews 2:6-9; Psalms 8:4-6; Matthew 9:6; Mark 2:10; Luke 5:24; Matthew 12:8; Mark 2:28; Luke 6:5; Acts 7:55-56; Revelation 1:13; Revelation 14:14; Matthew 16:27-28; Mark 8:38; Luke 9:26; Matthew 10:23; Matthew 24:30; Mark 13:26; Luke 21:27; Matthew 24:44; Luke 12:40; Matthew 26:64; Mark 14:62; Luke 22:69; Luke 18:8; Luke 21:36; John 5:27

## 2224: Jesus Christ, the Lord (id: 2224)

A title that signifies Jesus Christ's absolute authority and the basis on which people may know him. It is especially associated with his resurrection and return.

Lord as a title of respect for the earthly Jesus Christ
-------------------------------------------------------

**[MAT 8:25](https://ref.ly/Matt8:25)** *See also* [MAT 15:25](https://ref.ly/Matt15:25), [MAT 15:27](https://ref.ly/Matt15:27) parallel [MRK 7:28](https://ref.ly/Mark7:28); [MAT 21:3](https://ref.ly/Matt21:3) parallels [MRK 11:3](https://ref.ly/Mark11:3), [LUK 19:31](https://ref.ly/Luke19:31)

Lord as a mark of Jesus Christ's authority as a teacher
-------------------------------------------------------

**[1TH 4:15](https://ref.ly/1Thess4:15)** *See also* [ACT 11:16](https://ref.ly/Acts11:16), [ACT 20:35](https://ref.ly/Acts20:35); [1CO 7:10](https://ref.ly/1Cor7:10)

Lord as a sign of Jesus Christ's divinity
-----------------------------------------

### Jesus Christ's divinity

**[JHN 20:28](https://ref.ly/John20:28)** *“Lord” is a common divine title in the Greek OT and is instinctively transferred to Jesus Christ in the NT.* *See also* [1CO 8:6](https://ref.ly/1Cor8:6); [2CO 3:17–3:18](https://ref.ly/2Cor3:17-2Cor3:18); [EPH 4:5](https://ref.ly/Eph4:5); [2TH 2:16](https://ref.ly/2Thess2:16); [2PE 1:2](https://ref.ly/2Pet1:2)

### The day of Christ Jesus

**[PHP 1:6](https://ref.ly/Phil1:6)** *The “day of Christ Jesus” is equivalent to the OT “day of the LORD”.* *See also* [1CO 1:8](https://ref.ly/1Cor1:8); [2CO 1:14](https://ref.ly/2Cor1:14); [PHP 1:10](https://ref.ly/Phil1:10), [PHP 2:16](https://ref.ly/Phil2:16); [REV 1:10](https://ref.ly/Rev1:10)

### Jesus Christ is ruler over all

**[REV 17:14](https://ref.ly/Rev17:14)** *See also* [DEU 10:17](https://ref.ly/Deut10:17); [REV 19:16](https://ref.ly/Rev19:16)

### Jesus Christ is the Saviour

**[ROM 10:13](https://ref.ly/Rom10:13)** *See also* [JOL 2:32](https://ref.ly/Joel2:32); [ACT 2:21](https://ref.ly/Acts2:21)

### Jesus Christ is Lord of the Sabbath

**[MAT 12:8](https://ref.ly/Matt12:8)** parallels [MRK 2:28](https://ref.ly/Mark2:28), [LUK 6:5](https://ref.ly/Luke6:5)

Jesus the Messiah is Lord
-------------------------

**[ACT 2:36](https://ref.ly/Acts2:36)** *“Christ” is the Greek equivalent of the Hebrew word “Messiah”.* *See also* [2CO 4:5](https://ref.ly/2Cor4:5); [COL 3:24](https://ref.ly/Col3:24)

### \`\`Jesus is Lord'' is the basic Christian statement of faith

**[ROM 10:9](https://ref.ly/Rom10:9)** *See also* [ACT 11:20](https://ref.ly/Acts11:20), [ACT 16:31](https://ref.ly/Acts16:31), [ACT 20:21](https://ref.ly/Acts20:21); [1CO 12:3](https://ref.ly/1Cor12:3); [2CO 4:5](https://ref.ly/2Cor4:5); [PHP 2:10–2:11](https://ref.ly/Phil2:10-Phil2:11)

### Jesus is Lord because of the resurrection

**[ROM 1:4](https://ref.ly/Rom1:4)** *See also* [ACT 4:33](https://ref.ly/Acts4:33); [ROM 4:24](https://ref.ly/Rom4:24), [ROM 14:9](https://ref.ly/Rom14:9); [HEB 13:20](https://ref.ly/Heb13:20)

### Lord is a natural title for the risen Christ

**[LUK 24:34](https://ref.ly/Luke24:34)** *See also* [LUK 22:61](https://ref.ly/Luke22:61); [ACT 1:21](https://ref.ly/Acts1:21), [ACT 7:59](https://ref.ly/Acts7:59); [1CO 9:1](https://ref.ly/1Cor9:1), [1CO 9:5](https://ref.ly/1Cor9:5); [1TH 4:17](https://ref.ly/1Thess4:17)

Jesus Christ's lordship is the basis for his relationship with Christians
-------------------------------------------------------------------------

### It is a personal relationship

**[PHP 3:8](https://ref.ly/Phil3:8)** *See also* [ACT 16:15](https://ref.ly/Acts16:15); [ROM 5:11](https://ref.ly/Rom5:11), [ROM 14:8](https://ref.ly/Rom14:8); [1CO 6:17](https://ref.ly/1Cor6:17); [2PE 2:20](https://ref.ly/2Pet2:20)

### \`\`The name of the Lord'' expresses this relationship

**[1CO 6:11](https://ref.ly/1Cor6:11)** *See also* [ACT 8:16](https://ref.ly/Acts8:16), [ACT 15:26](https://ref.ly/Acts15:26), [ACT 19:5](https://ref.ly/Acts19:5), [ACT 21:13](https://ref.ly/Acts21:13); [EPH 5:20](https://ref.ly/Eph5:20); [COL 3:17](https://ref.ly/Col3:17)

### \`\`Jesus our Lord'' expresses this relationship

**[EPH 6:24](https://ref.ly/Eph6:24)** *See also* [1CO 15:57](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:57); [2CO 8:9](https://ref.ly/2Cor8:9); [GAL 6:14](https://ref.ly/Gal6:14); [EPH 5:20](https://ref.ly/Eph5:20); [1TH 5:28](https://ref.ly/1Thess5:28); [2TI 1:8](https://ref.ly/2Tim1:8)

### \`\`In the Lord'' as an expression of this relationship

**[PHM 1:16](https://ref.ly/Phlm1:16)** *See also* [ROM 16:12](https://ref.ly/Rom16:12); [EPH 6:10](https://ref.ly/Eph6:10); [PHP 1:14](https://ref.ly/Phil1:14), [PHP 2:29](https://ref.ly/Phil2:29), [PHP 3:1](https://ref.ly/Phil3:1); [PHM 1:20](https://ref.ly/Phlm1:20)

### The \`\`grace of the Lord'' as God's provision for this relationship

**[1TI 1:14](https://ref.ly/1Tim1:14)** *See also* [2CO 13:14](https://ref.ly/2Cor13:14); [2TH 3:18](https://ref.ly/2Thess3:18); [PHM 1:25](https://ref.ly/Phlm1:25); [2PE 3:18](https://ref.ly/2Pet3:18); [JUD 1:21](https://ref.ly/Jude1:21)

Jesus Christ's lordship is the basis for Christian obedience
------------------------------------------------------------

**[COL 2:6](https://ref.ly/Col2:6)** *See also* [ROM 12:11](https://ref.ly/Rom12:11); [COL 3:23](https://ref.ly/Col3:23); [2TH 1:8](https://ref.ly/2Thess1:8); [2TI 2:19](https://ref.ly/2Tim2:19); [1PE 3:15](https://ref.ly/1Pet3:15)

Jesus Christ's lordship will be fully revealed
----------------------------------------------

**[1TH 4:16](https://ref.ly/1Thess4:16)** *See also* [1CO 1:7](https://ref.ly/1Cor1:7); [PHP 3:20](https://ref.ly/Phil3:20); [1TH 5:23](https://ref.ly/1Thess5:23); [2TH 1:7](https://ref.ly/2Thess1:7); [1TI 6:14](https://ref.ly/1Tim6:14)

Jesus Christ's lordship signifies his absolute authority
--------------------------------------------------------

### Jesus Christ as judge of all

**[1CO 4:4](https://ref.ly/1Cor4:4)** *See also* [1CO 11:32](https://ref.ly/1Cor11:32); [2CO 10:18](https://ref.ly/2Cor10:18); [1TH 4:6](https://ref.ly/1Thess4:6); [2TH 1:8–1:9](https://ref.ly/2Thess1:8-2Thess1:9)

**[ROM 10:12](https://ref.ly/Rom10:12)** *See also* [ACT 10:36](https://ref.ly/Acts10:36); [1CO 8:6](https://ref.ly/1Cor8:6); [PHP 2:10–2:11](https://ref.ly/Phil2:10-Phil2:11); [COL 1:16–1:17](https://ref.ly/Col1:16-Col1:17)

## 2227: Immanuel (id: 2227)

An OT name given to Jesus Christ, meaning “God with us”.

Actual uses of the name Immanuel
--------------------------------

**[ISA 7:14](https://ref.ly/Isa7:14)** *The name was given originally to a child of Isaiah's day who would signify God's salvation and judgment for Judah*; **[ISA 8:7–8:10](https://ref.ly/Isa8:7-Isa8:10)** *The original fulfilment of the Immanuel prophecy would bring judgment on Judah*; **[MAT 1:22–1:23](https://ref.ly/Matt1:22-Matt1:23)** *Isaiah's prophecy is fulfilled through the virginal conception of Jesus Christ.*

The significance of Immanuel
----------------------------

### God is with his people

**[GEN 28:15](https://ref.ly/Gen28:15)** *See also* [EXO 33:14](https://ref.ly/Exod33:14); [NUM 14:9](https://ref.ly/Num14:9); [DEU 4:7](https://ref.ly/Deut4:7); [2CH 13:12](https://ref.ly/2Chr13:12); [PSA 46:7](https://ref.ly/Ps46:7), [PSA 46:11](https://ref.ly/Ps46:11); [HAG 2:4](https://ref.ly/Hag2:4); [ROM 8:31](https://ref.ly/Rom8:31); [HEB 13:5](https://ref.ly/Heb13:5)

### God dwells with his people

**[REV 21:3](https://ref.ly/Rev21:3)** *See also* [LEV 26:11–26:12](https://ref.ly/Lev26:11-Lev26:12); [EZK 37:27](https://ref.ly/Ezek37:27); [2CO 6:16](https://ref.ly/2Cor6:16)

### Jesus Christ is always with believers

**[MAT 28:20](https://ref.ly/Matt28:20)** *See also* [JHN 14:18](https://ref.ly/John14:18), [JHN 14:23](https://ref.ly/John14:23), [JHN 15:4–15:5](https://ref.ly/John15:4-John15:5), [JHN 15:7](https://ref.ly/John15:7); [ACT 18:10](https://ref.ly/Acts18:10); [GAL 2:20](https://ref.ly/Gal2:20)

### The Holy Spirit is always with believers

**[JHN 14:17](https://ref.ly/John14:17)** *See also* [ROM 8:9–8:11](https://ref.ly/Rom8:9-Rom8:11); [1CO 3:16](https://ref.ly/1Cor3:16); [2CO 1:22](https://ref.ly/2Cor1:22); [EPH 2:22](https://ref.ly/Eph2:22); [2TI 1:14](https://ref.ly/2Tim1:14); [1JN 4:13](https://ref.ly/1John4:13)

* **Associated Passages:** Isaiah 7:14; Isaiah 8:7-10; Matthew 1:22-23; Genesis 28:15; Exodus 33:14; Numbers 14:9; Deuteronomy 4:7; 2 Chronicles 13:12; Psalms 46:7; Psalms 46:11; Haggai 2:4; Romans 8:31; Hebrews 13:5; Revelation 21:3; Leviticus 26:11-12; Ezekiel 37:27; 2 Corinthians 6:16; Matthew 28:20; John 14:18; John 14:23; John 15:4-5; John 15:7; Acts 18:10; Galatians 2:20; John 14:17; Romans 8:9-11; 1 Corinthians 3:16; 2 Corinthians 1:22; Ephesians 2:22; 2 Timothy 1:14; 1 John 4:13
* **Associated Articles:** 1035: God, faithfulness of (ID: `1035@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 1429: prophecy, fulfilment of OT (ID: `1429@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2018: Jesus Christ, divinity of (ID: `2018@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2021: Jesus Christ, faithfulness of (ID: `2021@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2033: Jesus Christ, humanity of (ID: `2033@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2203: Jesus Christ, titles and names of (ID: `2203@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2206: Jesus, the Christ (ID: `2206@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2218: Jesus Christ, Son of God (ID: `2218@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2515: Jesus Christ, birth of (ID: `2515@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2550: Jesus Christ, pre-existence of (ID: `2550@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2595: incarnation (ID: `2595@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 7135: Israel, as the people of God (ID: `7135@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 2230: Messiah, coming of (id: 2230)

The coming of a figure chosen and anointed by God to deliver and redeem his people. Anointing was seen as a sign of being chosen by God for a special task of leadership or responsibility. The OT looked ahead to the final coming of such a figure to usher in a new era in the history of the people of God; the NT sees this expectation fulfilled in the person and work of Jesus Christ.

Anointing as a sign of being chosen by God
------------------------------------------

### Anointing with oil

**[LEV 8:12](https://ref.ly/Lev8:12)** *See also* [1SA 16:12–16:13](https://ref.ly/1Sam16:12-1Sam16:13); [2SA 2:4](https://ref.ly/2Sam2:4), [2SA 5:3](https://ref.ly/2Sam5:3) parallel [1CH 11:3](https://ref.ly/1Chr11:3); [1KI 1:39](https://ref.ly/1Kgs1:39); [2KI 9:6](https://ref.ly/2Kgs9:6); [PSA 89:20](https://ref.ly/Ps89:20)

### Anointing with the Holy Spirit

**[ISA 61:1](https://ref.ly/Isa61:1)** *See also* [LUK 4:18](https://ref.ly/Luke4:18); [JDG 14:19](https://ref.ly/Judg14:19); [1SA 11:6](https://ref.ly/1Sam11:6), [1SA 16:13](https://ref.ly/1Sam16:13); [ISA 11:2](https://ref.ly/Isa11:2); [MAT 12:18](https://ref.ly/Matt12:18); [ISA 42:1](https://ref.ly/Isa42:1)

Anointing as a sign of national and spiritual leadership
--------------------------------------------------------

### Anointed to be king

**[1CH 29:22](https://ref.ly/1Chr29:22)** *See also* [JDG 9:7–9:15](https://ref.ly/Judg9:7-Judg9:15); [1SA 9:16](https://ref.ly/1Sam9:16), [1SA 15:17](https://ref.ly/1Sam15:17); [2SA 19:10](https://ref.ly/2Sam19:10); [1KI 1:34](https://ref.ly/1Kgs1:34); [2KI 9:3](https://ref.ly/2Kgs9:3), [2KI 11:12](https://ref.ly/2Kgs11:12) parallel [2CH 23:11](https://ref.ly/2Chr23:11); [2CH 22:7](https://ref.ly/2Chr22:7)

### Anointed to be priest

**[EXO 40:13–40:15](https://ref.ly/Exod40:13-Exod40:15)** *See also* [EXO 28:41](https://ref.ly/Exod28:41), [EXO 29:7](https://ref.ly/Exod29:7); [LEV 7:35–7:36](https://ref.ly/Lev7:35-Lev7:36), [LEV 16:32](https://ref.ly/Lev16:32); [NUM 3:3](https://ref.ly/Num3:3)

### Anointed to be judge

The coming of the Spirit on some of the judges is a spiritual anointing: [JDG 3:10](https://ref.ly/Judg3:10), [JDG 6:34](https://ref.ly/Judg6:34), [JDG 11:29](https://ref.ly/Judg11:29), [JDG 15:14](https://ref.ly/Judg15:14)

### Anointed to be prophet

[1KI 19:16](https://ref.ly/1Kgs19:16); ; [ISA 48:16](https://ref.ly/Isa48:16); ; [EZK 11:5](https://ref.ly/Ezek11:5), [EZK 37:1](https://ref.ly/Ezek37:1); ; [MIC 3:8](https://ref.ly/Mic3:8)

## 2233: Son of Man (id: 2233)

A Hebrew and Aramaic term, often used to mean a human being in general. In the Gospels Jesus Christ uses it to refer to himself in his earthly ministry and his future death, exaltation and coming as judge and Saviour.

Sons of men as a term for humanity in general
---------------------------------------------

### Human beings are inferior to God

**[PSA 115:16](https://ref.ly/Ps115:16)** *The Hebrew term here translated “man” literally means “sons of men”. Many of the OT references cited in this theme follow this pattern.* *See also* [PSA 11:4](https://ref.ly/Ps11:4), [PSA 33:13–33:14](https://ref.ly/Ps33:13-Ps33:14), [PSA 45:2](https://ref.ly/Ps45:2)

### Human beings are dependent on God's care

**[PSA 8:4](https://ref.ly/Ps8:4)** *See also* [PSA 36:7](https://ref.ly/Ps36:7), [PSA 80:17](https://ref.ly/Ps80:17), [PSA 107:8](https://ref.ly/Ps107:8), [PSA 107:15](https://ref.ly/Ps107:15), [PSA 107:21](https://ref.ly/Ps107:21), [PSA 107:31](https://ref.ly/Ps107:31)

### Human beings are mortal

**[ECC 9:3](https://ref.ly/Eccl9:3)** *See also* [ECC 3:18–3:19](https://ref.ly/Eccl3:18-Eccl3:19); [EZK 31:14](https://ref.ly/Ezek31:14)

### Human beings are sinful and untrustworthy

**[PSA 146:3](https://ref.ly/Ps146:3)** *See also* [PSA 14:2–14:3](https://ref.ly/Ps14:2-Ps14:3) parallel [PSA 53:2–53:3](https://ref.ly/Ps53:2-Ps53:3); [MIC 5:7](https://ref.ly/Mic5:7)

Son of Man as a term for individual men
---------------------------------------

### The sons of Adam

[GEN 4:1–4:2](https://ref.ly/Gen4:1-Gen4:2) *“a man” is literally “son of Adam” in Hebrew*; ; [GEN 5:3–5:4](https://ref.ly/Gen5:3-Gen5:4)

### Ezekiel

**[EZK 2:1](https://ref.ly/Ezek2:1)** *Ezekiel is called “son of man” 93 times, though this form of address is unique to him in the OT. It may emphasise his remoteness or his humanity.* *See also* [EZK 2:3](https://ref.ly/Ezek2:3), [EZK 2:6](https://ref.ly/Ezek2:6), [EZK 2:8](https://ref.ly/Ezek2:8), [EZK 3:1](https://ref.ly/Ezek3:1)

### Other people

[JOB 25:6](https://ref.ly/Job25:6); ; [DAN 8:17](https://ref.ly/Dan8:17)

A son of man as a ruler of God's future kingdom
-----------------------------------------------

**[DAN 7:13](https://ref.ly/Dan7:13)** *The Aramaic “one like a son of man” stresses this person's humanity and mysterious identity*; **[DAN 7:13–7:14](https://ref.ly/Dan7:13-Dan7:14)** *He enters God's presence and is given final authority over God's kingdom*; **[DAN 7:27](https://ref.ly/Dan7:27)** *He shares the kingdom with God's people.* *See also* [DAN 7:18](https://ref.ly/Dan7:18) *“saints of the Most High” have sometimes been interpreted as angels*

Son of Man as a title for Jesus Christ
--------------------------------------

### Used by Jesus Christ to emphasise his humanity and authority

**[MRK 2:10–2:11](https://ref.ly/Mark2:10-Mark2:11)** parallels [MAT 9:6](https://ref.ly/Matt9:6), [LUK 5:24](https://ref.ly/Luke5:24)**[MRK 8:31](https://ref.ly/Mark8:31)** parallel [LUK 9:22](https://ref.ly/Luke9:22)

### The Son of Man receives God's kingdom

**[ACT 7:56](https://ref.ly/Acts7:56)** *See also* [DAN 7:13](https://ref.ly/Dan7:13); [MRK 14:62](https://ref.ly/Mark14:62) parallels [MAT 26:64](https://ref.ly/Matt26:64), [LUK 22:69](https://ref.ly/Luke22:69); [HEB 2:6–2:9](https://ref.ly/Heb2:6-Heb2:9); [PSA 8:4–8:6](https://ref.ly/Ps8:4-Ps8:6)

* **Associated Passages:** Psalms 115:16; Psalms 11:4; Psalms 33:13-14; Psalms 45:2; Psalms 8:4; Psalms 36:7; Psalms 80:17; Psalms 107:8; Psalms 107:15; Psalms 107:21; Psalms 107:31; Ecclesiastes 9:3; Ecclesiastes 3:18-19; Ezekiel 31:14; Psalms 146:3; Psalms 14:2-3; Psalms 53:2-3; Micah 5:7; Genesis 4:1-2; Genesis 5:3-4; Ezekiel 2:1; Ezekiel 2:3; Ezekiel 2:6; Ezekiel 2:8; Ezekiel 3:1; Job 25:6; Daniel 8:17; Daniel 7:13; Daniel 7:13-14; Daniel 7:27; Daniel 7:18; Mark 2:10-11; Matthew 9:6; Luke 5:24; Mark 8:31; Luke 9:22; Acts 7:56; Mark 14:62; Matthew 26:64; Luke 22:69; Hebrews 2:6-9; Psalms 8:4-6

## 2303: Jesus Christ, as creator (id: 2303)

Scripture identifies the pre\-existent Jesus Christ as involved in the work of creation, and relates this to his work in redemption, by which a new creation is brought out of the ruins of the old.

Jesus Christ's creation of the present world
--------------------------------------------

### Jesus Christ created all things

**[JHN 1:3](https://ref.ly/John1:3)** *See also* [JHN 1:10](https://ref.ly/John1:10); [ACT 3:15](https://ref.ly/Acts3:15); [1CO 8:6](https://ref.ly/1Cor8:6); [COL 1:15–1:16](https://ref.ly/Col1:15-Col1:16); [HEB 1:2](https://ref.ly/Heb1:2)

### Jesus Christ sustains the created universe

**[HEB 1:3](https://ref.ly/Heb1:3)** *See also* [1CO 8:6](https://ref.ly/1Cor8:6); [COL 1:17](https://ref.ly/Col1:17); [REV 3:14](https://ref.ly/Rev3:14) *The word translated “ruler” can mean either “beginning” or “first in rank”.*

### Jesus Christ will bring the entire work of creation to perfection

**[EPH 1:9–1:10](https://ref.ly/Eph1:9-Eph1:10)** *See also* [ROM 8:19–8:22](https://ref.ly/Rom8:19-Rom8:22); [COL 1:20](https://ref.ly/Col1:20)

Jesus Christ makes a new creation possible
------------------------------------------

### Jesus Christ recreates people through a new birth

**[2CO 5:17](https://ref.ly/2Cor5:17)** *See also* [JHN 1:12–1:13](https://ref.ly/John1:12-John1:13), [JHN 3:5–3:6](https://ref.ly/John3:5-John3:6); [GAL 6:15](https://ref.ly/Gal6:15); [JAS 1:18](https://ref.ly/Jas1:18)

### Jesus Christ's work of new creation should be evident in believers' lives

**[EPH 4:24](https://ref.ly/Eph4:24)** *See also* [EPH 3:15](https://ref.ly/Eph3:15); [COL 3:10](https://ref.ly/Col3:10)

### Through Jesus Christ a new heaven and earth will be created

**[2PE 3:13](https://ref.ly/2Pet3:13)** *The promise was given in [Isa 65:17](https://ref.ly/Isa65:17); [66:22](https://ref.ly/Isa66:22).* *See also* [REV 21:1](https://ref.ly/Rev21:1), [REV 21:4–21:5](https://ref.ly/Rev21:4-Rev21:5)

## 2306: Jesus Christ, as high priest (id: 2306)

Jesus Christ, being a truly human high priest, perfectly represents humanity before God. He made atonement for sins by his own sacrificial death. Being a truly divine high priest, this act of Christ's was perfect, once for all and of eternal value.

The ministry of Jesus Christ as high priest
-------------------------------------------

### He made atonement for sin

**[HEB 2:17](https://ref.ly/Heb2:17)** *See also* [HEB 8:3](https://ref.ly/Heb8:3), [HEB 9:7](https://ref.ly/Heb9:7), [HEB 9:11–9:12](https://ref.ly/Heb9:11-Heb9:12), [HEB 13:11–13:13](https://ref.ly/Heb13:11-Heb13:13)

### He represents human beings before God

**[HEB 5:1](https://ref.ly/Heb5:1)** *See also* [ROM 8:34](https://ref.ly/Rom8:34); [1JN 2:1–2:2](https://ref.ly/1John2:1-1John2:2)

### He entered the Most Holy Place

**[HEB 9:24](https://ref.ly/Heb9:24)** *On the Day of Atonement the high priest entered the Most Holy Place (the sanctuary) which represented the presence of God. Jesus Christ fulfilled this ritual by entering heaven.* *See also* [HEB 4:14](https://ref.ly/Heb4:14), [HEB 6:19–6:20](https://ref.ly/Heb6:19-Heb6:20), [HEB 9:7](https://ref.ly/Heb9:7), [HEB 9:12](https://ref.ly/Heb9:12)

### He makes believers perfect

**[HEB 10:14](https://ref.ly/Heb10:14)** *See also* [HEB 10:10](https://ref.ly/Heb10:10), [HEB 13:12](https://ref.ly/Heb13:12)

### He brings believers close to God

**[HEB 10:19–10:22](https://ref.ly/Heb10:19-Heb10:22)**

### He helps those being tempted

**[HEB 2:18](https://ref.ly/Heb2:18)** *See also* [HEB 4:15](https://ref.ly/Heb4:15), [HEB 5:2](https://ref.ly/Heb5:2)

### He intercedes continually

**[HEB 7:24–7:25](https://ref.ly/Heb7:24-Heb7:25)** *See also* [JHN 17:20](https://ref.ly/John17:20); [ROM 8:34](https://ref.ly/Rom8:34)

Jesus Christ, the human high priest
-----------------------------------

### As a man he is able to represent human beings

**[HEB 2:17](https://ref.ly/Heb2:17)** *See also* [HEB 5:1](https://ref.ly/Heb5:1)

### He is divinely appointed

**[HEB 5:5–5:6](https://ref.ly/Heb5:5-Heb5:6)** *See also* [HEB 3:1–3:2](https://ref.ly/Heb3:1-Heb3:2)

Jesus Christ, the divine high priest
------------------------------------

### He is sinless

**[HEB 7:26–7:27](https://ref.ly/Heb7:26-Heb7:27)** *Jesus Christ is strongly contrasted with other high priests because he did not have to offer sacrifices for his own sins.*

### He is eternal

**[HEB 6:20](https://ref.ly/Heb6:20)** *See also* [HEB 5:6](https://ref.ly/Heb5:6), [HEB 7:17](https://ref.ly/Heb7:17), [HEB 7:21](https://ref.ly/Heb7:21), [HEB 7:28](https://ref.ly/Heb7:28)

### His atoning work was completed once for all

**[HEB 7:27](https://ref.ly/Heb7:27)** *Other high priests had to repeat their sacrifices.* *See also* [HEB 9:12](https://ref.ly/Heb9:12), [HEB 9:25–9:26](https://ref.ly/Heb9:25-Heb9:26), [HEB 9:28](https://ref.ly/Heb9:28), [HEB 10:10](https://ref.ly/Heb10:10)

### He is exalted

**[HEB 8:1](https://ref.ly/Heb8:1)** *See also* [ZEC 6:13](https://ref.ly/Zech6:13); [HEB 7:26](https://ref.ly/Heb7:26)

Jesus Christ's high priesthood was of the order of Melchizedek
--------------------------------------------------------------

**[HEB 6:20](https://ref.ly/Heb6:20)** *The priesthood of Melchizedek resembles that of Jesus Christ because he too was king and had neither beginning nor end.* *See also* [PSA 110:4](https://ref.ly/Ps110:4); [HEB 5:6](https://ref.ly/Heb5:6), [HEB 5:10](https://ref.ly/Heb5:10), [HEB 7:1–7:4](https://ref.ly/Heb7:1-Heb7:4), [HEB 7:14–7:17](https://ref.ly/Heb7:14-Heb7:17)

Responses to Jesus Christ's high priesthood
-------------------------------------------

[HEB 4:14–4:15](https://ref.ly/Heb4:14-Heb4:15) *a call to keep to the faith*; ; [HEB 4:16](https://ref.ly/Heb4:16) *an invitation to seek God's help in times of need*; ; [HEB 10:19–10:22](https://ref.ly/Heb10:19-Heb10:22) *an invitation to draw near to God*; ; [HEB 12:1–12:3](https://ref.ly/Heb12:1-Heb12:3) *a call to run the race of faith*; ; [HEB 12:28–12:29](https://ref.ly/Heb12:28-Heb12:29) *a call to offer thanksgiving and worship*

* **Associated Passages:** Hebrews 2:17; Hebrews 8:3; Hebrews 9:7; Hebrews 9:11-12; Hebrews 13:11-13; Hebrews 5:1; Romans 8:34; 1 John 2:1-2; Hebrews 9:24; Hebrews 4:14; Hebrews 6:19-20; Hebrews 9:12; Hebrews 10:14; Hebrews 10:10; Hebrews 13:12; Hebrews 10:19-22; Hebrews 2:18; Hebrews 4:15; Hebrews 5:2; Hebrews 7:24-25; John 17:20; Hebrews 5:5-6; Hebrews 3:1-2; Hebrews 7:26-27; Hebrews 6:20; Hebrews 5:6; Hebrews 7:17; Hebrews 7:21; Hebrews 7:28; Hebrews 7:27; Hebrews 9:25-26; Hebrews 9:28; Hebrews 8:1; Zechariah 6:13; Hebrews 7:26; Psalms 110:4; Hebrews 5:10; Hebrews 7:1-4; Hebrews 7:14-17; Hebrews 4:14-15; Hebrews 4:16; Hebrews 12:1-3; Hebrews 12:28-29
* **Associated Articles:** 2075: Jesus Christ, sinlessness of (ID: `2075@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2410: cross, the (ID: `2410@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6606: access to God (ID: `6606@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6614: atonement (ID: `6614@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6684: mediator (ID: `6684@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6689: mercy, of Jesus Christ (ID: `6689@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6712: propitiation (ID: `6712@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 7308: Atonement, Day of (ID: `7308@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 7378: high priest, in NT (ID: `7378@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 7396: Most Holy Place (ID: `7396@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 7414: priesthood, in NT (ID: `7414@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 7436: sacrifice, NT fulfilment of (ID: `7436@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 2309: Jesus Christ, as judge (id: 2309)

Jesus Christ executed judgment against the forces of evil through his death on the cross. Individuals will be judged according to their response to his saving grace.

Jesus Christ is appointed judge by God the Father
-------------------------------------------------

**[JHN 5:22](https://ref.ly/John5:22)** *See also* [JHN 5:27](https://ref.ly/John5:27); [ACT 10:42](https://ref.ly/Acts10:42), [ACT 17:31](https://ref.ly/Acts17:31)

Jesus Christ is a just judge
----------------------------

**[JHN 5:30](https://ref.ly/John5:30)** *See also* [ISA 11:3–11:4](https://ref.ly/Isa11:3-Isa11:4); [MIC 4:3](https://ref.ly/Mic4:3); [JHN 8:15–8:16](https://ref.ly/John8:15-John8:16); [ACT 17:31](https://ref.ly/Acts17:31); [REV 19:11](https://ref.ly/Rev19:11)

Jesus Christ's death brought judgment on Satan and evil world powers
--------------------------------------------------------------------

**[JHN 12:31–12:33](https://ref.ly/John12:31-John12:33)** *See also* [JHN 16:11](https://ref.ly/John16:11)

Jesus Christ will act as judge at the end of time
-------------------------------------------------

**[2TI 4:1](https://ref.ly/2Tim4:1)** *See also* [MAT 25:31–25:32](https://ref.ly/Matt25:31-Matt25:32); [ROM 2:16](https://ref.ly/Rom2:16); [2TH 1:7–1:10](https://ref.ly/2Thess1:7-2Thess1:10); [2TI 4:8](https://ref.ly/2Tim4:8); [REV 19:11–19:16](https://ref.ly/Rev19:11-Rev19:16), [REV 22:12](https://ref.ly/Rev22:12)

People will be judged according to their response to Jesus Christ
-----------------------------------------------------------------

**[JHN 3:18](https://ref.ly/John3:18)** *See also* [MAT 10:32–10:33](https://ref.ly/Matt10:32-Matt10:33) parallel [LUK 12:8–12:9](https://ref.ly/Luke12:8-Luke12:9); [MRK 8:38](https://ref.ly/Mark8:38) parallel [LUK 9:26](https://ref.ly/Luke9:26); [JHN 9:39](https://ref.ly/John9:39), [JHN 12:48](https://ref.ly/John12:48)

Jesus Christ's teaching on judgment
-----------------------------------

### Jesus Christ will separate the righteous from the unrighteous

**[MAT 25:31–25:32](https://ref.ly/Matt25:31-Matt25:32)** *See also* [MAT 3:12](https://ref.ly/Matt3:12), [MAT 13:24–13:30](https://ref.ly/Matt13:24-Matt13:30), [MAT 13:36–13:42](https://ref.ly/Matt13:36-Matt13:42) *the parable of the weeds*; [MAT 13:47–13:50](https://ref.ly/Matt13:47-Matt13:50) *the parable of the net*; [MAT 25:33–25:46](https://ref.ly/Matt25:33-Matt25:46) *the parable of the sheep and the goats*

### Those who reject Jesus Christ will be punished

[DAN 2:34–2:35](https://ref.ly/Dan2:34-Dan2:35); ; [MAT 21:33–21:44](https://ref.ly/Matt21:33-Matt21:44) parallels [MRK 12:1–12:11](https://ref.ly/Mark12:1-Mark12:11), [LUK 20:9–20:18](https://ref.ly/Luke20:9-Luke20:18) *the parable of the tenants*

### Christians will stand before Jesus Christ as judge and be rewarded for what they have done

**[MAT 16:27](https://ref.ly/Matt16:27)** *See also* [MAT 25:14–25:30](https://ref.ly/Matt25:14-Matt25:30) *the parable of the talents*; [LUK 19:12–19:27](https://ref.ly/Luke19:12-Luke19:27) *the parable of the ten minas*; [2CO 5:10](https://ref.ly/2Cor5:10)

### The day of Jesus Christ's return as judge is unknown

**[MRK 13:32–13:36](https://ref.ly/Mark13:32-Mark13:36)** *See also* [MAT 24:36–24:44](https://ref.ly/Matt24:36-Matt24:44) parallel [LUK 17:26–17:37](https://ref.ly/Luke17:26-Luke17:37); [MAT 25:1–25:13](https://ref.ly/Matt25:1-Matt25:13) *the parable of the ten virgins*

* **Associated Passages:** John 5:22; John 5:27; Acts 10:42; Acts 17:31; John 5:30; Isaiah 11:3-4; Micah 4:3; John 8:15-16; Revelation 19:11; John 12:31-33; John 16:11; 2 Timothy 4:1; Matthew 25:31-32; Romans 2:16; 2 Thessalonians 1:7-10; 2 Timothy 4:8; Revelation 19:11-16; Revelation 22:12; John 3:18; Matthew 10:32-33; Luke 12:8-9; Mark 8:38; Luke 9:26; John 9:39; John 12:48; Matthew 3:12; Matthew 13:24-30; Matthew 13:36-42; Matthew 13:47-50; Matthew 25:33-46; Daniel 2:34-35; Matthew 21:33-44; Mark 12:1-11; Luke 20:9-18; Matthew 16:27; Matthew 25:14-30; Luke 19:12-27; 2 Corinthians 5:10; Mark 13:32-36; Matthew 24:36-44; Luke 17:26-37; Matthew 25:1-13

## 2312: Jesus Christ, as king (id: 2312)

Jesus Christ is declared king at his birth: he descends from the royal line of David. People rejected his kingly claims at his crucifixion but God exalted him to his rightful place of power and majesty. At the end of time Jesus Christ will rule the nations for ever.

Jesus Christ descends from the royal line of David
--------------------------------------------------

### He was the Son of David

**[MAT 1:1](https://ref.ly/Matt1:1)** *The Messiah was expected to come from David's line. The genealogy given by Matthew follows the royal line of the kings descended from David.* *See also* [MAT 9:27](https://ref.ly/Matt9:27), [MAT 12:23](https://ref.ly/Matt12:23), [MAT 15:22](https://ref.ly/Matt15:22); [LUK 1:32–1:33](https://ref.ly/Luke1:32-Luke1:33), [LUK 2:4](https://ref.ly/Luke2:4), [LUK 3:31](https://ref.ly/Luke3:31)

### He was born in Bethlehem, the town of David

**[JHN 7:42](https://ref.ly/John7:42)** *See also* [MAT 2:3–2:6](https://ref.ly/Matt2:3-Matt2:6); [MIC 5:2](https://ref.ly/Mic5:2); [LUK 2:15–2:16](https://ref.ly/Luke2:15-Luke2:16)

Jesus Christ is regarded as king
--------------------------------

**[JHN 1:49](https://ref.ly/John1:49)** *By Nathanael.* *See also* [MAT 2:1–2:2](https://ref.ly/Matt2:1-Matt2:2) *by the Magi*; [JHN 6:15](https://ref.ly/John6:15) *by the crowds*; [ACT 17:7](https://ref.ly/Acts17:7) *by Jason of Thessalonica*

Jesus Christ refused worldly kingdoms
-------------------------------------

**[JHN 18:36](https://ref.ly/John18:36)** *See also* [MAT 4:8–4:10](https://ref.ly/Matt4:8-Matt4:10) parallel [LUK 4:5–4:8](https://ref.ly/Luke4:5-Luke4:8); [JHN 6:15](https://ref.ly/John6:15)

Jesus Christ entered Jerusalem as a king
----------------------------------------

**[MAT 21:1–21:9](https://ref.ly/Matt21:1-Matt21:9)** parallel [JHN 12:12–12:15](https://ref.ly/John12:12-John12:15) *See also* [ZEC 9:9](https://ref.ly/Zech9:9)

Jesus Christ's kingship is an issue at his trial
------------------------------------------------

### Pilate questions Jesus Christ

**[LUK 23:2–23:3](https://ref.ly/Luke23:2-Luke23:3)** parallels [MAT 27:11](https://ref.ly/Matt27:11), [MRK 15:2](https://ref.ly/Mark15:2), [JHN 18:33](https://ref.ly/John18:33) *Pilate's first words to Jesus Christ are the same in all the Gospels.*

### Jesus Christ claims to be a spiritual king

**[JHN 18:36–18:37](https://ref.ly/John18:36-John18:37)** *See also* [MAT 27:11](https://ref.ly/Matt27:11) parallels [MRK 15:2](https://ref.ly/Mark15:2), [LUK 23:3](https://ref.ly/Luke23:3)

### Pilate appeals to the crowd to accept Jesus Christ as their king

**[MRK 15:9](https://ref.ly/Mark15:9)**

### The crowd reject Jesus Christ as king

**[MRK 15:12–15:13](https://ref.ly/Mark15:12-Mark15:13)** *See also* [JHN 19:12–19:15](https://ref.ly/John19:12-John19:15)

### Jesus Christ is mocked as king

**[MAT 27:27–27:30](https://ref.ly/Matt27:27-Matt27:30)** parallels [MRK 15:16–15:20](https://ref.ly/Mark15:16-Mark15:20), [JHN 19:2–19:3](https://ref.ly/John19:2-John19:3)

Jesus Christ is declared king at his crucifixion
------------------------------------------------

**[JHN 19:19–19:22](https://ref.ly/John19:19-John19:22)** parallels [MAT 27:37](https://ref.ly/Matt27:37), [MRK 15:26](https://ref.ly/Mark15:26), [LUK 23:38](https://ref.ly/Luke23:38) *Jesus Christ's claim to be king was the “crime” for which he was executed.*

God has exalted Jesus Christ to his rightful place as king
----------------------------------------------------------

**[HEB 1:3](https://ref.ly/Heb1:3)** *See also* [HEB 8:1](https://ref.ly/Heb8:1), [HEB 12:2](https://ref.ly/Heb12:2); [REV 5:6](https://ref.ly/Rev5:6), [REV 7:17](https://ref.ly/Rev7:17), [REV 22:1–22:3](https://ref.ly/Rev22:1-Rev22:3)

As king, Jesus Christ welcomes believers into his kingdom
---------------------------------------------------------

**[LUK 23:42–23:43](https://ref.ly/Luke23:42-Luke23:43)** *See also* [2TI 4:18](https://ref.ly/2Tim4:18); [REV 3:20–3:21](https://ref.ly/Rev3:20-Rev3:21)

Jesus Christ is king of all kings
---------------------------------

### He will rule over the nations

**[REV 1:5](https://ref.ly/Rev1:5)** *See also* [PSA 2:7–2:9](https://ref.ly/Ps2:7-Ps2:9); [DAN 7:13–7:14](https://ref.ly/Dan7:13-Dan7:14); [MAT 19:28](https://ref.ly/Matt19:28), [MAT 25:31–25:32](https://ref.ly/Matt25:31-Matt25:32); [ROM 15:12](https://ref.ly/Rom15:12); [1CO 15:25](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:25); [PHP 2:9–2:10](https://ref.ly/Phil2:9-Phil2:10); [REV 12:5](https://ref.ly/Rev12:5), [REV 17:14](https://ref.ly/Rev17:14), [REV 19:11–19:16](https://ref.ly/Rev19:11-Rev19:16)

### He is king for ever

**[REV 11:15](https://ref.ly/Rev11:15)** *See also* [ISA 9:7](https://ref.ly/Isa9:7); [LUK 1:33](https://ref.ly/Luke1:33); [HEB 1:8](https://ref.ly/Heb1:8); [PSA 45:6](https://ref.ly/Ps45:6)

* **Associated Passages:** Matthew 1:1; Matthew 9:27; Matthew 12:23; Matthew 15:22; Luke 1:32-33; Luke 2:4; Luke 3:31; John 7:42; Matthew 2:3-6; Micah 5:2; Luke 2:15-16; John 1:49; Matthew 2:1-2; John 6:15; Acts 17:7; John 18:36; Matthew 4:8-10; Luke 4:5-8; Matthew 21:1-9; John 12:12-15; Zechariah 9:9; Luke 23:2-3; Matthew 27:11; Mark 15:2; John 18:33; John 18:36-37; Luke 23:3; Mark 15:9; Mark 15:12-13; John 19:12-15; Matthew 27:27-30; Mark 15:16-20; John 19:2-3; John 19:19-22; Matthew 27:37; Mark 15:26; Luke 23:38; Hebrews 1:3; Hebrews 8:1; Hebrews 12:2; Revelation 5:6; Revelation 7:17; Revelation 22:1-3; Luke 23:42-43; 2 Timothy 4:18; Revelation 3:20-21; Revelation 1:5; Psalms 2:7-9; Daniel 7:13-14; Matthew 19:28; Matthew 25:31-32; Romans 15:12; 1 Corinthians 15:25; Philippians 2:9-10; Revelation 12:5; Revelation 17:14; Revelation 19:11-16; Revelation 11:15; Isaiah 9:7; Luke 1:33; Hebrews 1:8; Psalms 45:6

## 2315: Jesus Christ, as Lamb (id: 2315)

Jesus Christ is referred to as the “Lamb of God”. This symbol points to Christ being a perfect sacrifice for sin. It also conveys his meekness and his willingness to submit to suffering and death.

The imagery of the lamb
-----------------------

### An image of innocence and attraction

**[ISA 11:6](https://ref.ly/Isa11:6)** *See also* [LEV 23:12](https://ref.ly/Lev23:12); [2SA 12:3](https://ref.ly/2Sam12:3)

### An image of submissiveness and vulnerability

**[JER 11:19](https://ref.ly/Jer11:19)** *See also* [ISA 40:11](https://ref.ly/Isa40:11); [LUK 10:3](https://ref.ly/Luke10:3); [JHN 21:15](https://ref.ly/John21:15)

### An image of quiet suffering

**[ISA 53:7](https://ref.ly/Isa53:7)**

### An image of sacrifice

**[EXO 29:38](https://ref.ly/Exod29:38)** *“each day” here refers to the seven\-day period of the consecration of priests.* *See also* [EXO 12:27](https://ref.ly/Exod12:27); [LEV 3:7](https://ref.ly/Lev3:7), [LEV 4:32](https://ref.ly/Lev4:32), [LEV 14:13](https://ref.ly/Lev14:13); [EZK 46:13](https://ref.ly/Ezek46:13); [MRK 14:12](https://ref.ly/Mark14:12) parallel [LUK 22:7](https://ref.ly/Luke22:7)

Jesus Christ is likened to a lamb
---------------------------------

**[JHN 1:36](https://ref.ly/John1:36)** *See also* [JHN 1:29](https://ref.ly/John1:29); [1CO 5:7](https://ref.ly/1Cor5:7); [1PE 1:19](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:19); [REV 5:6](https://ref.ly/Rev5:6)

The symbolism of the lamb applies to Jesus Christ
-------------------------------------------------

### Jesus Christ is innocent and draws people to himself

**[LUK 23:41](https://ref.ly/Luke23:41)** *See also* [JHN 12:32](https://ref.ly/John12:32); [HEB 4:15](https://ref.ly/Heb4:15), [HEB 7:26](https://ref.ly/Heb7:26); [1PE 2:22](https://ref.ly/1Pet2:22); [ISA 53:9](https://ref.ly/Isa53:9)

### Jesus Christ was submissive and vulnerable

**[MAT 26:38–26:39](https://ref.ly/Matt26:38-Matt26:39)** parallels [MRK 14:35–14:36](https://ref.ly/Mark14:35-Mark14:36), [LUK 22:41–22:42](https://ref.ly/Luke22:41-Luke22:42) *See also* [JHN 3:27](https://ref.ly/John3:27); [1CO 1:27](https://ref.ly/1Cor1:27); [PHP 2:7–2:8](https://ref.ly/Phil2:7-Phil2:8); [HEB 4:15](https://ref.ly/Heb4:15)

### Jesus Christ suffered quietly

**[MAT 27:28–27:31](https://ref.ly/Matt27:28-Matt27:31)** parallel [MRK 15:17–15:20](https://ref.ly/Mark15:17-Mark15:20) *See also* [MAT 26:62–26:63](https://ref.ly/Matt26:62-Matt26:63) parallel [MRK 14:60–14:61](https://ref.ly/Mark14:60-Mark14:61); [MAT 27:12–27:14](https://ref.ly/Matt27:12-Matt27:14) parallel [MRK 15:3–15:5](https://ref.ly/Mark15:3-Mark15:5); [LUK 23:8–23:11](https://ref.ly/Luke23:8-Luke23:11); [JHN 19:2–19:3](https://ref.ly/John19:2-John19:3); [ACT 8:32–8:35](https://ref.ly/Acts8:32-Acts8:35); [ISA 53:7–53:8](https://ref.ly/Isa53:7-Isa53:8); [1PE 2:23](https://ref.ly/1Pet2:23)

### Jesus Christ is seen as a sacrifice

## 2318: Jesus Christ, as prophet (id: 2318)

Jesus Christ was acclaimed as a prophet by those who witnessed his miracles and heard his teaching. They recognised him as a bearer of the word of God, who spoke with authority concerning the nature and purposes of God.

Examples of those who recognised Jesus Christ as a prophet
----------------------------------------------------------

### People anticipating the coming prophet

**[JHN 6:14](https://ref.ly/John6:14)** *The reference is to the promised prophet, who, like Moses, would see God face to face (see [Dt 18:15,18](https://ref.ly/Deut18:15,Deut18:18)).* *See also* [JHN 1:21](https://ref.ly/John1:21), [JHN 7:40](https://ref.ly/John7:40), [JHN 7:52](https://ref.ly/John7:52)

### A Samaritan woman

[JHN 4:17–4:19](https://ref.ly/John4:17-John4:19)

### Witnesses of Jesus Christ's miracles

[MAT 14:1–14:5](https://ref.ly/Matt14:1-Matt14:5) parallel [MRK 6:14–6:15](https://ref.ly/Mark6:14-Mark6:15); ; [MAT 16:13–16:14](https://ref.ly/Matt16:13-Matt16:14) parallels [MRK 8:27–8:28](https://ref.ly/Mark8:27-Mark8:28), [LUK 9:18–9:19](https://ref.ly/Luke9:18-Luke9:19)

### The crowd as Jesus Christ approached Jerusalem

[MAT 21:10–21:11](https://ref.ly/Matt21:10-Matt21:11), [MAT 21:46](https://ref.ly/Matt21:46)

### Two of Jesus Christ's disciples after his death

[LUK 24:19](https://ref.ly/Luke24:19)

### The apostles Peter and Stephen

[ACT 3:20–3:23](https://ref.ly/Acts3:20-Acts3:23), [ACT 7:37](https://ref.ly/Acts7:37); ; [DEU 18:15–18:18](https://ref.ly/Deut18:15-Deut18:18)

Indications of Jesus Christ being a prophet
-------------------------------------------

### He announced coming blessing from God

**[JHN 7:37–7:40](https://ref.ly/John7:37-John7:40)** *See also* [MAT 5:3–5:12](https://ref.ly/Matt5:3-Matt5:12) parallel [LUK 6:20–6:23](https://ref.ly/Luke6:20-Luke6:23); [MAT 13:16–13:17](https://ref.ly/Matt13:16-Matt13:17) parallel [LUK 10:23–10:24](https://ref.ly/Luke10:23-Luke10:24); [JHN 20:19–20:21](https://ref.ly/John20:19-John20:21), [JHN 20:29](https://ref.ly/John20:29)

### He announced coming judgment and woe

**[ACT 3:23](https://ref.ly/Acts3:23)** *See also* [MAT 11:20–11:24](https://ref.ly/Matt11:20-Matt11:24) parallel [LUK 10:13–10:15](https://ref.ly/Luke10:13-Luke10:15); [MAT 23:13–23:39](https://ref.ly/Matt23:13-Matt23:39); [LUK 6:24–6:26](https://ref.ly/Luke6:24-Luke6:26)

### He possessed supernatural knowledge and insight

**[JHN 2:24–2:25](https://ref.ly/John2:24-John2:25)** *See also* [MAT 9:4](https://ref.ly/Matt9:4) parallels [MRK 2:8](https://ref.ly/Mark2:8), [LUK 5:22](https://ref.ly/Luke5:22); [LUK 7:39–7:43](https://ref.ly/Luke7:39-Luke7:43), [LUK 9:47](https://ref.ly/Luke9:47); [JHN 4:16–4:19](https://ref.ly/John4:16-John4:19)

### He performed mighty works and miracles

[LUK 7:12–7:17](https://ref.ly/Luke7:12-Luke7:17); ; [JHN 9:17](https://ref.ly/John9:17)

--------------------------------------------------------

[MRK 1:22](https://ref.ly/Mark1:22), [MRK 3:28](https://ref.ly/Mark3:28); ; [JHN 7:16](https://ref.ly/John7:16), [JHN 14:10](https://ref.ly/John14:10)

The place of Jesus Christ in relation to other prophets
-------------------------------------------------------

## 2321: Jesus Christ, as redeemer (id: 2321)

Jesus Christ redeems believers from all forms of sinful bondage and oppression through his death and resurrection. The price of that redemption, his own death, represents a ransom paid to secure the freedom of those held in bondage to sin.

The incarnate God as redeemer
-----------------------------

### God as redeemer

**[ISA 63:16](https://ref.ly/Isa63:16)** *See also* [JOB 19:25](https://ref.ly/Job19:25); [ISA 49:26](https://ref.ly/Isa49:26), [ISA 59:20](https://ref.ly/Isa59:20); [LUK 1:68–1:75](https://ref.ly/Luke1:68-Luke1:75)

### Jesus Christ as redeemer

**[1CO 1:30](https://ref.ly/1Cor1:30)**

Forms of bondage from which Jesus Christ redeems believers
----------------------------------------------------------

### Jesus Christ redeems from slavery to sin

**[REV 1:5](https://ref.ly/Rev1:5)** *See also* [PSA 130:8](https://ref.ly/Ps130:8); [ROM 3:23–3:24](https://ref.ly/Rom3:23-Rom3:24), [ROM 6:18](https://ref.ly/Rom6:18), [ROM 6:22](https://ref.ly/Rom6:22); [TIT 2:14](https://ref.ly/Titus2:14), [TIT 3:3–3:5](https://ref.ly/Titus3:3-Titus3:5); [1PE 3:18](https://ref.ly/1Pet3:18)

### Jesus Christ redeems from the curse of the law

**[GAL 3:13](https://ref.ly/Gal3:13)** *See also* [GAL 4:4–4:5](https://ref.ly/Gal4:4-Gal4:5)

### Jesus Christ redeems from empty religion

**[1PE 1:18](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:18)** *See also* [GAL 4:3](https://ref.ly/Gal4:3); [COL 2:20](https://ref.ly/Col2:20); [HEB 9:14](https://ref.ly/Heb9:14)

### Jesus Christ redeems from the power of Satan

**[COL 1:13](https://ref.ly/Col1:13)** *See also* [ACT 26:18](https://ref.ly/Acts26:18); [GAL 1:4](https://ref.ly/Gal1:4)

### Jesus Christ redeems from the coming judgment

**[1TH 1:10](https://ref.ly/1Thess1:10)** *See also* [ROM 5:9](https://ref.ly/Rom5:9), [ROM 8:1–8:2](https://ref.ly/Rom8:1-Rom8:2); [1TH 5:9](https://ref.ly/1Thess5:9)

### Jesus Christ redeems from death

**[HEB 2:14–2:15](https://ref.ly/Heb2:14-Heb2:15)** *See also* [HOS 13:14](https://ref.ly/Hos13:14); [1CO 15:54–15:57](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:54-1Cor15:57)

------------------------------------------------------

### Redemption comes through the incarnation of Jesus Christ

**[GAL 4:4–4:5](https://ref.ly/Gal4:4-Gal4:5)** *See also* [ROM 8:3](https://ref.ly/Rom8:3); [HEB 2:14](https://ref.ly/Heb2:14)

### Jesus Christ redeems by paying a ransom

**[MAT 20:28](https://ref.ly/Matt20:28)** parallel [MRK 10:45](https://ref.ly/Mark10:45) *See also* [ACT 20:28](https://ref.ly/Acts20:28); [HEB 9:15](https://ref.ly/Heb9:15); [REV 5:9](https://ref.ly/Rev5:9)

-----------------------------------------------------

## 2324: Jesus Christ, as Saviour (id: 2324)

God's work of salvation is accomplished supremely through the cross and resurrection of Jesus Christ. Through faith, the believer is able to share in all the saving benefits won by Jesus Christ through his obedience to God.

Jesus Christ is the Saviour
---------------------------

### Jesus Christ is called Saviour

**[TIT 1:4](https://ref.ly/Titus1:4)** *See also* [LUK 2:11](https://ref.ly/Luke2:11); [TIT 3:6](https://ref.ly/Titus3:6); [2PE 1:1](https://ref.ly/2Pet1:1), [2PE 3:2](https://ref.ly/2Pet3:2), [2PE 3:18](https://ref.ly/2Pet3:18)

### Jesus Christ is the promised Saviour

**[ACT 13:23](https://ref.ly/Acts13:23)** *See also* [LUK 1:69–1:75](https://ref.ly/Luke1:69-Luke1:75), [LUK 2:28–2:30](https://ref.ly/Luke2:28-Luke2:30)

### Jesus Christ's purpose is to save

**[LUK 19:10](https://ref.ly/Luke19:10)** *See also* [MAT 1:21](https://ref.ly/Matt1:21); [1TI 1:15](https://ref.ly/1Tim1:15)

Jesus Christ's qualities as Saviour
-----------------------------------

### Jesus Christ is the unique Saviour

**[ACT 4:12](https://ref.ly/Acts4:12)** *See also* [JHN 6:68–6:69](https://ref.ly/John6:68-John6:69), [JHN 10:9](https://ref.ly/John10:9), [JHN 14:6](https://ref.ly/John14:6); [ACT 10:42–10:43](https://ref.ly/Acts10:42-Acts10:43)

**[HEB 7:25](https://ref.ly/Heb7:25)** *See also* [JHN 19:30](https://ref.ly/John19:30); [PHP 3:21](https://ref.ly/Phil3:21); [COL 1:19–1:20](https://ref.ly/Col1:19-Col1:20); [HEB 5:9](https://ref.ly/Heb5:9), [HEB 9:26–9:28](https://ref.ly/Heb9:26-Heb9:28); [1JN 1:9](https://ref.ly/1John1:9); [JUD 1:24](https://ref.ly/Jude1:24)

**[JHN 4:42](https://ref.ly/John4:42)** *See also* [LUK 2:30–2:32](https://ref.ly/Luke2:30-Luke2:32); [1TI 2:5–2:6](https://ref.ly/1Tim2:5-1Tim2:6), [1TI 4:10](https://ref.ly/1Tim4:10); [1JN 4:14](https://ref.ly/1John4:14)

**[2TI 1:10](https://ref.ly/2Tim1:10)** *See also* [1CO 15:55–15:57](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:55-1Cor15:57); [HEB 2:15](https://ref.ly/Heb2:15); [REV 20:6](https://ref.ly/Rev20:6), [REV 21:4](https://ref.ly/Rev21:4)

### Jesus Christ saves from Satan's power

### Jesus Christ saves so that people may live for God

**[1JN 4:9](https://ref.ly/1John4:9)** *See also* [ROM 6:8–6:11](https://ref.ly/Rom6:8-Rom6:11), [ROM 7:21–7:25](https://ref.ly/Rom7:21-Rom7:25); [GAL 2:20](https://ref.ly/Gal2:20); [2TI 1:9](https://ref.ly/2Tim1:9); [HEB 9:14–9:15](https://ref.ly/Heb9:14-Heb9:15); [1PE 2:24](https://ref.ly/1Pet2:24); [1JN 3:5–3:6](https://ref.ly/1John3:5-1John3:6), [1JN 5:18](https://ref.ly/1John5:18)

## 2327: Jesus Christ, as servant (id: 2327)

Jesus Christ laid aside his majesty in order to serve humanity. His death is the supreme example of his servanthood: the fulfilling of the will of God his Father.

The prophets speak of the Messiah as a servant
----------------------------------------------

**[MAT 12:17–12:21](https://ref.ly/Matt12:17-Matt12:21)** *See also* [ISA 42:1–42:4](https://ref.ly/Isa42:1-Isa42:4), [ISA 49:1–49:7](https://ref.ly/Isa49:1-Isa49:7), [ISA 50:4–50:9](https://ref.ly/Isa50:4-Isa50:9), [ISA 52:13–53:12](https://ref.ly/Isa52:13-Isa53:12); [EZK 34:23–34:24](https://ref.ly/Ezek34:23-Ezek34:24), [EZK 37:24–37:25](https://ref.ly/Ezek37:24-Ezek37:25); [ZEC 3:8](https://ref.ly/Zech3:8)

Jesus Christ describes himself as a servant
-------------------------------------------

**[LUK 22:27](https://ref.ly/Luke22:27)** *See also* [MAT 20:28](https://ref.ly/Matt20:28) parallel [MRK 10:45](https://ref.ly/Mark10:45)

Jesus Christ acts as a servant
------------------------------

### By coming to dwell among humanity as a man

**[PHP 2:6–2:7](https://ref.ly/Phil2:6-Phil2:7)** *See also* [2CO 8:9](https://ref.ly/2Cor8:9)

### By obeying God's will

**[JHN 4:34](https://ref.ly/John4:34)** *See also* [JHN 5:30](https://ref.ly/John5:30), [JHN 6:38](https://ref.ly/John6:38), [JHN 14:31](https://ref.ly/John14:31); [HEB 10:5–10:7](https://ref.ly/Heb10:5-Heb10:7); [PSA 40:6–40:8](https://ref.ly/Ps40:6-Ps40:8)

### By ministering to his disciples

[JHN 13:1–13:17](https://ref.ly/John13:1-John13:17)

### By dying on the cross

**[MAT 20:28](https://ref.ly/Matt20:28)** parallel [MRK 10:45](https://ref.ly/Mark10:45) *See also* [MAT 26:39](https://ref.ly/Matt26:39) parallels [MRK 14:36](https://ref.ly/Mark14:36), [LUK 22:42](https://ref.ly/Luke22:42); [PHP 2:8](https://ref.ly/Phil2:8)

The exaltation of Jesus Christ the servant
------------------------------------------

### He will complete his task

[JHN 17:4](https://ref.ly/John17:4), [JHN 19:30](https://ref.ly/John19:30)

### He will be exalted by God

**[ACT 3:13](https://ref.ly/Acts3:13)** *See also* [ISA 52:13](https://ref.ly/Isa52:13); [ACT 3:26](https://ref.ly/Acts3:26); [PHP 2:9–2:11](https://ref.ly/Phil2:9-Phil2:11)

Jesus Christ's obedience and servanthood an example to believers
----------------------------------------------------------------

**[JHN 13:14–13:15](https://ref.ly/John13:14-John13:15)** *See also* [PHP 2:5](https://ref.ly/Phil2:5); [1PE 2:21](https://ref.ly/1Pet2:21)

* **Associated Passages:** Matthew 12:17-21; Isaiah 42:1-4; Isaiah 49:1-7; Isaiah 50:4-9; Isaiah 52:13-53:12; Ezekiel 34:23-24; Ezekiel 37:24-25; Zechariah 3:8; Luke 22:27; Matthew 20:28; Mark 10:45; Philippians 2:6-7; 2 Corinthians 8:9; John 4:34; John 5:30; John 6:38; John 14:31; Hebrews 10:5-7; Psalms 40:6-8; John 13:1-17; Matthew 26:39; Mark 14:36; Luke 22:42; Philippians 2:8; John 17:4; John 19:30; Acts 3:13; Isaiah 52:13; Acts 3:26; Philippians 2:9-11; John 13:14-15; Philippians 2:5; 1 Peter 2:21

## 2330: Jesus Christ, as shepherd (id: 2330)

A title for Jesus Christ indicating believers' dependence on him as he protects, tends and guides those whom he knows intimately.

Prophecies about the shepherd Messiah
-------------------------------------

**[EZK 34:23](https://ref.ly/Ezek34:23)** *See also* [EZK 37:24](https://ref.ly/Ezek37:24); [MIC 5:2](https://ref.ly/Mic5:2); [MAT 2:6](https://ref.ly/Matt2:6); [MIC 5:4](https://ref.ly/Mic5:4); [ZEC 13:7](https://ref.ly/Zech13:7); [MAT 26:31](https://ref.ly/Matt26:31) parallel [MRK 14:27](https://ref.ly/Mark14:27)

Jesus Christ's role as the good shepherd
----------------------------------------

### He has compassion for the helpless

**[MAT 9:36](https://ref.ly/Matt9:36)** *See also* [MRK 6:34](https://ref.ly/Mark6:34); [JHN 11:52](https://ref.ly/John11:52)

### He seeks lost sheep

**[MAT 18:12–18:14](https://ref.ly/Matt18:12-Matt18:14)** parallel [LUK 15:3–15:7](https://ref.ly/Luke15:3-Luke15:7) *See also* [MAT 10:6](https://ref.ly/Matt10:6), [MAT 15:24](https://ref.ly/Matt15:24); [LUK 19:10](https://ref.ly/Luke19:10); [JHN 10:16](https://ref.ly/John10:16)

### He knows his own sheep

**[JHN 10:14–10:15](https://ref.ly/John10:14-John10:15)** *See also* [MAT 25:32](https://ref.ly/Matt25:32); [JHN 10:27](https://ref.ly/John10:27)

### His sheep know his voice

**[JHN 10:4](https://ref.ly/John10:4)** *See also* [JHN 10:3](https://ref.ly/John10:3), [JHN 10:5](https://ref.ly/John10:5), [JHN 10:16](https://ref.ly/John10:16), [JHN 10:27](https://ref.ly/John10:27)

### He provides for and protects his sheep

**[JHN 10:9](https://ref.ly/John10:9)** *See also* [JHN 10:28](https://ref.ly/John10:28)

### He lays down his life for his sheep

**[JHN 10:11](https://ref.ly/John10:11)** *See also* [MAT 26:31](https://ref.ly/Matt26:31) parallel [MRK 14:27](https://ref.ly/Mark14:27); [JHN 10:14–10:15](https://ref.ly/John10:14-John10:15), [JHN 10:17–10:18](https://ref.ly/John10:17-John10:18)

### He judges the sheep

[MAT 25:32–25:46](https://ref.ly/Matt25:32-Matt25:46)

--------------------------------

### Christians are Jesus Christ's flock

**[LUK 12:32](https://ref.ly/Luke12:32)** *See also* [MAT 10:16](https://ref.ly/Matt10:16); [JHN 10:16](https://ref.ly/John10:16); [ACT 20:29](https://ref.ly/Acts20:29); [ROM 8:36](https://ref.ly/Rom8:36)

---------------------------------------

## 2333: Jesus Christ, attitude to OT (id: 2333)

Jesus Christ's teaching was based largely on the OT, which he treated as God's inspired and authoritative word, but which he had the authority to interpret.

Jesus Christ recognises the OT as Scripture
-------------------------------------------

### Jesus Christ calls the OT \`\`Scripture''

**[JHN 10:35](https://ref.ly/John10:35)** *See also* [MRK 12:10](https://ref.ly/Mark12:10), [MRK 12:24](https://ref.ly/Mark12:24) parallel [MAT 22:29](https://ref.ly/Matt22:29); [LUK 4:21](https://ref.ly/Luke4:21); [JHN 5:39](https://ref.ly/John5:39), [JHN 7:38](https://ref.ly/John7:38), [JHN 13:18](https://ref.ly/John13:18)

Jesus Christ underlines the authority of the OT
-----------------------------------------------

**[JHN 5:46–5:47](https://ref.ly/John5:46-John5:47)**

### The OT is authoritative over Jesus Christ's opponents

**[MAT 23:23](https://ref.ly/Matt23:23)** *See also* [MAT 5:19–5:20](https://ref.ly/Matt5:19-Matt5:20), [MAT 23:2–23:3](https://ref.ly/Matt23:2-Matt23:3); [MRK 2:24–2:27](https://ref.ly/Mark2:24-Mark2:27) parallels [MAT 12:2–12:6](https://ref.ly/Matt12:2-Matt12:6), [LUK 6:2–6:4](https://ref.ly/Luke6:2-Luke6:4)

### The OT is authoritative over Satan

**[MAT 4:4](https://ref.ly/Matt4:4)** parallel [LUK 4:4](https://ref.ly/Luke4:4) *See also* [DEU 8:3](https://ref.ly/Deut8:3); [MAT 4:7](https://ref.ly/Matt4:7) parallel [LUK 4:12](https://ref.ly/Luke4:12); [DEU 6:16](https://ref.ly/Deut6:16); [MAT 4:10](https://ref.ly/Matt4:10) parallel [LUK 4:8](https://ref.ly/Luke4:8); [DEU 6:13](https://ref.ly/Deut6:13)

Jesus Christ regards the OT as being fulfilled in himself
---------------------------------------------------------

### Jesus Christ regards his ministry as fulfilling the OT

**[MAT 5:17–5:18](https://ref.ly/Matt5:17-Matt5:18)** *See also* [MAT 11:4–11:6](https://ref.ly/Matt11:4-Matt11:6) parallel [LUK 7:22–7:23](https://ref.ly/Luke7:22-Luke7:23); [MAT 26:56](https://ref.ly/Matt26:56) parallel [MRK 14:49](https://ref.ly/Mark14:49); [LUK 4:17–4:21](https://ref.ly/Luke4:17-Luke4:21); [ISA 61:1–61:2](https://ref.ly/Isa61:1-Isa61:2); [JHN 15:25](https://ref.ly/John15:25); [PSA 35:19](https://ref.ly/Ps35:19), [PSA 69:4](https://ref.ly/Ps69:4)

### Jesus Christ regards his death as fulfilling OT prophecy

**[LUK 18:31–18:32](https://ref.ly/Luke18:31-Luke18:32)** *See also* [MAT 12:39–12:40](https://ref.ly/Matt12:39-Matt12:40), [MAT 26:28](https://ref.ly/Matt26:28) parallel [LUK 22:20](https://ref.ly/Luke22:20); [MAT 26:31](https://ref.ly/Matt26:31) parallel [MRK 14:27](https://ref.ly/Mark14:27); [ZEC 13:7](https://ref.ly/Zech13:7)

----------------------------------------------------

Jesus Christ appeals to the OT in its entirety
----------------------------------------------

**[LUK 11:50–11:51](https://ref.ly/Luke11:50-Luke11:51)** *The murders of Abel and Zechariah occur in the first ([Ge 4:8](https://ref.ly/Gen4:8)) and last ([2Ch 24:21](https://ref.ly/2Chr24:21)) books of the Hebrew OT (Chronicles comes at the close of the OT according to the Hebrew arrangement).* *See also* [LUK 24:27](https://ref.ly/Luke24:27), [LUK 24:44](https://ref.ly/Luke24:44) *The Law, the Prophets and the Psalms are the three divisions of the Hebrew OT.*

Jesus Christ treats the OT as a true historical record

## 2336: Jesus Christ, exaltation of (id: 2336)

Having completed his work on earth, Jesus Christ is raised to God's right hand where he receives honour, power and glory.

Jesus Christ is exalted to God's right hand
-------------------------------------------

**[1PE 3:21–3:22](https://ref.ly/1Pet3:21-1Pet3:22)** *God's right hand is the position of authority second only to the Father.* *See also* [MAT 26:64](https://ref.ly/Matt26:64) parallels [MRK 14:62](https://ref.ly/Mark14:62), [LUK 22:69](https://ref.ly/Luke22:69); [ACT 2:33](https://ref.ly/Acts2:33), [ACT 3:20–3:21](https://ref.ly/Acts3:20-Acts3:21), [ACT 7:55–7:56](https://ref.ly/Acts7:55-Acts7:56); [HEB 1:3](https://ref.ly/Heb1:3), [HEB 12:2](https://ref.ly/Heb12:2)

Jesus Christ is exalted because he first humbled himself
--------------------------------------------------------

**[LUK 24:26](https://ref.ly/Luke24:26)** *See also* [PHP 2:6–2:11](https://ref.ly/Phil2:6-Phil2:11); [1TI 3:16](https://ref.ly/1Tim3:16); [REV 5:6–5:14](https://ref.ly/Rev5:6-Rev5:14), [REV 7:17](https://ref.ly/Rev7:17), [REV 22:3](https://ref.ly/Rev22:3)

Jesus Christ's exaltation follows his resurrection and ascension
----------------------------------------------------------------

**[1PE 1:21](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:21)** *See also* [MRK 16:19](https://ref.ly/Mark16:19); [ACT 13:37](https://ref.ly/Acts13:37); [EPH 1:20](https://ref.ly/Eph1:20)

Jesus Christ's exaltation is predicted in the OT
------------------------------------------------

### As God's servant

**[ISA 52:13](https://ref.ly/Isa52:13)** *This “servant” is a specific prediction of Jesus Christ.*

Jesus Christ is exalted by God the Father
-----------------------------------------

**[PHP 2:9–2:11](https://ref.ly/Phil2:9-Phil2:11)** *See also* [ACT 2:36](https://ref.ly/Acts2:36), [ACT 5:31](https://ref.ly/Acts5:31)

The work of the exalted Christ
------------------------------

### As Saviour

**[ACT 5:31](https://ref.ly/Acts5:31)** *See also* [HEB 7:25](https://ref.ly/Heb7:25)

### As high priest and advocate

**[ROM 8:34](https://ref.ly/Rom8:34)** *See also* [HEB 4:14](https://ref.ly/Heb4:14), [HEB 7:24–7:26](https://ref.ly/Heb7:24-Heb7:26), [HEB 8:1–8:2](https://ref.ly/Heb8:1-Heb8:2), [HEB 9:24](https://ref.ly/Heb9:24); [1JN 2:1](https://ref.ly/1John2:1)

### In giving the Holy Spirit and spiritual gifts to his people

**[ACT 2:33](https://ref.ly/Acts2:33)** *See also* [EPH 4:8–4:13](https://ref.ly/Eph4:8-Eph4:13)

### In making every authority subject to him

**[EPH 1:20–1:22](https://ref.ly/Eph1:20-Eph1:22)** *See also* [1CO 15:24–15:26](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:24-1Cor15:26); [PHP 2:9–2:11](https://ref.ly/Phil2:9-Phil2:11); [HEB 2:7–2:9](https://ref.ly/Heb2:7-Heb2:9), [HEB 10:12–10:13](https://ref.ly/Heb10:12-Heb10:13); [1PE 3:22](https://ref.ly/1Pet3:22); [REV 17:14](https://ref.ly/Rev17:14), [REV 19:16](https://ref.ly/Rev19:16)

Believers should lead lives that are mindful of Jesus Christ's exaltation
-------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Believers are exalted with Jesus Christ

**[EPH 2:6](https://ref.ly/Eph2:6)** *See also* [REV 3:21](https://ref.ly/Rev3:21)

### Believers should be concerned with heavenly values

**[COL 3:1–3:4](https://ref.ly/Col3:1-Col3:4)** *See also* [PHP 3:20](https://ref.ly/Phil3:20); [HEB 12:2–12:3](https://ref.ly/Heb12:2-Heb12:3)

## 2339: Jesus Christ, example of (id: 2339)

Jesus Christ sets his disciples an example, especially in servanthood, self\-denial and endurance of suffering, so that they may become like him.

Jesus Christ calls believers to follow his example
--------------------------------------------------

**[JHN 13:14–13:16](https://ref.ly/John13:14-John13:16)** *See also* [HEB 3:1](https://ref.ly/Heb3:1), [HEB 12:2–12:3](https://ref.ly/Heb12:2-Heb12:3); [1PE 2:21](https://ref.ly/1Pet2:21); [1JN 2:6](https://ref.ly/1John2:6)

The qualities of Jesus Christ which set an example for believers
----------------------------------------------------------------

### Self\-denial

**[PHP 2:4–2:5](https://ref.ly/Phil2:4-Phil2:5)** *See also* [MAT 10:38](https://ref.ly/Matt10:38), [MAT 16:24](https://ref.ly/Matt16:24) parallels [MRK 8:34](https://ref.ly/Mark8:34), [LUK 9:23](https://ref.ly/Luke9:23); [LUK 14:27](https://ref.ly/Luke14:27); [HEB 12:2](https://ref.ly/Heb12:2)

### Endurance of suffering

**[1PE 2:21–2:23](https://ref.ly/1Pet2:21-1Pet2:23)** *See also* [MAT 10:24–10:25](https://ref.ly/Matt10:24-Matt10:25); [JHN 15:20](https://ref.ly/John15:20); [1TH 2:14–2:15](https://ref.ly/1Thess2:14-1Thess2:15); [HEB 12:3](https://ref.ly/Heb12:3)

### Service

[MAT 20:25–20:28](https://ref.ly/Matt20:25-Matt20:28) parallel [MRK 10:42–10:45](https://ref.ly/Mark10:42-Mark10:45); ; [JHN 13:13–13:17](https://ref.ly/John13:13-John13:17)

### Faithfulness

[HEB 3:1–3:2](https://ref.ly/Heb3:1-Heb3:2)

### Love

[EPH 5:1–5:2](https://ref.ly/Eph5:1-Eph5:2), [EPH 5:25](https://ref.ly/Eph5:25); ; [1JN 3:16](https://ref.ly/1John3:16)

### Patience

[1TI 1:16](https://ref.ly/1Tim1:16)

### Forgiveness of others

[EPH 4:32](https://ref.ly/Eph4:32); ; [COL 3:13](https://ref.ly/Col3:13)

### Gentleness and humility

[MAT 11:29](https://ref.ly/Matt11:29)

### Purity

[1JN 3:3](https://ref.ly/1John3:3)

### Prayer

[LUK 11:1](https://ref.ly/Luke11:1)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
