## 2345: Jesus Christ, kingdom of (id: 2345)

The present and future realm in which Jesus Christ exercises full authority, and through which he triumphs over all opposition.

Jesus Christ's kingdom is a heavenly kingdom
--------------------------------------------

### It is not of this world

**[JHN 18:36](https://ref.ly/John18:36)** *See also* [REV 5:6](https://ref.ly/Rev5:6), [REV 7:10](https://ref.ly/Rev7:10), [REV 21:1](https://ref.ly/Rev21:1), [REV 21:3](https://ref.ly/Rev21:3)

### The kingdom was given to him by God

**[DAN 7:14](https://ref.ly/Dan7:14)** *See also* [PSA 72:1](https://ref.ly/Ps72:1); [DAN 2:44](https://ref.ly/Dan2:44); [MAT 28:18](https://ref.ly/Matt28:18); [JHN 16:15](https://ref.ly/John16:15)

### The kingdom is his by right

**[COL 1:15–1:16](https://ref.ly/Col1:15-Col1:16)** *See also* [HEB 1:8](https://ref.ly/Heb1:8); [PSA 45:6](https://ref.ly/Ps45:6); [REV 22:13](https://ref.ly/Rev22:13)

Jesus Christ inherits the kingdom promised to David
---------------------------------------------------

**[LUK 1:32](https://ref.ly/Luke1:32)** *See also* [ROM 15:12](https://ref.ly/Rom15:12); [ISA 11:10](https://ref.ly/Isa11:10); [REV 2:27](https://ref.ly/Rev2:27); [PSA 2:9](https://ref.ly/Ps2:9)

Jesus Christ reveals God's kingdom on earth
-------------------------------------------

### Jesus Christ brought in God's kingdom

**[MAT 4:17](https://ref.ly/Matt4:17)** *The expressions “kingdom of heaven” and the “kingdom of God” are interchangeable.* *See also* [MAT 3:2](https://ref.ly/Matt3:2), [MAT 10:7](https://ref.ly/Matt10:7), [MAT 12:28](https://ref.ly/Matt12:28) parallel [LUK 11:20](https://ref.ly/Luke11:20); [MRK 1:15](https://ref.ly/Mark1:15); [LUK 17:20–17:21](https://ref.ly/Luke17:20-Luke17:21)

### Miracles are a sign of the kingdom

**[JHN 6:14–6:15](https://ref.ly/John6:14-John6:15)** *See also* [MAT 8:26–8:27](https://ref.ly/Matt8:26-Matt8:27) parallels [MRK 4:39–4:41](https://ref.ly/Mark4:39-Mark4:41), [LUK 8:24–8:25](https://ref.ly/Luke8:24-Luke8:25) *authority over the created world*; [MAT 11:2–11:5](https://ref.ly/Matt11:2-Matt11:5) parallel [LUK 7:19–7:22](https://ref.ly/Luke7:19-Luke7:22) *authority to heal*[LUK 7:11–7:15](https://ref.ly/Luke7:11-Luke7:15); [REV 1:17–1:18](https://ref.ly/Rev1:17-Rev1:18)

### Parables are a sign of the kingdom

**[MAT 13:1–13:52](https://ref.ly/Matt13:1-Matt13:52)** *See also* [MRK 4:1–4:34](https://ref.ly/Mark4:1-Mark4:34); [LUK 8:4–8:15](https://ref.ly/Luke8:4-Luke8:15), [LUK 13:18–13:21](https://ref.ly/Luke13:18-Luke13:21)

Jesus Christ exercises kingdom authority today
----------------------------------------------

### Believers enter Jesus Christ's kingdom immediately

**[LUK 23:42–23:43](https://ref.ly/Luke23:42-Luke23:43)** *See also* [MAT 5:3](https://ref.ly/Matt5:3) parallel [LUK 6:20](https://ref.ly/Luke6:20); [MAT 11:11](https://ref.ly/Matt11:11)

### Believers are redeemed from the kingdom of darkness

**[COL 1:12–1:13](https://ref.ly/Col1:12-Col1:13)** *See also* [EPH 5:5](https://ref.ly/Eph5:5)

### Believers enjoy the blessings of Jesus Christ's kingdom now

**[MAT 16:19](https://ref.ly/Matt16:19)** *See also* [DAN 7:22](https://ref.ly/Dan7:22), [DAN 7:27](https://ref.ly/Dan7:27); [LUK 12:32](https://ref.ly/Luke12:32), [LUK 22:29–22:30](https://ref.ly/Luke22:29-Luke22:30); [JAS 2:5](https://ref.ly/Jas2:5); [REV 1:5–1:6](https://ref.ly/Rev1:5-Rev1:6), [REV 1:9](https://ref.ly/Rev1:9), [REV 3:21](https://ref.ly/Rev3:21)

### Jesus Christ rules over every authority now

**[1PE 3:22](https://ref.ly/1Pet3:22)** *See also* [EPH 1:20–1:23](https://ref.ly/Eph1:20-Eph1:23); [PHP 2:9](https://ref.ly/Phil2:9); [COL 2:10](https://ref.ly/Col2:10); [HEB 12:2](https://ref.ly/Heb12:2); [REV 12:10](https://ref.ly/Rev12:10), [REV 19:16](https://ref.ly/Rev19:16)

Jesus Christ's kingdom will be fully established at his return
--------------------------------------------------------------

### His kingdom will come with power at a specific moment

**[MAT 25:31](https://ref.ly/Matt25:31)** *See also* [ZEC 9:10](https://ref.ly/Zech9:10); [MAT 24:30–24:31](https://ref.ly/Matt24:30-Matt24:31) parallels [MRK 13:26–13:27](https://ref.ly/Mark13:26-Mark13:27), [LUK 21:27](https://ref.ly/Luke21:27); [2TI 4:1](https://ref.ly/2Tim4:1)

### His kingdom will replace all earthly authority

**[REV 11:15](https://ref.ly/Rev11:15)** *See also* [1CO 15:24–15:25](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:24-1Cor15:25), [1CO 15:50–15:52](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:50-1Cor15:52); [PHP 3:20–3:21](https://ref.ly/Phil3:20-Phil3:21)

### All creation will acknowledge Jesus Christ's kingship

**[PHP 2:10–2:11](https://ref.ly/Phil2:10-Phil2:11)** *See also* [PSA 2:6–2:8](https://ref.ly/Ps2:6-Ps2:8); [REV 5:13](https://ref.ly/Rev5:13)

**[LUK 1:33](https://ref.ly/Luke1:33)** *See also* [ISA 9:7](https://ref.ly/Isa9:7)

## 2351: Jesus Christ, miracles of (id: 2351)

Supernatural acts of Jesus Christ, revealing and confirming his Messianic credentials, and the coming of God's kingdom. The miracles of Christ are to be seen as an integral part of his ministry.

Examples of the kind of miracles Jesus Christ performed
-------------------------------------------------------

### Authority over natural forces

**[MAT 8:27](https://ref.ly/Matt8:27)** parallels [MRK 4:41](https://ref.ly/Mark4:41), [LUK 8:25](https://ref.ly/Luke8:25) *See also* [MAT 14:19–14:20](https://ref.ly/Matt14:19-Matt14:20) parallels [MRK 6:41–6:43](https://ref.ly/Mark6:41-Mark6:43), [LUK 9:16–9:17](https://ref.ly/Luke9:16-Luke9:17), [JHN 6:11–6:13](https://ref.ly/John6:11-John6:13) *the feeding of 5,000*; [MAT 14:25](https://ref.ly/Matt14:25) parallels [MRK 6:48](https://ref.ly/Mark6:48), [JHN 6:19](https://ref.ly/John6:19) *Jesus Christ walks on water*; [MAT 17:27](https://ref.ly/Matt17:27); [LUK 5:4](https://ref.ly/Luke5:4), [LUK 5:6](https://ref.ly/Luke5:6); [JHN 2:9](https://ref.ly/John2:9) *Jesus Christ turns water into wine.*

### Healing the sick

**[MAT 4:24](https://ref.ly/Matt4:24)** *See also* [MAT 8:13](https://ref.ly/Matt8:13) parallel [LUK 7:10](https://ref.ly/Luke7:10); [MAT 8:15](https://ref.ly/Matt8:15) parallels [MRK 1:31](https://ref.ly/Mark1:31), [LUK 4:39](https://ref.ly/Luke4:39) *Simon's mother\-in\-law*; [MAT 9:22](https://ref.ly/Matt9:22) parallels [MRK 5:29](https://ref.ly/Mark5:29), [LUK 8:44](https://ref.ly/Luke8:44) *the woman with the issue of blood*; [MAT 9:29–9:30](https://ref.ly/Matt9:29-Matt9:30), [MAT 12:13](https://ref.ly/Matt12:13) parallels [MRK 3:5](https://ref.ly/Mark3:5), [LUK 6:10](https://ref.ly/Luke6:10) *the man with a shrivelled hand*; [MRK 7:35](https://ref.ly/Mark7:35); [LUK 17:14](https://ref.ly/Luke17:14); [JHN 4:52–4:53](https://ref.ly/John4:52-John4:53), [JHN 5:8–5:9](https://ref.ly/John5:8-John5:9), [JHN 9:6–9:7](https://ref.ly/John9:6-John9:7)

### Casting out demons

**[MRK 1:34](https://ref.ly/Mark1:34)** parallels [MAT 8:16](https://ref.ly/Matt8:16), [LUK 4:41](https://ref.ly/Luke4:41) *See also* [MAT 9:33](https://ref.ly/Matt9:33), [MAT 12:22](https://ref.ly/Matt12:22) parallel [LUK 11:14](https://ref.ly/Luke11:14); [MAT 17:18](https://ref.ly/Matt17:18) parallels [MRK 9:25–9:26](https://ref.ly/Mark9:25-Mark9:26), [LUK 9:42](https://ref.ly/Luke9:42)

### Raising the dead

**[LUK 7:14–7:15](https://ref.ly/Luke7:14-Luke7:15)** *See also* [MAT 9:25](https://ref.ly/Matt9:25) parallels [MRK 5:41–5:42](https://ref.ly/Mark5:41-Mark5:42), [LUK 8:54–8:55](https://ref.ly/Luke8:54-Luke8:55); [JHN 11:43–11:44](https://ref.ly/John11:43-John11:44)

The purpose of Jesus Christ's miracles
--------------------------------------

### To bring healing and wholeness

**[LUK 8:35](https://ref.ly/Luke8:35)** *See also* [MAT 15:28](https://ref.ly/Matt15:28); [LUK 17:14–17:15](https://ref.ly/Luke17:14-Luke17:15); [JHN 9:38](https://ref.ly/John9:38)

### To reveal God's kingdom

**[MAT 12:28](https://ref.ly/Matt12:28)** parallel [LUK 11:20](https://ref.ly/Luke11:20) *See also* [MAT 11:4–11:5](https://ref.ly/Matt11:4-Matt11:5) parallel [LUK 7:22](https://ref.ly/Luke7:22)

### To fulfil God's word

**[MAT 8:16–8:17](https://ref.ly/Matt8:16-Matt8:17)** *See also* [ISA 53:4](https://ref.ly/Isa53:4); [MAT 12:15–12:17](https://ref.ly/Matt12:15-Matt12:17); [LUK 4:18–4:19](https://ref.ly/Luke4:18-Luke4:19); [ISA 61:1–61:2](https://ref.ly/Isa61:1-Isa61:2); [LUK 4:21](https://ref.ly/Luke4:21)

### To bring glory to God

**[JHN 11:4](https://ref.ly/John11:4)** *See also* [MAT 15:31](https://ref.ly/Matt15:31); [JHN 2:11](https://ref.ly/John2:11)

### To show Jesus to be the Messiah

**[ACT 2:22](https://ref.ly/Acts2:22)** *See also* [MAT 11:3–11:5](https://ref.ly/Matt11:3-Matt11:5) parallel [LUK 7:19–7:22](https://ref.ly/Luke7:19-Luke7:22); [JHN 5:36](https://ref.ly/John5:36), [JHN 10:25](https://ref.ly/John10:25), [JHN 10:37–10:38](https://ref.ly/John10:37-John10:38), [JHN 11:42](https://ref.ly/John11:42)

Varying responses to Jesus Christ's miracles
--------------------------------------------

### Terror and fear

**[MRK 4:41](https://ref.ly/Mark4:41)** parallel [LUK 8:25](https://ref.ly/Luke8:25) *See also* [MAT 8:34](https://ref.ly/Matt8:34); [MRK 5:15](https://ref.ly/Mark5:15) parallel [LUK 8:35](https://ref.ly/Luke8:35)

### Wonder and amazement

**[LUK 4:36](https://ref.ly/Luke4:36)** parallel [MRK 1:27](https://ref.ly/Mark1:27) *See also* [MAT 9:33](https://ref.ly/Matt9:33), [MAT 12:23](https://ref.ly/Matt12:23); [LUK 9:43](https://ref.ly/Luke9:43), [LUK 11:14](https://ref.ly/Luke11:14)

### Faith and gratitude

**[LUK 19:37](https://ref.ly/Luke19:37)** *See also* [MRK 5:18–5:20](https://ref.ly/Mark5:18-Mark5:20) parallel [LUK 8:38–8:39](https://ref.ly/Luke8:38-Luke8:39); [LUK 17:15–17:16](https://ref.ly/Luke17:15-Luke17:16); [JHN 9:38](https://ref.ly/John9:38), [JHN 14:11](https://ref.ly/John14:11), [JHN 20:30–20:31](https://ref.ly/John20:30-John20:31)

### Opposition and hatred

**[JHN 15:24](https://ref.ly/John15:24)** *See also* [MAT 11:20–11:21](https://ref.ly/Matt11:20-Matt11:21) parallel [LUK 10:13](https://ref.ly/Luke10:13); [MAT 12:24](https://ref.ly/Matt12:24) parallels [MRK 3:22](https://ref.ly/Mark3:22), [LUK 11:15](https://ref.ly/Luke11:15); [JHN 12:10–12:11](https://ref.ly/John12:10-John12:11), [JHN 12:37–12:38](https://ref.ly/John12:37-John12:38)

Limitations on Jesus Christ's miracles
--------------------------------------

### Jesus Christ restricted his miracles because of superficial faith

**[JHN 2:23–2:24](https://ref.ly/John2:23-John2:24)** *See also* [MAT 12:38–12:39](https://ref.ly/Matt12:38-Matt12:39) parallel [LUK 11:29](https://ref.ly/Luke11:29); [MAT 16:1–16:4](https://ref.ly/Matt16:1-Matt16:4) parallel [MRK 8:11–8:12](https://ref.ly/Mark8:11-Mark8:12); [JHN 2:18](https://ref.ly/John2:18), [JHN 6:30](https://ref.ly/John6:30)

### Miracles require faith

**[MAT 13:58](https://ref.ly/Matt13:58)** parallel [MRK 6:5](https://ref.ly/Mark6:5) *See also* [MAT 14:28–14:31](https://ref.ly/Matt14:28-Matt14:31), [MAT 17:14–17:20](https://ref.ly/Matt17:14-Matt17:20)

------------------------------------------------

### Through the disciples during Jesus Christ's lifetime

### Through the church

[1CO 12:10](https://ref.ly/1Cor12:10), [1CO 12:28–12:29](https://ref.ly/1Cor12:28-1Cor12:29)

## 2354: Jesus Christ, mission of (id: 2354)

The work that Jesus Christ was sent to do, including both his healing and preaching ministry, but particularly his work of salvation. Jesus Christ sends Christians to continue his work by proclaiming his message of salvation.

Jesus Christ was called to his mission from the beginning of time
-----------------------------------------------------------------

**[ISA 49:1](https://ref.ly/Isa49:1)** *See also* [MIC 5:2](https://ref.ly/Mic5:2); [1PE 1:20](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:20)

Jesus' mission as Messiah was foretold
--------------------------------------

### His mission to help and heal the poor

**[ISA 61:1–61:3](https://ref.ly/Isa61:1-Isa61:3)** *See also* [ISA 11:3–11:5](https://ref.ly/Isa11:3-Isa11:5), [ISA 32:3–32:4](https://ref.ly/Isa32:3-Isa32:4), [ISA 35:5–35:6](https://ref.ly/Isa35:5-Isa35:6), [ISA 42:3](https://ref.ly/Isa42:3), [ISA 42:7](https://ref.ly/Isa42:7)

### His mission to rule and establish the kingdom of God

**[ISA 9:6–9:7](https://ref.ly/Isa9:6-Isa9:7)** *See also* [GEN 49:10](https://ref.ly/Gen49:10); [PSA 132:11](https://ref.ly/Ps132:11); [JER 23:5–23:6](https://ref.ly/Jer23:5-Jer23:6); [DAN 2:44](https://ref.ly/Dan2:44)

### His mission to establish justice and peace

**[ISA 11:4–11:5](https://ref.ly/Isa11:4-Isa11:5)** *See also* [ISA 2:4](https://ref.ly/Isa2:4), [ISA 9:4–9:7](https://ref.ly/Isa9:4-Isa9:7), [ISA 42:4](https://ref.ly/Isa42:4)

### His mission to suffer and die

**[ISA 53:3–53:10](https://ref.ly/Isa53:3-Isa53:10)** *See also* [ISA 50:6](https://ref.ly/Isa50:6), [ISA 52:14](https://ref.ly/Isa52:14); [DAN 9:26](https://ref.ly/Dan9:26); [MRK 8:31](https://ref.ly/Mark8:31); [LUK 24:26–24:27](https://ref.ly/Luke24:26-Luke24:27); [ACT 8:32–8:35](https://ref.ly/Acts8:32-Acts8:35)

### His mission was fulfilled in humility and poverty

**[ZEC 9:9](https://ref.ly/Zech9:9)** *See also* [ISA 42:2–42:3](https://ref.ly/Isa42:2-Isa42:3), [ISA 49:7](https://ref.ly/Isa49:7)

### His mission was for all nations

**[ISA 49:6](https://ref.ly/Isa49:6)** *See also* [ISA 11:10](https://ref.ly/Isa11:10), [ISA 42:1–42:6](https://ref.ly/Isa42:1-Isa42:6), [ISA 55:4–55:5](https://ref.ly/Isa55:4-Isa55:5)

Aspects of Jesus Christ's mission
---------------------------------

### Preaching and teaching

**[LUK 4:43](https://ref.ly/Luke4:43)** parallel [MRK 1:38](https://ref.ly/Mark1:38) *See also* [MAT 4:17](https://ref.ly/Matt4:17), [MAT 5:2](https://ref.ly/Matt5:2); [MRK 1:21](https://ref.ly/Mark1:21); [JHN 8:2](https://ref.ly/John8:2), [JHN 18:37](https://ref.ly/John18:37)

### Sacrificial service

**[MAT 20:28](https://ref.ly/Matt20:28)** parallel [MRK 10:45](https://ref.ly/Mark10:45) *See also* [LUK 22:27](https://ref.ly/Luke22:27); [JHN 13:13–13:16](https://ref.ly/John13:13-John13:16); [PHP 2:7](https://ref.ly/Phil2:7)

### Healing

**[MAT 4:23](https://ref.ly/Matt4:23)** *A healing ministry was one of the signs of the expected Messiah.* *See also* [MAT 14:14](https://ref.ly/Matt14:14); [MRK 1:34](https://ref.ly/Mark1:34); [LUK 4:40](https://ref.ly/Luke4:40), [LUK 5:15](https://ref.ly/Luke5:15); [JHN 9:4–9:7](https://ref.ly/John9:4-John9:7)

### Judgment

**[JHN 9:39](https://ref.ly/John9:39)** *Jesus Christ does not come to condemn, but the response people make to him is the ultimate criterion of judgment. Those truly seeking God turn to faith in Jesus Christ; unbelievers, by their rejection of him, are confirmed in their unbelief.* *See also* [LUK 12:49](https://ref.ly/Luke12:49); [JHN 3:17–3:18](https://ref.ly/John3:17-John3:18), [JHN 5:22](https://ref.ly/John5:22), [JHN 8:10–8:11](https://ref.ly/John8:10-John8:11), [JHN 8:26](https://ref.ly/John8:26), [JHN 12:47–12:48](https://ref.ly/John12:47-John12:48)

Criteria for the direction of Jesus Christ's mission
----------------------------------------------------

### Obedience to his Father's will

**[JHN 6:38](https://ref.ly/John6:38)** *See also* [MAT 26:39](https://ref.ly/Matt26:39) parallels [MRK 14:36](https://ref.ly/Mark14:36), [LUK 22:42](https://ref.ly/Luke22:42); [JHN 4:34](https://ref.ly/John4:34), [JHN 14:31](https://ref.ly/John14:31), [JHN 18:11](https://ref.ly/John18:11)

### The fulfilment of the Law and the Prophets

**[MAT 5:17](https://ref.ly/Matt5:17)** *See also* [MAT 13:35](https://ref.ly/Matt13:35), [MAT 26:54](https://ref.ly/Matt26:54); [LUK 4:18–4:21](https://ref.ly/Luke4:18-Luke4:21), [LUK 18:31](https://ref.ly/Luke18:31); [ROM 3:21](https://ref.ly/Rom3:21)

Jesus Christ's saving death is the supreme aspect and focus of his mission
--------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Jesus Christ came to save and to give life

**[JHN 10:10](https://ref.ly/John10:10)** *See also* [MAT 1:21](https://ref.ly/Matt1:21); [LUK 19:10](https://ref.ly/Luke19:10); [JHN 3:17](https://ref.ly/John3:17); [1TI 1:15](https://ref.ly/1Tim1:15); [2TI 1:10](https://ref.ly/2Tim1:10)

### Jesus Christ came to suffer and to die

**[MAT 16:21](https://ref.ly/Matt16:21)** parallels [MRK 8:31](https://ref.ly/Mark8:31), [LUK 9:22](https://ref.ly/Luke9:22) *See also* [MAT 20:28](https://ref.ly/Matt20:28) parallel [MRK 10:45](https://ref.ly/Mark10:45); [JHN 12:27](https://ref.ly/John12:27); [ROM 3:24–3:25](https://ref.ly/Rom3:24-Rom3:25); [COL 1:20](https://ref.ly/Col1:20); [1JN 4:10](https://ref.ly/1John4:10)

### Jesus Christ was aware of the personal cost of his mission

**[LUK 12:50](https://ref.ly/Luke12:50)** *See also* [MAT 26:38–26:39](https://ref.ly/Matt26:38-Matt26:39) parallels [MRK 14:34–14:36](https://ref.ly/Mark14:34-Mark14:36), [LUK 22:42](https://ref.ly/Luke22:42)

The mission of Jesus Christ continues today
-------------------------------------------

### Jesus Christ's own work continues

**[HEB 7:24–7:25](https://ref.ly/Heb7:24-Heb7:25)** *See also* [ROM 8:34](https://ref.ly/Rom8:34), [ROM 15:18](https://ref.ly/Rom15:18); [2CO 4:10–4:11](https://ref.ly/2Cor4:10-2Cor4:11); [HEB 6:20](https://ref.ly/Heb6:20), [HEB 9:12](https://ref.ly/Heb9:12), [HEB 9:14](https://ref.ly/Heb9:14), [HEB 13:21](https://ref.ly/Heb13:21)

### Christians are called to share in Jesus Christ's mission

**[JHN 20:21](https://ref.ly/John20:21)** *See also* [MAT 28:19–28:20](https://ref.ly/Matt28:19-Matt28:20); [MRK 16:15](https://ref.ly/Mark16:15); [JHN 14:12](https://ref.ly/John14:12)

* **Associated Passages:** Isaiah 49:1; Micah 5:2; 1 Peter 1:20; Isaiah 61:1-3; Isaiah 11:3-5; Isaiah 32:3-4; Isaiah 35:5-6; Isaiah 42:3; Isaiah 42:7; Isaiah 9:6-7; Genesis 49:10; Psalms 132:11; Jeremiah 23:5-6; Daniel 2:44; Isaiah 11:4-5; Isaiah 2:4; Isaiah 9:4-7; Isaiah 42:4; Isaiah 53:3-10; Isaiah 50:6; Isaiah 52:14; Daniel 9:26; Mark 8:31; Luke 24:26-27; Acts 8:32-35; Zechariah 9:9; Isaiah 42:2-3; Isaiah 49:7; Isaiah 49:6; Isaiah 11:10; Isaiah 42:1-6; Isaiah 55:4-5; Luke 4:43; Mark 1:38; Matthew 4:17; Matthew 5:2; Mark 1:21; John 8:2; John 18:37; Matthew 20:28; Mark 10:45; Luke 22:27; John 13:13-16; Philippians 2:7; Matthew 4:23; Matthew 14:14; Mark 1:34; Luke 4:40; Luke 5:15; John 9:4-7; John 9:39; Luke 12:49; John 3:17-18; John 5:22; John 8:10-11; John 8:26; John 12:47-48; John 6:38; Matthew 26:39; Mark 14:36; Luke 22:42; John 4:34; John 14:31; John 18:11; Matthew 5:17; Matthew 13:35; Matthew 26:54; Luke 4:18-21; Luke 18:31; Romans 3:21; John 10:10; Matthew 1:21; Luke 19:10; John 3:17; 1 Timothy 1:15; 2 Timothy 1:10; Matthew 16:21; Luke 9:22; John 12:27; Romans 3:24-25; Colossians 1:20; 1 John 4:10; Luke 12:50; Matthew 26:38-39; Mark 14:34-36; Hebrews 7:24-25; Romans 8:34; Romans 15:18; 2 Corinthians 4:10-11; Hebrews 6:20; Hebrews 9:12; Hebrews 9:14; Hebrews 13:21; John 20:21; Matthew 28:19-20; Mark 16:15; John 14:12

## 2357: Jesus Christ, parables of (id: 2357)

A central feature of Jesus Christ's teaching was the use of extended similies and short stories about the kingdom of God, based on human experience. Christ used them frequently to call for a response to his message.

Parables are a central feature of Jesus Christ's teaching
---------------------------------------------------------

**[MAT 13:34–13:35](https://ref.ly/Matt13:34-Matt13:35)** *See also* [PSA 78:2](https://ref.ly/Ps78:2); [MRK 4:33–4:34](https://ref.ly/Mark4:33-Mark4:34)

Different characteristics of Jesus Christ's parables
----------------------------------------------------

### They vary in complexity and length

[MAT 7:6](https://ref.ly/Matt7:6), [MAT 13:18–13:23](https://ref.ly/Matt13:18-Matt13:23) parallels [MRK 4:13–4:20](https://ref.ly/Mark4:13-Mark4:20), [LUK 8:11–8:15](https://ref.ly/Luke8:11-Luke8:15); ; [MAT 13:37–13:45](https://ref.ly/Matt13:37-Matt13:45), [MAT 13:52](https://ref.ly/Matt13:52)

### They vary in their use of metaphors, word pictures, objects and actions

[MAT 5:13–5:16](https://ref.ly/Matt5:13-Matt5:16), [MAT 13:44](https://ref.ly/Matt13:44), [MAT 18:2–18:3](https://ref.ly/Matt18:2-Matt18:3), [MAT 21:18–21:22](https://ref.ly/Matt21:18-Matt21:22) parallels [MRK 11:12–11:14](https://ref.ly/Mark11:12-Mark11:14), [MRK 11:20–11:24](https://ref.ly/Mark11:20-Mark11:24); ; [LUK 15:8–15:10](https://ref.ly/Luke15:8-Luke15:10)

### They have different levels of meaning

Often the full impact of a parable may be lost if the Jewish context is not understood: [LUK 10:30–10:37](https://ref.ly/Luke10:30-Luke10:37), [LUK 15:11–15:32](https://ref.ly/Luke15:11-Luke15:32)

### They draw on human experience

[MAT 13:33](https://ref.ly/Matt13:33) parallel [LUK 13:20–13:21](https://ref.ly/Luke13:20-Luke13:21); ; [MAT 18:12–18:14](https://ref.ly/Matt18:12-Matt18:14) parallel [LUK 15:4–15:7](https://ref.ly/Luke15:4-Luke15:7); ; [LUK 7:41–7:43](https://ref.ly/Luke7:41-Luke7:43)

The themes of Jesus Christ's parables
-------------------------------------

### The kingdom of God

**[MRK 4:30](https://ref.ly/Mark4:30)** parallel [LUK 13:18](https://ref.ly/Luke13:18) *See also* [MAT 13:31–13:32](https://ref.ly/Matt13:31-Matt13:32) parallels [MRK 4:31–4:32](https://ref.ly/Mark4:31-Mark4:32), [LUK 13:19–13:21](https://ref.ly/Luke13:19-Luke13:21); [MAT 13:44–13:45](https://ref.ly/Matt13:44-Matt13:45); [MRK 4:26–4:29](https://ref.ly/Mark4:26-Mark4:29)

### Relationship with God

**[LUK 15:20](https://ref.ly/Luke15:20)** *See also* [MAT 7:9–7:11](https://ref.ly/Matt7:9-Matt7:11) parallel [LUK 11:11–11:13](https://ref.ly/Luke11:11-Luke11:13); [MAT 18:12–18:14](https://ref.ly/Matt18:12-Matt18:14) parallel [LUK 15:4–15:7](https://ref.ly/Luke15:4-Luke15:7); [LUK 18:7–18:8](https://ref.ly/Luke18:7-Luke18:8)

### Right behaviour

**[LUK 10:37](https://ref.ly/Luke10:37)** *See also* [MAT 7:24–7:27](https://ref.ly/Matt7:24-Matt7:27) parallel [LUK 6:47–6:49](https://ref.ly/Luke6:47-Luke6:49); [LUK 13:6–13:9](https://ref.ly/Luke13:6-Luke13:9), [LUK 15:27](https://ref.ly/Luke15:27)

### The time of the end

**[MAT 25:34](https://ref.ly/Matt25:34)** *See also* [MAT 25:1](https://ref.ly/Matt25:1), [MAT 25:14–25:19](https://ref.ly/Matt25:14-Matt25:19) parallel [LUK 19:11–19:15](https://ref.ly/Luke19:11-Luke19:15); [MRK 13:35](https://ref.ly/Mark13:35); [LUK 12:35–12:36](https://ref.ly/Luke12:35-Luke12:36), [LUK 12:40](https://ref.ly/Luke12:40) parallel [MAT 24:44](https://ref.ly/Matt24:44); [LUK 16:22–16:23](https://ref.ly/Luke16:22-Luke16:23)

### Jesus Christ speaks about himself

**[MAT 21:37](https://ref.ly/Matt21:37)** parallels [MRK 12:6](https://ref.ly/Mark12:6), [LUK 20:13](https://ref.ly/Luke20:13) *See also* [MAT 22:2](https://ref.ly/Matt22:2), [MAT 25:10](https://ref.ly/Matt25:10)JHN [6:35](https://ref.ly/Matt6:35), [JHN 8:12](https://ref.ly/John8:12), [JHN 10:14](https://ref.ly/John10:14), [JHN 15:1](https://ref.ly/John15:1)

Understanding Jesus Christ's parables
-------------------------------------

### Further explanation is sometimes needed

**[MAT 13:36](https://ref.ly/Matt13:36)** *See also* [MAT 13:18](https://ref.ly/Matt13:18) parallels [MRK 4:13](https://ref.ly/Mark4:13), [LUK 8:11](https://ref.ly/Luke8:11); [MAT 15:15](https://ref.ly/Matt15:15) parallel [MRK 7:17](https://ref.ly/Mark7:17)

### The meaning is sometimes hidden

**[LUK 8:9–8:10](https://ref.ly/Luke8:9-Luke8:10)** parallels [MAT 13:11–13:16](https://ref.ly/Matt13:11-Matt13:16), [MRK 4:11–4:12](https://ref.ly/Mark4:11-Mark4:12) *The meaning of Jesus Christ's parables was concealed only from those whose hearts and minds were closed.* *See also* [ISA 6:9–6:10](https://ref.ly/Isa6:9-Isa6:10)

Responses to Jesus Christ's parables
------------------------------------

### The parables demand action

**[MAT 5:14–5:16](https://ref.ly/Matt5:14-Matt5:16)** *See also* [MAT 4:24](https://ref.ly/Matt4:24), [MAT 7:5–7:6](https://ref.ly/Matt7:5-Matt7:6), [MAT 13:43](https://ref.ly/Matt13:43), [MAT 13:45–13:46](https://ref.ly/Matt13:45-Matt13:46), [MAT 25:13](https://ref.ly/Matt25:13), [MAT 25:40](https://ref.ly/Matt25:40), [MAT 25:45](https://ref.ly/Matt25:45); [LUK 12:21](https://ref.ly/Luke12:21), [LUK 12:32–12:33](https://ref.ly/Luke12:32-Luke12:33)

### Positive responses

**[MAT 13:16](https://ref.ly/Matt13:16)** *See also* [MAT 7:28–7:29](https://ref.ly/Matt7:28-Matt7:29), [MAT 13:51](https://ref.ly/Matt13:51)

### Rejection of Jesus Christ and his parables

**[LUK 20:19](https://ref.ly/Luke20:19)** parallels [MAT 21:45–21:46](https://ref.ly/Matt21:45-Matt21:46), [MRK 12:12](https://ref.ly/Mark12:12) *See also* [LUK 16:14](https://ref.ly/Luke16:14)

## 2360: Jesus Christ, prayers of (id: 2360)

Prayer was the essence of Jesus Christ's relationship with the Father. He prayed for himself and his mission, and he continues to pray for all believers.

Jesus Christ's practice of prayer
---------------------------------

### He prayed regularly

**[LUK 5:16](https://ref.ly/Luke5:16)** *Luke records more instances of Jesus Christ praying than any other Gospel writer.*

### He often prayed alone

**[MRK 1:35](https://ref.ly/Mark1:35)** *See also* [MAT 14:23](https://ref.ly/Matt14:23) parallel [MRK 6:46](https://ref.ly/Mark6:46); [LUK 6:12](https://ref.ly/Luke6:12), [LUK 9:18](https://ref.ly/Luke9:18)

Prayer at specific times in Jesus Christ's life
-----------------------------------------------

Before his death: [MAT 26:36–26:46](https://ref.ly/Matt26:36-Matt26:46) parallels [MRK 14:32–14:41](https://ref.ly/Mark14:32-Mark14:41), [LUK 22:39–22:46](https://ref.ly/Luke22:39-Luke22:46); ; [JHN 17:1–17:26](https://ref.ly/John17:1-John17:26); [MAT 27:46](https://ref.ly/Matt27:46) parallel [MRK 15:34](https://ref.ly/Mark15:34); ; [LUK 23:34](https://ref.ly/Luke23:34), [LUK 23:46](https://ref.ly/Luke23:46), [LUK 3:21–3:22](https://ref.ly/Luke3:21-Luke3:22) *at his baptism*; ; [LUK 6:12–6:13](https://ref.ly/Luke6:12-Luke6:13) *before choosing the apostles*; ; [LUK 9:28–9:29](https://ref.ly/Luke9:28-Luke9:29) *before his transfiguration*

Characteristics of Jesus Christ's prayers
-----------------------------------------

### Communion with his Father

[MAT 6:9](https://ref.ly/Matt6:9) parallel [LUK 11:2](https://ref.ly/Luke11:2); ; [MAT 11:27](https://ref.ly/Matt11:27) parallel [LUK 10:22](https://ref.ly/Luke10:22)

### Submission to his Father

**[HEB 5:7](https://ref.ly/Heb5:7)** *See also* [MAT 6:10](https://ref.ly/Matt6:10), [MAT 26:36](https://ref.ly/Matt26:36) parallels [MRK 14:36](https://ref.ly/Mark14:36), [LUK 22:42](https://ref.ly/Luke22:42)

### Giving praise and thanks to his Father

**[MAT 11:25–11:26](https://ref.ly/Matt11:25-Matt11:26)** parallel [LUK 10:21](https://ref.ly/Luke10:21) *See also* [MAT 14:19](https://ref.ly/Matt14:19) parallels [MRK 6:41](https://ref.ly/Mark6:41), [LUK 9:16](https://ref.ly/Luke9:16), [JHN 6:11](https://ref.ly/John6:11); [MAT 15:36](https://ref.ly/Matt15:36) parallel [MRK 8:6–8:7](https://ref.ly/Mark8:6-Mark8:7); [MAT 26:26–26:27](https://ref.ly/Matt26:26-Matt26:27) parallels [MRK 14:22–14:23](https://ref.ly/Mark14:22-Mark14:23), [LUK 22:17–22:19](https://ref.ly/Luke22:17-Luke22:19), [1CO 11:24](https://ref.ly/1Cor11:24) *the Lord's Supper*; [LUK 24:30](https://ref.ly/Luke24:30); [JHN 11:41–11:42](https://ref.ly/John11:41-John11:42)

The scope of Jesus Christ's prayers
-----------------------------------

[MAT 19:13–19:15](https://ref.ly/Matt19:13-Matt19:15) parallels [MRK 10:13–10:16](https://ref.ly/Mark10:13-Mark10:16), [LUK 18:15–18:17](https://ref.ly/Luke18:15-Luke18:17) *for children*; [LUK 22:31–22:32](https://ref.ly/Luke22:31-Luke22:32); ; [JHN 14:16](https://ref.ly/John14:16), [JHN 17:6–17:19](https://ref.ly/John17:6-John17:19); [LUK 23:34](https://ref.ly/Luke23:34) *for his persecutors*; [JHN 12:27–12:28](https://ref.ly/John12:27-John12:28), [JHN 17:1–17:5](https://ref.ly/John17:1-John17:5); [JHN 17:20–17:26](https://ref.ly/John17:20-John17:26) *for all believers*

Jesus Christ's continuing ministry of prayer
--------------------------------------------

**[HEB 7:25](https://ref.ly/Heb7:25)** *See also* [ROM 8:34](https://ref.ly/Rom8:34); [1JN 2:1](https://ref.ly/1John2:1)

Jesus Christ's teaching about prayer
------------------------------------

**[MAT 6:9–6:15](https://ref.ly/Matt6:9-Matt6:15)** parallel [LUK 11:2–11:4](https://ref.ly/Luke11:2-Luke11:4) *See also* [MAT 5:44](https://ref.ly/Matt5:44), [MAT 6:5–6:8](https://ref.ly/Matt6:5-Matt6:8); [LUK 6:28](https://ref.ly/Luke6:28), [LUK 18:1–18:8](https://ref.ly/Luke18:1-Luke18:8), [LUK 18:9–18:14](https://ref.ly/Luke18:9-Luke18:14), [LUK 21:36](https://ref.ly/Luke21:36)

## 2363: Jesus Christ, preaching and teaching of (id: 2363)

A vital feature of Jesus Christ's ministry, focusing on his authoritative proclamation of the kingdom of God.

Jesus Christ's mission as preaching and teaching
------------------------------------------------

**[LUK 4:43](https://ref.ly/Luke4:43)** parallel [MRK 1:38](https://ref.ly/Mark1:38) *See also* [MAT 11:5](https://ref.ly/Matt11:5) parallel [LUK 7:22](https://ref.ly/Luke7:22); [MRK 6:6](https://ref.ly/Mark6:6); [JHN 7:16](https://ref.ly/John7:16); [ACT 1:1](https://ref.ly/Acts1:1)

Jesus Christ was regarded as a teacher and prophet
--------------------------------------------------

**[JHN 1:38](https://ref.ly/John1:38)** *“Rabbi” was an honorific title given to Jesus Christ unofficially by the people.* *See also* [MAT 16:14](https://ref.ly/Matt16:14) parallels [MRK 8:28](https://ref.ly/Mark8:28), [LUK 9:19](https://ref.ly/Luke9:19); [MAT 23:10](https://ref.ly/Matt23:10), [MAT 26:25](https://ref.ly/Matt26:25); [MRK 9:5](https://ref.ly/Mark9:5), [MRK 10:51](https://ref.ly/Mark10:51); [JHN 13:13](https://ref.ly/John13:13)

The sources of Jesus Christ's preaching and teaching
----------------------------------------------------

### Jesus Christ's words were grounded in Scripture

**[LUK 24:27](https://ref.ly/Luke24:27)** *See also* [MAT 4:4](https://ref.ly/Matt4:4) parallel [LUK 4:4](https://ref.ly/Luke4:4); [DEU 8:3](https://ref.ly/Deut8:3); [MAT 21:16](https://ref.ly/Matt21:16); [PSA 8:2](https://ref.ly/Ps8:2); [MAT 22:29–22:32](https://ref.ly/Matt22:29-Matt22:32) parallels [MRK 12:24–12:27](https://ref.ly/Mark12:24-Mark12:27), [LUK 20:35–20:38](https://ref.ly/Luke20:35-Luke20:38)

### Jesus Christ's words came from God

**[JHN 7:16](https://ref.ly/John7:16)** *See also* [JHN 3:2](https://ref.ly/John3:2), [JHN 8:28](https://ref.ly/John8:28), [JHN 12:49–12:50](https://ref.ly/John12:49-John12:50)

### Jesus Christ spoke in the power of the Spirit

**[ACT 1:2](https://ref.ly/Acts1:2)** *See also* [LUK 4:14–4:15](https://ref.ly/Luke4:14-Luke4:15); [JHN 3:34](https://ref.ly/John3:34), [JHN 6:63](https://ref.ly/John6:63)

The content of Jesus Christ's preaching and teaching
----------------------------------------------------

### The kingdom of God

**[LUK 9:11](https://ref.ly/Luke9:11)** *See also* [MAT 4:17](https://ref.ly/Matt4:17), [MAT 4:23](https://ref.ly/Matt4:23), [MAT 6:33](https://ref.ly/Matt6:33), [MAT 13:24](https://ref.ly/Matt13:24); [MRK 1:15](https://ref.ly/Mark1:15); [JHN 3:3](https://ref.ly/John3:3)

### God as Father

**[JHN 14:8–14:14](https://ref.ly/John14:8-John14:14)** *See also* [MAT 6:31–6:32](https://ref.ly/Matt6:31-Matt6:32) parallel [LUK 12:30–12:31](https://ref.ly/Luke12:30-Luke12:31); [MAT 10:32–10:33](https://ref.ly/Matt10:32-Matt10:33), [MAT 18:10](https://ref.ly/Matt18:10); [MRK 11:25](https://ref.ly/Mark11:25); [JHN 5:17–5:23](https://ref.ly/John5:17-John5:23), [JHN 8:18–8:19](https://ref.ly/John8:18-John8:19)

### Jesus Christ's own identity

**[JHN 4:25–4:26](https://ref.ly/John4:25-John4:26)** *See also* [MAT 16:13–16:17](https://ref.ly/Matt16:13-Matt16:17) parallels [MRK 8:27–8:30](https://ref.ly/Mark8:27-Mark8:30), [LUK 9:18–9:21](https://ref.ly/Luke9:18-Luke9:21); [LUK 4:20–4:21](https://ref.ly/Luke4:20-Luke4:21), [LUK 24:44](https://ref.ly/Luke24:44); [JHN 10:11](https://ref.ly/John10:11), [JHN 14:6–14:7](https://ref.ly/John14:6-John14:7)

### Jesus Christ's mission

**[MRK 9:31](https://ref.ly/Mark9:31)** parallels [MAT 17:22–17:23](https://ref.ly/Matt17:22-Matt17:23), [LUK 9:44](https://ref.ly/Luke9:44) *See also* [MAT 20:17–20:19](https://ref.ly/Matt20:17-Matt20:19) parallels [MRK 10:32–10:34](https://ref.ly/Mark10:32-Mark10:34), [LUK 18:31–18:34](https://ref.ly/Luke18:31-Luke18:34); [LUK 19:9–19:10](https://ref.ly/Luke19:9-Luke19:10), [LUK 24:46](https://ref.ly/Luke24:46); [JHN 6:51](https://ref.ly/John6:51), [JHN 10:14–10:15](https://ref.ly/John10:14-John10:15)

### How people should live

**[MAT 5:48](https://ref.ly/Matt5:48)** *See also* [MAT 5:20–5:22](https://ref.ly/Matt5:20-Matt5:22), [MAT 5:43–5:44](https://ref.ly/Matt5:43-Matt5:44), [MAT 7:12](https://ref.ly/Matt7:12), [MAT 19:21–19:24](https://ref.ly/Matt19:21-Matt19:24) parallels [MRK 10:21–10:25](https://ref.ly/Mark10:21-Mark10:25), [LUK 18:22–18:25](https://ref.ly/Luke18:22-Luke18:25); [MAT 22:35–22:40](https://ref.ly/Matt22:35-Matt22:40) parallel [MRK 12:28–12:31](https://ref.ly/Mark12:28-Mark12:31); [LUK 6:35](https://ref.ly/Luke6:35); [JHN 13:34–13:35](https://ref.ly/John13:34-John13:35), [JHN 15:12–15:13](https://ref.ly/John15:12-John15:13)

### The future

**[MRK 14:62](https://ref.ly/Mark14:62)** parallel [LUK 22:69](https://ref.ly/Luke22:69) *See also* [MAT 10:15](https://ref.ly/Matt10:15) parallel [LUK 10:12](https://ref.ly/Luke10:12); [MAT 12:36–12:37](https://ref.ly/Matt12:36-Matt12:37), [MAT 24:1–24:2](https://ref.ly/Matt24:1-Matt24:2) parallels [MRK 13:1–13:2](https://ref.ly/Mark13:1-Mark13:2), [LUK 21:5–21:6](https://ref.ly/Luke21:5-Luke21:6); [MAT 24:36–24:44](https://ref.ly/Matt24:36-Matt24:44), [MAT 25:31–25:33](https://ref.ly/Matt25:31-Matt25:33); [LUK 17:26–17:35](https://ref.ly/Luke17:26-Luke17:35)

### Jesus Christ criticised false teachings

**[MAT 15:6–15:9](https://ref.ly/Matt15:6-Matt15:9)** parallel [MRK 7:6–7:7](https://ref.ly/Mark7:6-Mark7:7) *See also* [ISA 29:13](https://ref.ly/Isa29:13); [MAT 7:15–7:16](https://ref.ly/Matt7:15-Matt7:16), [MAT 16:12](https://ref.ly/Matt16:12), [MAT 23:2–23:4](https://ref.ly/Matt23:2-Matt23:4); [MRK 12:38–12:39](https://ref.ly/Mark12:38-Mark12:39) parallel [LUK 20:45–20:46](https://ref.ly/Luke20:45-Luke20:46)

The results of Jesus Christ's preaching and teaching
----------------------------------------------------

### Jesus Christ invited a response

**[MAT 11:28–11:30](https://ref.ly/Matt11:28-Matt11:30)** *See also* [MAT 13:23](https://ref.ly/Matt13:23) parallels [MRK 4:20](https://ref.ly/Mark4:20), [LUK 8:15](https://ref.ly/Luke8:15); [MAT 22:8–22:10](https://ref.ly/Matt22:8-Matt22:10); [LUK 14:21–14:24](https://ref.ly/Luke14:21-Luke14:24); [JHN 5:24](https://ref.ly/John5:24)

### Jesus Christ looked for an obedient response

**[LUK 11:28](https://ref.ly/Luke11:28)** *See also* [MAT 7:24–7:27](https://ref.ly/Matt7:24-Matt7:27), [MAT 11:15](https://ref.ly/Matt11:15), [MAT 13:23](https://ref.ly/Matt13:23) parallels [MRK 4:20](https://ref.ly/Mark4:20), [LUK 8:15](https://ref.ly/Luke8:15); [MAT 28:20](https://ref.ly/Matt28:20); [MRK 4:9](https://ref.ly/Mark4:9); [JHN 14:23–14:24](https://ref.ly/John14:23-John14:24)

### People responded to Jesus Christ's preaching and teaching

**[JHN 12:42](https://ref.ly/John12:42)** *See also* [MAT 8:19–8:22](https://ref.ly/Matt8:19-Matt8:22) parallel [LUK 9:57–9:60](https://ref.ly/Luke9:57-Luke9:60); [MAT 13:10–13:15](https://ref.ly/Matt13:10-Matt13:15) parallel [MRK 4:10–4:12](https://ref.ly/Mark4:10-Mark4:12); [JHN 4:39](https://ref.ly/John4:39), [JHN 6:68–6:69](https://ref.ly/John6:68-John6:69)

Characteristics of Jesus Christ's preaching and teaching
--------------------------------------------------------

### It had authority

**[MAT 7:28–7:29](https://ref.ly/Matt7:28-Matt7:29)** *See also* [MAT 21:23](https://ref.ly/Matt21:23) parallels [MRK 11:28](https://ref.ly/Mark11:28), [LUK 20:2](https://ref.ly/Luke20:2); [MAT 22:22](https://ref.ly/Matt22:22) parallels [MRK 12:17](https://ref.ly/Mark12:17), [LUK 20:26](https://ref.ly/Luke20:26); [MRK 1:22](https://ref.ly/Mark1:22) parallel [LUK 4:32](https://ref.ly/Luke4:32); [MRK 1:27](https://ref.ly/Mark1:27); [JHN 7:15](https://ref.ly/John7:15)

### Jesus Christ lived out what he preached and taught

**[JHN 10:38](https://ref.ly/John10:38)** *The “miracles” (literally “works”) conveyed the same message as Jesus Christ's words.* *See also* [MAT 11:29](https://ref.ly/Matt11:29), [MAT 16:24](https://ref.ly/Matt16:24) parallels [MRK 8:34](https://ref.ly/Mark8:34), [LUK 9:23](https://ref.ly/Luke9:23); [JHN 13:15](https://ref.ly/John13:15), [JHN 13:34](https://ref.ly/John13:34)

Jesus Christ's preaching and teaching methods
---------------------------------------------

## 2366: Jesus Christ, prophecies concerning (id: 2366)

The OT points ahead to the person and ministry of Jesus Christ. Christ's fulfilment of OT prophecy is often noted by NT writers as a demonstration of God's faithfulness to his promises of salvation and as confirmation of the divine authority of Jesus Christ.

Jesus Christ fulfils OT prophecy
--------------------------------

### He fulfils the OT as a whole

**[LUK 24:27](https://ref.ly/Luke24:27)** *See also* [MAT 5:17](https://ref.ly/Matt5:17); [LUK 24:44](https://ref.ly/Luke24:44); [2CO 1:20](https://ref.ly/2Cor1:20)

### He fulfils God's promises to Abraham

**[GAL 3:14](https://ref.ly/Gal3:14)** *See also* [LUK 1:54–1:55](https://ref.ly/Luke1:54-Luke1:55), [LUK 1:72–1:74](https://ref.ly/Luke1:72-Luke1:74); [GAL 3:16](https://ref.ly/Gal3:16)

### He fulfils God's promises through the prophets

**[ACT 10:43](https://ref.ly/Acts10:43)** *See also* [MAT 26:56](https://ref.ly/Matt26:56); [ACT 3:18](https://ref.ly/Acts3:18), [ACT 3:24](https://ref.ly/Acts3:24), [ACT 13:27](https://ref.ly/Acts13:27); [ROM 1:2](https://ref.ly/Rom1:2); [1PE 1:10](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:10)

Prophecies about Jesus Christ's birth
-------------------------------------

**[MAT 1:23](https://ref.ly/Matt1:23)** *See also* [ISA 7:14](https://ref.ly/Isa7:14); [MAT 1:21](https://ref.ly/Matt1:21); [LUK 1:31–1:32](https://ref.ly/Luke1:31-Luke1:32); [ISA 9:6](https://ref.ly/Isa9:6); [MAT 2:6–2:7](https://ref.ly/Matt2:6-Matt2:7); [MIC 5:2](https://ref.ly/Mic5:2); [MAT 2:15](https://ref.ly/Matt2:15); [HOS 11:1](https://ref.ly/Hos11:1)

### He divides people and is rejected

## 2369: Jesus Christ, responses to (id: 2369)

The NT records a number of responses to Jesus Christ on the part of those who encountered him, both positive and negative.

Negative responses to Jesus Christ
----------------------------------

### Rejection

[MAT 21:42](https://ref.ly/Matt21:42); ; [MRK 7:5–7:8](https://ref.ly/Mark7:5-Mark7:8); ; [LUK 4:28–4:30](https://ref.ly/Luke4:28-Luke4:30), [LUK 10:16](https://ref.ly/Luke10:16)

### Lack of faith

**[MRK 6:4–6:6](https://ref.ly/Mark6:4-Mark6:6)** parallel [MAT 13:57–13:58](https://ref.ly/Matt13:57-Matt13:58)

### Questioning his authority

*See also* [MRK 11:27–11:33](https://ref.ly/Mark11:27-Mark11:33) parallels [MAT 21:23–21:27](https://ref.ly/Matt21:23-Matt21:27), [LUK 20:1–20:8](https://ref.ly/Luke20:1-Luke20:8)

### Hardening of hearts

[MAT 13:10–13:17](https://ref.ly/Matt13:10-Matt13:17); ; [JHN 12:37–12:41](https://ref.ly/John12:37-John12:41)

### Attributing his power to satanic forces

**[MAT 9:33–9:34](https://ref.ly/Matt9:33-Matt9:34)**

### Demanding his death

*See also* [LUK 23:20–23:24](https://ref.ly/Luke23:20-Luke23:24); [JHN 10:22–10:40](https://ref.ly/John10:22-John10:40)

## 2372: Jesus Christ, victory of (id: 2372)

Jesus Christ triumphs over and disarms all the powers of evil arrayed against him. Believers are able to share in this victory through faith in Jesus Christ.

The scope of Jesus Christ's victory
-----------------------------------

### Over temptation

**[HEB 4:15](https://ref.ly/Heb4:15)** *See also* [MAT 4:1–4:11](https://ref.ly/Matt4:1-Matt4:11) parallel [LUK 4:1–4:13](https://ref.ly/Luke4:1-Luke4:13)

### Over sin

**[ROM 5:20–5:21](https://ref.ly/Rom5:20-Rom5:21)** *See also* [1JN 3:5](https://ref.ly/1John3:5), [1JN 3:8](https://ref.ly/1John3:8)

### Over Satan

**[JHN 12:31](https://ref.ly/John12:31)** *Satan is called “the prince of this world” in John's Gospel.* *See also* [LUK 10:18–10:19](https://ref.ly/Luke10:18-Luke10:19); [JHN 14:30](https://ref.ly/John14:30), [JHN 16:11](https://ref.ly/John16:11); [HEB 2:14–2:15](https://ref.ly/Heb2:14-Heb2:15)

### Over evil spirits

[MRK 1:23–1:27](https://ref.ly/Mark1:23-Mark1:27) parallel [LUK 4:33–4:36](https://ref.ly/Luke4:33-Luke4:36)

### Over all powers

**[COL 2:15](https://ref.ly/Col2:15)** *“powers and authorities” include evil spiritual beings.* *See also* [ROM 8:38–8:39](https://ref.ly/Rom8:38-Rom8:39); [1CO 15:24–15:25](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:24-1Cor15:25); [EPH 1:21–1:22](https://ref.ly/Eph1:21-Eph1:22), [EPH 4:8](https://ref.ly/Eph4:8); [PSA 68:18](https://ref.ly/Ps68:18)

### Over the world

**[JHN 16:33](https://ref.ly/John16:33)** *Here, as elsewhere in John's Gospel, “world” refers to the human race in rebellion against God.* *See also* [2TH 2:8](https://ref.ly/2Thess2:8) *“the lawless one” represents the leader of human forces of evil*; [1JN 5:4–5:5](https://ref.ly/1John5:4-1John5:5); [REV 17:12–17:14](https://ref.ly/Rev17:12-Rev17:14), [REV 19:11–19:21](https://ref.ly/Rev19:11-Rev19:21)

### Over death

**[ROM 6:9](https://ref.ly/Rom6:9)** *See also* [ACT 2:24](https://ref.ly/Acts2:24); [1CO 15:26](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:26), [1CO 15:54–15:57](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:54-1Cor15:57); [2TI 1:10](https://ref.ly/2Tim1:10); [REV 1:18](https://ref.ly/Rev1:18)

The manner of Jesus Christ's victory
------------------------------------

### By the written word of God

[MAT 4:4–4:10](https://ref.ly/Matt4:4-Matt4:10) parallel [LUK 4:4–4:12](https://ref.ly/Luke4:4-Luke4:12)

### By his death on the cross

**[HEB 2:14](https://ref.ly/Heb2:14)** *See also* [COL 2:15](https://ref.ly/Col2:15); [REV 12:11](https://ref.ly/Rev12:11)

### By God's authority

**[LUK 11:20](https://ref.ly/Luke11:20)** parallel [MAT 12:28](https://ref.ly/Matt12:28)

### By his spoken word

**[MAT 8:16](https://ref.ly/Matt8:16)** *See also* [MAT 8:8](https://ref.ly/Matt8:8) parallel [LUK 7:7](https://ref.ly/Luke7:7); [MAT 8:13](https://ref.ly/Matt8:13)

Consequences of Jesus Christ's victory
--------------------------------------

### Assurance for believers

[JHN 16:33](https://ref.ly/John16:33); ; [1TH 4:13](https://ref.ly/1Thess4:13); ; [REV 5:5](https://ref.ly/Rev5:5)

### Victory for believers

**[1CO 15:57](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:57)** *See also* [ROM 7:21–7:25](https://ref.ly/Rom7:21-Rom7:25), [ROM 8:37](https://ref.ly/Rom8:37), [ROM 16:20](https://ref.ly/Rom16:20)

* **Associated Passages:** Hebrews 4:15; Matthew 4:1-11; Luke 4:1-13; Romans 5:20-21; 1 John 3:5; 1 John 3:8; John 12:31; Luke 10:18-19; John 14:30; John 16:11; Hebrews 2:14-15; Mark 1:23-27; Luke 4:33-36; Colossians 2:15; Romans 8:38-39; 1 Corinthians 15:24-25; Ephesians 1:21-22; Ephesians 4:8; Psalms 68:18; John 16:33; 2 Thessalonians 2:8; 1 John 5:4-5; Revelation 17:12-14; Revelation 19:11-21; Romans 6:9; Acts 2:24; 1 Corinthians 15:26; 1 Corinthians 15:54-57; 2 Timothy 1:10; Revelation 1:18; Matthew 4:4-10; Luke 4:4-12; Hebrews 2:14; Revelation 12:11; Luke 11:20; Matthew 12:28; Matthew 8:16; Matthew 8:8; Luke 7:7; Matthew 8:13; 1 Thessalonians 4:13; Revelation 5:5; 1 Corinthians 15:57; Romans 7:21-25; Romans 8:37; Romans 16:20
* **Associated Articles:** 2012: Jesus Christ, authority of (ID: `2012@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2224: Jesus Christ, the Lord (ID: `2224@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2312: Jesus Christ, as king (ID: `2312@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2321: Jesus Christ, as redeemer (ID: `2321@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2324: Jesus Christ, as Saviour (ID: `2324@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2525: Jesus Christ, cross of (ID: `2525@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2560: Jesus Christ, resurrection of (ID: `2560@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2575: Jesus Christ, temptation of (ID: `2575@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 4127: Satan, defeat of (ID: `4127@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 5596: victory (ID: `5596@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 8482: spiritual warfare (ID: `8482@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 9020: death (ID: `9020@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 2375: kingdom of God (id: 2375)

Or, less frequently, “kingdom of heaven”, the kingly rule of God in the lives of people and nations. It refers to the recognition of the authority of God, rather than a definite geographical area, and begins with the ministry of Jesus Christ.

* **Associated Articles:** 2376: kingdom of God, coming of (ID: `2376@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2377: kingdom of God, entry into (ID: `2377@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2378: kingdom of God, characteristics of (ID: `2378@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 2376: kingdom of God, coming of (id: 2376)

The kingdom of God comes into being wherever the kingly authority of God is acknowledged. Although God is always sovereign, Scripture looks to a future “realm” or “reign” of salvation. This has come in Christ and yet will come in its fulness only when Jesus Christ returns.

God is sovereign over Israel and over the whole earth
-----------------------------------------------------

**[PSA 47:7–47:8](https://ref.ly/Ps47:7-Ps47:8)** *See also* [EXO 15:18](https://ref.ly/Exod15:18); [1SA 12:12](https://ref.ly/1Sam12:12); [1CH 16:31](https://ref.ly/1Chr16:31), [1CH 28:5](https://ref.ly/1Chr28:5), [1CH 29:11–29:12](https://ref.ly/1Chr29:11-1Chr29:12); [PSA 9:7–9:8](https://ref.ly/Ps9:7-Ps9:8), [PSA 45:6](https://ref.ly/Ps45:6), [PSA 93:1–93:2](https://ref.ly/Ps93:1-Ps93:2), [PSA 103:19](https://ref.ly/Ps103:19), [PSA 145:11–145:13](https://ref.ly/Ps145:11-Ps145:13); [ISA 37:16](https://ref.ly/Isa37:16); [DAN 4:34–4:35](https://ref.ly/Dan4:34-Dan4:35)

The coming reign of God
-----------------------

### Its expectation

**[ISA 51:4–51:5](https://ref.ly/Isa51:4-Isa51:5)**; **[MRK 15:43](https://ref.ly/Mark15:43)** parallel [LUK 23:51](https://ref.ly/Luke23:51) *See also* [ISA 2:2–2:4](https://ref.ly/Isa2:2-Isa2:4) parallel [MIC 4:1–4:3](https://ref.ly/Mic4:1-Mic4:3); [ISA 32:1](https://ref.ly/Isa32:1); [JER 3:17](https://ref.ly/Jer3:17); [DAN 2:44](https://ref.ly/Dan2:44), [DAN 7:18](https://ref.ly/Dan7:18), [DAN 7:21–7:22](https://ref.ly/Dan7:21-Dan7:22), [DAN 7:27](https://ref.ly/Dan7:27); [ZEC 8:22](https://ref.ly/Zech8:22), [ZEC 14:9](https://ref.ly/Zech14:9); [MRK 11:10](https://ref.ly/Mark11:10)

### Its assocication with the coming of the Messiah

**[ISA 9:6–9:7](https://ref.ly/Isa9:6-Isa9:7)**; **[DAN 7:14](https://ref.ly/Dan7:14)** *“Son of Man” was Jesus Christ's usual way of referring to himself.* *See also* [ISA 11:1–11:9](https://ref.ly/Isa11:1-Isa11:9); [JER 23:5–23:6](https://ref.ly/Jer23:5-Jer23:6); [MIC 5:2](https://ref.ly/Mic5:2)

The kingdom of God was central in the preaching of Jesus Christ and the apostles
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**[MAT 24:14](https://ref.ly/Matt24:14)**; **[LUK 8:1](https://ref.ly/Luke8:1)**; **[ACT 28:31](https://ref.ly/Acts28:31)** *See also* [MAT 4:17](https://ref.ly/Matt4:17), [MAT 4:23](https://ref.ly/Matt4:23), [MAT 9:35](https://ref.ly/Matt9:35), [MAT 10:7](https://ref.ly/Matt10:7) *Jesus Christ's instructions to the Twelve*; [MRK 1:13–1:14](https://ref.ly/Mark1:13-Mark1:14); [LUK 4:43](https://ref.ly/Luke4:43), [LUK 9:2](https://ref.ly/Luke9:2), [LUK 9:11](https://ref.ly/Luke9:11), [LUK 10:9](https://ref.ly/Luke10:9); [ACT 1:3](https://ref.ly/Acts1:3), [ACT 1:6–1:8](https://ref.ly/Acts1:6-Acts1:8), [ACT 8:12](https://ref.ly/Acts8:12), [ACT 19:8](https://ref.ly/Acts19:8), [ACT 20:25](https://ref.ly/Acts20:25), [ACT 28:23](https://ref.ly/Acts28:23)

The kingdom of God has come in Christ: it is present
----------------------------------------------------

**[MAT 11:12](https://ref.ly/Matt11:12)** *Following the Jewish convention of avoiding the use of the divine name, Matthew usually speaks of “the kingdom of heaven”.* *See also* [MAT 3:1–3:2](https://ref.ly/Matt3:1-Matt3:2), [MAT 4:17](https://ref.ly/Matt4:17), [MAT 13:31–13:32](https://ref.ly/Matt13:31-Matt13:32) parallels [MRK 4:30–4:32](https://ref.ly/Mark4:30-Mark4:32), [LUK 13:18–13:19](https://ref.ly/Luke13:18-Luke13:19); [MAT 13:33](https://ref.ly/Matt13:33) parallel [LUK 13:20–13:21](https://ref.ly/Luke13:20-Luke13:21); [MAT 16:28](https://ref.ly/Matt16:28) parallels [MRK 9:1](https://ref.ly/Mark9:1), [LUK 9:27](https://ref.ly/Luke9:27); [LUK 11:20](https://ref.ly/Luke11:20), [LUK 16:16](https://ref.ly/Luke16:16), [LUK 17:20–17:21](https://ref.ly/Luke17:20-Luke17:21)

The kingdom of God will come in its fulness only when Jesus Christ returns: it is future
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## 2377: kingdom of God, entry into (id: 2377)

Entering or inheriting the kingdom of God is the privilege of those who acknowledge and live by the rule of God and have become part of the new order of salvation and righteousness in Christ.

Entry into the kingdom of God is of vital importance
----------------------------------------------------

### It is costly

**[MAT 13:44](https://ref.ly/Matt13:44)**; **[ACT 14:22](https://ref.ly/Acts14:22)** *See also* [MAT 8:19–8:20](https://ref.ly/Matt8:19-Matt8:20) parallel [LUK 9:57–9:58](https://ref.ly/Luke9:57-Luke9:58); [MAT 13:45–13:46](https://ref.ly/Matt13:45-Matt13:46); [LUK 18:29–18:30](https://ref.ly/Luke18:29-Luke18:30); [2TH 1:5](https://ref.ly/2Thess1:5); [REV 1:9](https://ref.ly/Rev1:9)

### It is a matter of urgency

**[LUK 9:59–9:62](https://ref.ly/Luke9:59-Luke9:62)** parallel [MAT 8:21–8:22](https://ref.ly/Matt8:21-Matt8:22)

Conditions of entry into the kingdom of God
-------------------------------------------

### Childlike trust

**[MRK 10:15](https://ref.ly/Mark10:15)** parallel [LUK 18:17](https://ref.ly/Luke18:17) *See also* [MAT 18:3](https://ref.ly/Matt18:3)

### To be born again of God's Spirit

**[JHN 3:3](https://ref.ly/John3:3)** *See also* [JHN 3:5](https://ref.ly/John3:5); [1CO 15:50](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:50)

### Obedience to God's will

**[MAT 7:21](https://ref.ly/Matt7:21)**

Warnings about entry into the kingdom of God
--------------------------------------------

### The way is narrow

**[LUK 13:24–13:28](https://ref.ly/Luke13:24-Luke13:28)** *See also* [MAT 7:13–7:14](https://ref.ly/Matt7:13-Matt7:14), [MAT 23:13](https://ref.ly/Matt23:13)

### The wicked will not inherit the kingdom

**[1CO 6:9–6:10](https://ref.ly/1Cor6:9-1Cor6:10)** *See also* [MAT 5:20](https://ref.ly/Matt5:20); [MRK 9:43–9:47](https://ref.ly/Mark9:43-Mark9:47); [GAL 5:19–5:21](https://ref.ly/Gal5:19-Gal5:21); [EPH 5:5](https://ref.ly/Eph5:5)

**[MAT 24:42–24:44](https://ref.ly/Matt24:42-Matt24:44)** *See also* [MAT 24:37–24:39](https://ref.ly/Matt24:37-Matt24:39) parallel [LUK 17:26–17:27](https://ref.ly/Luke17:26-Luke17:27); [MAT 25:13](https://ref.ly/Matt25:13); [LUK 12:35–12:40](https://ref.ly/Luke12:35-Luke12:40)

### Entry is not based on outward appearances nor granted to all who claim to know the Lord

**[MAT 7:21–7:23](https://ref.ly/Matt7:21-Matt7:23)** *See also* [MAT 13:24–13:30](https://ref.ly/Matt13:24-Matt13:30), [MAT 13:47–13:50](https://ref.ly/Matt13:47-Matt13:50); [LUK 13:25–13:27](https://ref.ly/Luke13:25-Luke13:27)

The kingdom of God is a kingdom of grace
----------------------------------------

### It belongs to those qualified by God

**[COL 1:12–1:13](https://ref.ly/Col1:12-Col1:13)** *See also* [LUK 12:32](https://ref.ly/Luke12:32), [LUK 22:29–22:30](https://ref.ly/Luke22:29-Luke22:30)

### It belongs to the poor and the poor in spirit

**[LUK 6:20](https://ref.ly/Luke6:20)** parallel [MAT 5:3](https://ref.ly/Matt5:3) *See also* [MAT 11:5](https://ref.ly/Matt11:5) parallel [LUK 7:22](https://ref.ly/Luke7:22); [MAT 19:23–19:24](https://ref.ly/Matt19:23-Matt19:24) parallels [MRK 10:23–10:25](https://ref.ly/Mark10:23-Mark10:25), [LUK 18:24–18:25](https://ref.ly/Luke18:24-Luke18:25) *It is hard for the rich to enter the kingdom of God*; [JAS 2:5](https://ref.ly/Jas2:5), [JAS 5:1](https://ref.ly/Jas5:1)

### It belongs to the childlike

**[MAT 19:14](https://ref.ly/Matt19:14)** parallels [MRK 10:14](https://ref.ly/Mark10:14), [LUK 18:16](https://ref.ly/Luke18:16)

### It belongs to sinners

**[MRK 2:17](https://ref.ly/Mark2:17)** parallels [MAT 9:12–9:13](https://ref.ly/Matt9:12-Matt9:13), [LUK 5:31–5:32](https://ref.ly/Luke5:31-Luke5:32) *See also* [MAT 21:31](https://ref.ly/Matt21:31)

### It belongs to those who are persecuted for Jesus Christ's sake

**[MAT 5:10](https://ref.ly/Matt5:10)** parallel [LUK 6:22–6:23](https://ref.ly/Luke6:22-Luke6:23)

### It belongs to Gentiles as well as to Jews

**[MAT 8:11](https://ref.ly/Matt8:11)** *See also* [MAT 21:43](https://ref.ly/Matt21:43), [MAT 22:8–22:10](https://ref.ly/Matt22:8-Matt22:10) *those initially uninvited represent the Gentiles*; [LUK 14:21–14:24](https://ref.ly/Luke14:21-Luke14:24)

* **Associated Passages:** Matthew 13:44; Acts 14:22; Matthew 8:19-20; Luke 9:57-58; Matthew 13:45-46; Luke 18:29-30; 2 Thessalonians 1:5; Revelation 1:9; Luke 9:59-62; Matthew 8:21-22; Mark 10:15; Luke 18:17; Matthew 18:3; John 3:3; John 3:5; 1 Corinthians 15:50; Matthew 7:21; Luke 13:24-28; Matthew 7:13-14; Matthew 23:13; 1 Corinthians 6:9-10; Matthew 5:20; Mark 9:43-47; Galatians 5:19-21; Ephesians 5:5; Matthew 24:42-44; Matthew 24:37-39; Luke 17:26-27; Matthew 25:13; Luke 12:35-40; Matthew 7:21-23; Matthew 13:24-30; Matthew 13:47-50; Luke 13:25-27; Colossians 1:12-13; Luke 12:32; Luke 22:29-30; Luke 6:20; Matthew 5:3; Matthew 11:5; Luke 7:22; Matthew 19:23-24; Mark 10:23-25; Luke 18:24-25; James 2:5; James 5:1; Matthew 19:14; Mark 10:14; Luke 18:16; Mark 2:17; Matthew 9:12-13; Luke 5:31-32; Matthew 21:31; Matthew 5:10; Luke 6:22-23; Matthew 8:11; Matthew 21:43; Matthew 22:8-10; Luke 14:21-24

## 2378: kingdom of God, characteristics of (id: 2378)

Those who have entered the kingdom must live according to its values, anticipating the reign of peace which will come when Jesus Christ returns.

The kingdom of God does not conform to the standards of this world
------------------------------------------------------------------

**[JHN 18:36](https://ref.ly/John18:36)**; **[ROM 14:17](https://ref.ly/Rom14:17)**

Those who inherit the kingdom of God are to bear its fruit
----------------------------------------------------------

**[1TH 2:12](https://ref.ly/1Thess2:12)** *See also* [MAT 25:34–25:36](https://ref.ly/Matt25:34-Matt25:36); [2PE 1:10–1:11](https://ref.ly/2Pet1:10-2Pet1:11)

The kingdom of God is and will be a kingdom of peace
----------------------------------------------------

### Peace between people

## 2400: Jesus Christ, gospel of (id: 2400)

* 2410: cross, the
* 2420: gospel
* **Associated Articles:** 2410: cross, the (ID: `2410@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2420: gospel (ID: `2420@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 2410: cross, the (id: 2410)

An instrument of execution, used especially by the Roman authorities for putting criminals to death. The sufferings of Jesus Christ on the cross, foreshadowed in the OT, are related in the NT gospel accounts. Scripture sees the death of Christ as central to the Christian faith. Through the cross and resurrection of Christ, God achieved the redemption of believers.

* **Associated Articles:** 2411: cross, predictions of (ID: `2411@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2412: cross, Gospel accounts of (ID: `2412@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2413: cross, of Jesus Christ (ID: `2413@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2414: cross, centrality of (ID: `2414@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 2411: cross, predictions of (id: 2411)

The death of Jesus Christ fulfils OT predictions and was clearly anticipated in his teaching.

The cross foreshadowed in the OT
--------------------------------

**[PSA 22:1](https://ref.ly/Ps22:1)** *See also* [GEN 3:15](https://ref.ly/Gen3:15); [PSA 22:6–22:7](https://ref.ly/Ps22:6-Ps22:7), [PSA 22:16–22:18](https://ref.ly/Ps22:16-Ps22:18), [PSA 31:5](https://ref.ly/Ps31:5), [PSA 69:21](https://ref.ly/Ps69:21); [ISA 52:12–52:13](https://ref.ly/Isa52:12-Isa52:13); [ZEC 12:10](https://ref.ly/Zech12:10), [ZEC 13:7](https://ref.ly/Zech13:7)

--------------------------------------------

----------------------------

**[MAT 26:12](https://ref.ly/Matt26:12)** parallel [MRK 14:8](https://ref.ly/Mark14:8) *Jesus Christ's reaction to the woman anointing him seems to suggest that he will die the death of a criminal.*

## 2412: cross, Gospel accounts of (id: 2412)

Each of the four Gospels provides a detailed account of Jesus Christ's death on the cross.

The way to the cross
--------------------

### Simon is compelled to carry the cross

**[MRK 15:21](https://ref.ly/Mark15:21)** parallels [MAT 27:32](https://ref.ly/Matt27:32), [LUK 23:26](https://ref.ly/Luke23:26)

### Women follow the cross and Jesus Christ is offered relief from pain

**[LUK 23:27–23:31](https://ref.ly/Luke23:27-Luke23:31)** *See also* [MAT 27:34](https://ref.ly/Matt27:34) parallel [MRK 15:23](https://ref.ly/Mark15:23)

The crucifixion of Jesus Christ
-------------------------------

### Jesus Christ crucified between two criminals

**[MRK 15:22–15:27](https://ref.ly/Mark15:22-Mark15:27)** parallels [MAT 27:33–27:38](https://ref.ly/Matt27:33-Matt27:38), [LUK 23:32–23:43](https://ref.ly/Luke23:32-Luke23:43) *“Golgotha” is a transliteration of the Aramaic word for “a skull”. Its actual location is uncertain.*

### The humiliation of Jesus Christ on the cross

**[MRK 15:29–15:32](https://ref.ly/Mark15:29-Mark15:32)** parallels [MAT 27:39–27:44](https://ref.ly/Matt27:39-Matt27:44), [LUK 23:35–23:39](https://ref.ly/Luke23:35-Luke23:39)

### The words of Jesus Christ on the cross

**[JHN 19:30](https://ref.ly/John19:30)** *See also* [MAT 27:46](https://ref.ly/Matt27:46) parallel [MRK 15:34](https://ref.ly/Mark15:34); [MAT 27:50](https://ref.ly/Matt27:50); [MRK 15:37](https://ref.ly/Mark15:37); [LUK 23:28–23:31](https://ref.ly/Luke23:28-Luke23:31), [LUK 23:34](https://ref.ly/Luke23:34), [LUK 23:43](https://ref.ly/Luke23:43), [LUK 23:46](https://ref.ly/Luke23:46); [JHN 19:26–19:28](https://ref.ly/John19:26-John19:28)

### The death of Jesus Christ

**[MRK 15:33–15:37](https://ref.ly/Mark15:33-Mark15:37)** parallels [MAT 27:45–27:50](https://ref.ly/Matt27:45-Matt27:50), [LUK 23:44–23:46](https://ref.ly/Luke23:44-Luke23:46) *See also* [JHN 19:28–19:35](https://ref.ly/John19:28-John19:35) *According to John, Jesus Christ was on the cross while the Passover lambs were being sacrificed.*

## 2414: cross, centrality of (id: 2414)

The death of Jesus Christ on the cross is central to the Christian faith. Through the cross and resurrection of Christ, God achieved the redemption of believers and brought hope to the world.

The gospel as the \`\`message of the cross''
--------------------------------------------

**[1CO 2:2](https://ref.ly/1Cor2:2)** *See also* [1CO 1:17–1:18](https://ref.ly/1Cor1:17-1Cor1:18), [1CO 1:23](https://ref.ly/1Cor1:23); [GAL 3:1](https://ref.ly/Gal3:1)

The cross redeems from the curse of the law
-------------------------------------------

## 2420: gospel (id: 2420)

The good news of God's redemption of sinful humanity through the life, death and resurrection of his Son Jesus Christ.

* **Associated Articles:** 2421: gospel, historical foundation of (ID: `2421@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2422: gospel, confirmation of (ID: `2422@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2423: gospel, essence of (ID: `2423@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2424: gospel, promises of (ID: `2424@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2425: gospel, requirements of (ID: `2425@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2426: gospel, responses to (ID: `2426@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2427: gospel, transmission of (ID: `2427@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2428: gospel, descriptions of (ID: `2428@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 2421: gospel, historical foundation of (id: 2421)

The gospel rests upon the history of Jesus Christ: his birth, obedient life, atoning death, physical resurrection from the dead and his ascension into heaven.

The incarnation of Jesus Christ
-------------------------------

### The historical facts

**[LUK 2:4–2:7](https://ref.ly/Luke2:4-Luke2:7)** *See also* [LUK 2:10–2:12](https://ref.ly/Luke2:10-Luke2:12); [MAT 1:20–1:21](https://ref.ly/Matt1:20-Matt1:21); [LUK 1:30–1:35](https://ref.ly/Luke1:30-Luke1:35)

### Its theological significance

**[JHN 1:14](https://ref.ly/John1:14)** *See also* [JHN 1:9](https://ref.ly/John1:9); [ROM 8:3](https://ref.ly/Rom8:3); [2CO 8:9](https://ref.ly/2Cor8:9); [GAL 4:4–4:5](https://ref.ly/Gal4:4-Gal4:5); [PHP 2:6–2:7](https://ref.ly/Phil2:6-Phil2:7); [1TI 3:16](https://ref.ly/1Tim3:16); [HEB 2:14](https://ref.ly/Heb2:14); [1JN 1:1–1:2](https://ref.ly/1John1:1-1John1:2)

## 2422: gospel, confirmation of (id: 2422)

The trustworthiness of the gospel of Jesus Christ rests upon the fulfilment of OT prophecies concerning Jesus Christ, the apostolic witness to Jesus Christ and the divine witness to Jesus Christ during his ministry, culminating in his resurrection.

Prophecies of the OT concerning Jesus Christ
--------------------------------------------

### Fulfilment of prophecy recognised by Jesus Christ

**[MAT 26:54–26:56](https://ref.ly/Matt26:54-Matt26:56)** *See also* [MAT 26:24](https://ref.ly/Matt26:24), [MAT 26:31](https://ref.ly/Matt26:31); [LUK 4:21](https://ref.ly/Luke4:21), [LUK 21:22](https://ref.ly/Luke21:22), [LUK 24:25–24:27](https://ref.ly/Luke24:25-Luke24:27), [LUK 24:44](https://ref.ly/Luke24:44), [LUK 24:46](https://ref.ly/Luke24:46); [JHN 13:18](https://ref.ly/John13:18); [PSA 41:9](https://ref.ly/Ps41:9)

### Fulfilment of prophecy recognised by NT speakers and writers

**[ROM 3:21](https://ref.ly/Rom3:21)** *See also* [LUK 1:68–1:70](https://ref.ly/Luke1:68-Luke1:70); [ACT 3:18](https://ref.ly/Acts3:18), [ACT 10:43](https://ref.ly/Acts10:43), [ACT 26:22](https://ref.ly/Acts26:22); [ROM 1:2](https://ref.ly/Rom1:2); [1CO 15:3–15:5](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:3-1Cor15:5); [1PE 1:10–1:12](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:10-1Pet1:12)MAT [1:22–1:23](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:22-1Pet1:23); [ISA 7:14](https://ref.ly/Isa7:14); [MAT 2:5–2:6](https://ref.ly/Matt2:5-Matt2:6); [MIC 5:2](https://ref.ly/Mic5:2); [MAT 2:15](https://ref.ly/Matt2:15); [HOS 11:1](https://ref.ly/Hos11:1); [MAT 2:17–2:18](https://ref.ly/Matt2:17-Matt2:18); [JER 31:15](https://ref.ly/Jer31:15); [MAT 2:23](https://ref.ly/Matt2:23), [MAT 4:14–4:16](https://ref.ly/Matt4:14-Matt4:16); [ISA 9:1–9:2](https://ref.ly/Isa9:1-Isa9:2); [MAT 8:17](https://ref.ly/Matt8:17); [ISA 53:4](https://ref.ly/Isa53:4); [MAT 12:17–12:21](https://ref.ly/Matt12:17-Matt12:21); [ISA 42:1–42:4](https://ref.ly/Isa42:1-Isa42:4); [MAT 21:4–21:5](https://ref.ly/Matt21:4-Matt21:5); [ZEC 9:9](https://ref.ly/Zech9:9); [MAT 27:9–27:10](https://ref.ly/Matt27:9-Matt27:10); [JHN 19:24](https://ref.ly/John19:24); [PSA 22:18](https://ref.ly/Ps22:18); [JHN 19:28](https://ref.ly/John19:28), [JHN 19:36](https://ref.ly/John19:36); [EXO 12:46](https://ref.ly/Exod12:46); [JHN 19:37](https://ref.ly/John19:37); [ZEC 12:10](https://ref.ly/Zech12:10); [ACT 2:25–2:28](https://ref.ly/Acts2:25-Acts2:28); [PSA 16:8–16:11](https://ref.ly/Ps16:8-Ps16:11)

### Realisation of types

The sign of Jonah: [MAT 12:38–12:41](https://ref.ly/Matt12:38-Matt12:41) parallel [LUK 11:29–11:32](https://ref.ly/Luke11:29-Luke11:32); ; [MAT 16:4](https://ref.ly/Matt16:4); [JHN 6:31–6:35](https://ref.ly/John6:31-John6:35), [JHN 6:48–6:51](https://ref.ly/John6:48-John6:51); [HEB 3:1–3:6](https://ref.ly/Heb3:1-Heb3:6) *Jesus Christ as the greater Moses*; ; [HEB 6:20–7:10](https://ref.ly/Heb6:20-Heb7:10) *Jesus Christ as the high priest after the order of Melchizedek*

## 2423: gospel, essence of (id: 2423)

The chief characteristic and fundamental doctrine of the gospel is that Jesus Christ is both Lord and Saviour.

Jesus Christ as Lord
--------------------

### The universal lordship of Jesus Christ

**[MAT 28:18](https://ref.ly/Matt28:18)** *See also* [DAN 7:13–7:14](https://ref.ly/Dan7:13-Dan7:14); [LUK 10:22](https://ref.ly/Luke10:22); [JHN 3:35](https://ref.ly/John3:35), [JHN 17:2](https://ref.ly/John17:2); [ACT 10:36](https://ref.ly/Acts10:36); [ROM 14:9](https://ref.ly/Rom14:9); [1CO 15:27](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:27); [EPH 1:20–1:22](https://ref.ly/Eph1:20-Eph1:22); [PHP 2:9–2:10](https://ref.ly/Phil2:9-Phil2:10); [COL 1:15–1:20](https://ref.ly/Col1:15-Col1:20)

### Personal implications of the lordship of Jesus Christ

**[LUK 12:8–12:9](https://ref.ly/Luke12:8-Luke12:9)**; **[ROM 10:9](https://ref.ly/Rom10:9)** *See also* [MAT 7:21–7:27](https://ref.ly/Matt7:21-Matt7:27) parallel [LUK 6:46–6:49](https://ref.ly/Luke6:46-Luke6:49); [JHN 13:13–13:14](https://ref.ly/John13:13-John13:14)

### The lordship of Jesus Christ can only be acknowledged through divine inspiration and revelation

**[1CO 12:3](https://ref.ly/1Cor12:3)** *See also* [JHN 16:13–16:15](https://ref.ly/John16:13-John16:15); [1JN 4:2–4:3](https://ref.ly/1John4:2-1John4:3)

Jesus Christ as Saviour
-----------------------

**[LUK 2:11](https://ref.ly/Luke2:11)** *See also* [JHN 1:29](https://ref.ly/John1:29), [JHN 4:42](https://ref.ly/John4:42); [ACT 5:31](https://ref.ly/Acts5:31); [1TI 2:5–2:6](https://ref.ly/1Tim2:5-1Tim2:6); [TIT 2:11–2:14](https://ref.ly/Titus2:11-Titus2:14); [1JN 4:14](https://ref.ly/1John4:14)

### Jesus Christ is the promised Messiah

**[MAT 1:20–1:23](https://ref.ly/Matt1:20-Matt1:23)** *See also* [ISA 7:14](https://ref.ly/Isa7:14); [PSA 130:8](https://ref.ly/Ps130:8); [ISA 53:11](https://ref.ly/Isa53:11); [ACT 13:23](https://ref.ly/Acts13:23)

### Jesus Christ did everything that was required to save his people

**[JHN 19:30](https://ref.ly/John19:30)** *He fulfilled all God's righteous requirements, made perfect atonement for sin and gained victory over death for all who believe in him.* *See also* [MAT 3:15](https://ref.ly/Matt3:15); [JHN 4:34](https://ref.ly/John4:34), [JHN 17:4](https://ref.ly/John17:4); [1CO 15:20–15:22](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:20-1Cor15:22)

### Salvation comes only through Jesus Christ

**[JHN 14:6](https://ref.ly/John14:6)** *See also* [ACT 4:12](https://ref.ly/Acts4:12), [ACT 10:43](https://ref.ly/Acts10:43), [ACT 16:30–16:31](https://ref.ly/Acts16:30-Acts16:31); [1TI 2:5](https://ref.ly/1Tim2:5)

### Jesus Christ will return to judge the world and bring his people to glory

**[MAT 16:27](https://ref.ly/Matt16:27)** *See also* [JHN 14:3](https://ref.ly/John14:3); [ACT 1:11](https://ref.ly/Acts1:11), [ACT 17:31](https://ref.ly/Acts17:31); [1TH 4:16–4:17](https://ref.ly/1Thess4:16-1Thess4:17); [2TI 4:1](https://ref.ly/2Tim4:1); [REV 1:7](https://ref.ly/Rev1:7), [REV 22:7](https://ref.ly/Rev22:7), [REV 22:12](https://ref.ly/Rev22:12), [REV 22:20](https://ref.ly/Rev22:20)

## 2424: gospel, promises of (id: 2424)

To all who believe and submit to its demands, the promises of the gospel include forgiveness of sins, new life in Jesus Christ and adoption into the family of God.

Forgiveness of sins
-------------------

### The sin of God's people is imputed to God's Son

**[JHN 1:29](https://ref.ly/John1:29)** *See also* [ISA 53:4–53:6](https://ref.ly/Isa53:4-Isa53:6); [LUK 24:46–24:47](https://ref.ly/Luke24:46-Luke24:47); [ACT 5:30–5:32](https://ref.ly/Acts5:30-Acts5:32), [ACT 13:38](https://ref.ly/Acts13:38); [TIT 2:13–2:14](https://ref.ly/Titus2:13-Titus2:14); [HEB 9:28](https://ref.ly/Heb9:28); [1PE 2:24](https://ref.ly/1Pet2:24)

### The righteousness of God's Son is imputed to God's people

**[ROM 1:16–1:17](https://ref.ly/Rom1:16-Rom1:17)** *See also* [ROM 3:21–3:26](https://ref.ly/Rom3:21-Rom3:26), [ROM 9:30](https://ref.ly/Rom9:30); [PHP 3:7–3:9](https://ref.ly/Phil3:7-Phil3:9)

--------------

**[ROM 5:1–5:2](https://ref.ly/Rom5:1-Rom5:2)** *See also* [JHN 14:27](https://ref.ly/John14:27); [ROM 8:1–8:4](https://ref.ly/Rom8:1-Rom8:4), [ROM 8:31–8:35](https://ref.ly/Rom8:31-Rom8:35)

## 2425: gospel, requirements of (id: 2425)

The gospel demands an obedient response to all that God has done for humanity in Jesus Christ. This includes faith in God, trust in the work of Jesus Christ, the repenting of sin, being baptised, and becoming like Christ through discipleship.

The requirement of faith
------------------------

### Belief in God

**[HEB 11:6](https://ref.ly/Heb11:6)** *See also* [JHN 10:38](https://ref.ly/John10:38), [JHN 11:25–11:27](https://ref.ly/John11:25-John11:27), [JHN 14:8–14:11](https://ref.ly/John14:8-John14:11)

### Trust in Jesus Christ

**[JHN 3:14–3:16](https://ref.ly/John3:14-John3:16)** *See also* [JHN 1:12–1:13](https://ref.ly/John1:12-John1:13), [JHN 3:36](https://ref.ly/John3:36), [JHN 7:37–7:39](https://ref.ly/John7:37-John7:39), [JHN 20:31](https://ref.ly/John20:31); [ACT 13:38–13:39](https://ref.ly/Acts13:38-Acts13:39), [ACT 16:31](https://ref.ly/Acts16:31); [ROM 3:22](https://ref.ly/Rom3:22)

The requirement of repentance
-----------------------------

### A conscious change of mind and heart

**[ACT 3:17–3:20](https://ref.ly/Acts3:17-Acts3:20)** *See also* [PSA 51:17](https://ref.ly/Ps51:17); [JER 3:12–3:13](https://ref.ly/Jer3:12-Jer3:13), [JER 6:16](https://ref.ly/Jer6:16); [LUK 18:13–18:14](https://ref.ly/Luke18:13-Luke18:14); [ACT 17:30](https://ref.ly/Acts17:30)

### Turning away from sin

**[ACT 8:22](https://ref.ly/Acts8:22)** *See also* [2CH 7:14](https://ref.ly/2Chr7:14); [PSA 34:14](https://ref.ly/Ps34:14); [ISA 59:20](https://ref.ly/Isa59:20); [JER 25:4–25:6](https://ref.ly/Jer25:4-Jer25:6)

### Turning towards God

**[ACT 20:21](https://ref.ly/Acts20:21)** *See also* [DEU 4:29–4:31](https://ref.ly/Deut4:29-Deut4:31), [DEU 30:8–30:10](https://ref.ly/Deut30:8-Deut30:10); [ISA 44:21–44:22](https://ref.ly/Isa44:21-Isa44:22), [ISA 55:6–55:7](https://ref.ly/Isa55:6-Isa55:7); [HOS 14:1–14:2](https://ref.ly/Hos14:1-Hos14:2); [JAS 4:8–4:10](https://ref.ly/Jas4:8-Jas4:10)

The requirement of baptism
--------------------------

**[ACT 2:38](https://ref.ly/Acts2:38)** *See also* [MAT 28:18–28:20](https://ref.ly/Matt28:18-Matt28:20); [ACT 8:12](https://ref.ly/Acts8:12), [ACT 8:36–8:38](https://ref.ly/Acts8:36-Acts8:38), [ACT 10:47–10:48](https://ref.ly/Acts10:47-Acts10:48), [ACT 19:1–19:5](https://ref.ly/Acts19:1-Acts19:5), [ACT 22:16](https://ref.ly/Acts22:16)

The requirement of public confession of Jesus Christ
----------------------------------------------------

**[ROM 10:9–10:10](https://ref.ly/Rom10:9-Rom10:10)** *See also* [MAT 10:32](https://ref.ly/Matt10:32) parallel [LUK 12:8–12:9](https://ref.ly/Luke12:8-Luke12:9)

## 2426: gospel, responses to (id: 2426)

The gospel cannot be subscribed to half\-heartedly or in part; it must be either accepted or rejected.

The gospel calls for a positive response
----------------------------------------

**[ROM 10:5–10:13](https://ref.ly/Rom10:5-Rom10:13)** *See also* [ACT 13:38–13:39](https://ref.ly/Acts13:38-Acts13:39), [ACT 16:29–16:32](https://ref.ly/Acts16:29-Acts16:32); [ROM 3:21–3:26](https://ref.ly/Rom3:21-Rom3:26); [JHN 6:41–6:52](https://ref.ly/John6:41-John6:52); [1JN 5:1](https://ref.ly/1John5:1), [1JN 5:5](https://ref.ly/1John5:5), [1JN 5:10–5:12](https://ref.ly/1John5:10-1John5:12)

The command to accept the gospel
--------------------------------

**[MAT 11:28](https://ref.ly/Matt11:28)**; **[ACT 17:30](https://ref.ly/Acts17:30)** *See also* [MAT 6:19–6:24](https://ref.ly/Matt6:19-Matt6:24) parallel [LUK 11:34–11:36](https://ref.ly/Luke11:34-Luke11:36); [MAT 7:7–7:12](https://ref.ly/Matt7:7-Matt7:12) parallel [LUK 11:9–11:13](https://ref.ly/Luke11:9-Luke11:13); [MAT 7:24–7:27](https://ref.ly/Matt7:24-Matt7:27) parallel [LUK 6:47–6:49](https://ref.ly/Luke6:47-Luke6:49); [JHN 4:13–4:14](https://ref.ly/John4:13-John4:14), [JHN 6:35–6:40](https://ref.ly/John6:35-John6:40), [JHN 8:31–8:32](https://ref.ly/John8:31-John8:32), [JHN 8:36](https://ref.ly/John8:36), [JHN 10:9–10:10](https://ref.ly/John10:9-John10:10), [JHN 11:25–11:26](https://ref.ly/John11:25-John11:26), [JHN 12:44–12:46](https://ref.ly/John12:44-John12:46)

Examples of people who accepted the gospel
------------------------------------------

**[MRK 1:16–1:18](https://ref.ly/Mark1:16-Mark1:18)** parallel [MAT 4:18–4:22](https://ref.ly/Matt4:18-Matt4:22) *See also* [MRK 1:19–1:20](https://ref.ly/Mark1:19-Mark1:20); [MAT 9:9](https://ref.ly/Matt9:9) parallels [MRK 2:14](https://ref.ly/Mark2:14), [LUK 5:27–5:28](https://ref.ly/Luke5:27-Luke5:28) *Matthew was also known as Levi*; [ACT 2:41](https://ref.ly/Acts2:41), [ACT 11:19–11:21](https://ref.ly/Acts11:19-Acts11:21), [ACT 13:46–13:48](https://ref.ly/Acts13:46-Acts13:48), [ACT 16:13–16:15](https://ref.ly/Acts16:13-Acts16:15)

Rejection of the gospel
-----------------------

### Through lack of perception

**[JHN 12:37–12:41](https://ref.ly/John12:37-John12:41)** *See also* [MAT 13:13–13:15](https://ref.ly/Matt13:13-Matt13:15) parallels [MRK 4:10–4:12](https://ref.ly/Mark4:10-Mark4:12), [LUK 8:9–8:10](https://ref.ly/Luke8:9-Luke8:10); [ISA 6:9](https://ref.ly/Isa6:9); [ROM 11:8](https://ref.ly/Rom11:8); [EPH 4:17–4:19](https://ref.ly/Eph4:17-Eph4:19)

### Through worldly distractions

**[MAT 13:22](https://ref.ly/Matt13:22)** parallels [MRK 4:18–4:19](https://ref.ly/Mark4:18-Mark4:19), [LUK 8:14](https://ref.ly/Luke8:14) *See also* [MAT 6:24](https://ref.ly/Matt6:24) parallel [LUK 16:13](https://ref.ly/Luke16:13); [2TI 4:10](https://ref.ly/2Tim4:10); [JAS 4:4](https://ref.ly/Jas4:4); [1JN 2:15](https://ref.ly/1John2:15)

### Through indifference

**[MAT 12:30](https://ref.ly/Matt12:30)** parallel [LUK 11:23](https://ref.ly/Luke11:23)

### Through hostility to God

**[ROM 8:6–8:8](https://ref.ly/Rom8:6-Rom8:8)** *See also* [JHN 7:13–7:20](https://ref.ly/John7:13-John7:20), [JHN 10:24–10:33](https://ref.ly/John10:24-John10:33); [ACT 4:15–4:18](https://ref.ly/Acts4:15-Acts4:18), [ACT 5:17–5:28](https://ref.ly/Acts5:17-Acts5:28), [ACT 7:51–7:53](https://ref.ly/Acts7:51-Acts7:53), [ACT 19:8–19:9](https://ref.ly/Acts19:8-Acts19:9), [ACT 21:27–21:32](https://ref.ly/Acts21:27-Acts21:32); [1TH 2:14–2:16](https://ref.ly/1Thess2:14-1Thess2:16)

## 2427: gospel, transmission of (id: 2427)

The gospel has been passed down through the NT witness to Jesus Christ, through the proclamation of the good news about Jesus Christ, and through the providential guidance of the Holy Spirit.

The NT witness to Jesus Christ
------------------------------

### The events of Jesus Christ's life were carefully recorded

**[LUK 1:1–1:4](https://ref.ly/Luke1:1-Luke1:4)** *See also* [JHN 21:24](https://ref.ly/John21:24); [ACT 1:1–1:2](https://ref.ly/Acts1:1-Acts1:2)

The apostles bore witness to the gospel
---------------------------------------

**[1CO 15:3–15:8](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:3-1Cor15:8)**; **[2PE 1:16](https://ref.ly/2Pet1:16)**; **[1JN 1:1–1:4](https://ref.ly/1John1:1-1John1:4)** *See also* [LUK 24:45–24:48](https://ref.ly/Luke24:45-Luke24:48); [JHN 15:27](https://ref.ly/John15:27); [ACT 1:8](https://ref.ly/Acts1:8), [ACT 1:21–1:22](https://ref.ly/Acts1:21-Acts1:22), [ACT 2:32](https://ref.ly/Acts2:32), [ACT 4:1–4:20](https://ref.ly/Acts4:1-Acts4:20), [ACT 5:32](https://ref.ly/Acts5:32), [ACT 13:30–13:31](https://ref.ly/Acts13:30-Acts13:31); [HEB 2:3–2:4](https://ref.ly/Heb2:3-Heb2:4); [1PE 5:1](https://ref.ly/1Pet5:1); [1JN 4:14](https://ref.ly/1John4:14)

The proclamation of the gospel
------------------------------

**[ACT 5:42](https://ref.ly/Acts5:42)**; **[ROM 10:14–10:15](https://ref.ly/Rom10:14-Rom10:15)**; **[1CO 15:1–15:2](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:1-1Cor15:2)**; **[EPH 3:8–3:9](https://ref.ly/Eph3:8-Eph3:9)** *See also* [ACT 8:12](https://ref.ly/Acts8:12); [1CO 1:21](https://ref.ly/1Cor1:21); [GAL 1:23](https://ref.ly/Gal1:23); [2TI 4:2](https://ref.ly/2Tim4:2); [HEB 13:7](https://ref.ly/Heb13:7)

The guidance of the Holy Spirit in the transmission of the gospel
-----------------------------------------------------------------

**[JHN 14:26](https://ref.ly/John14:26), [JHN 15:26](https://ref.ly/John15:26)** *See also* [JHN 16:12–16:15](https://ref.ly/John16:12-John16:15); [ACT 5:32](https://ref.ly/Acts5:32); [HEB 2:3–2:4](https://ref.ly/Heb2:3-Heb2:4); [1JN 5:6](https://ref.ly/1John5:6)

## 2428: gospel, descriptions of (id: 2428)

The beauty, authority and importance of the gospel can be seen from the way it is described in Scripture.

In the Gospels
--------------

### As good and joyful news

**[MAT 4:23](https://ref.ly/Matt4:23)** *See also* [MRK 1:14](https://ref.ly/Mark1:14), [MRK 16:15](https://ref.ly/Mark16:15); [LUK 2:10–2:11](https://ref.ly/Luke2:10-Luke2:11)

### As being of heavenly origin

**[JHN 17:16–17:18](https://ref.ly/John17:16-John17:18)** *See also* [JHN 8:28](https://ref.ly/John8:28), [JHN 12:49–12:50](https://ref.ly/John12:49-John12:50), [JHN 14:10](https://ref.ly/John14:10), [JHN 14:24](https://ref.ly/John14:24)

### As words of life

**[JHN 6:63](https://ref.ly/John6:63)** *See also* [JHN 3:11–3:15](https://ref.ly/John3:11-John3:15)

### As being complete and gloriously rich

**[COL 1:25–1:27](https://ref.ly/Col1:25-Col1:27)** *See also* [ROM 10:12–10:13](https://ref.ly/Rom10:12-Rom10:13); [EPH 3:8](https://ref.ly/Eph3:8)

---------

---------

## 2505: Jesus Christ, ascension of (id: 2505)

The return of Jesus Christ to his Father in order to establish his kingdom, having completed his work on earth.

Jesus Christ's ascension described
----------------------------------

**[ACT 1:9–1:11](https://ref.ly/Acts1:9-Acts1:11)** *As in the OT, the cloud symbolises God's presence.* *See also* [MRK 16:19](https://ref.ly/Mark16:19); [LUK 24:51](https://ref.ly/Luke24:51); [ACT 1:2](https://ref.ly/Acts1:2); [EPH 4:10](https://ref.ly/Eph4:10); [1TI 3:16](https://ref.ly/1Tim3:16); [HEB 9:24](https://ref.ly/Heb9:24); [1PE 3:22](https://ref.ly/1Pet3:22); [REV 12:5](https://ref.ly/Rev12:5)

Predictions of Jesus Christ's ascension
---------------------------------------

### In the OT

**[EPH 4:7–4:8](https://ref.ly/Eph4:7-Eph4:8)** *See also* [PSA 68:18](https://ref.ly/Ps68:18)

### Jesus Christ looks forward to his ascension as his return to his Father

**[JHN 16:28](https://ref.ly/John16:28)** *See also* [JHN 6:62](https://ref.ly/John6:62), [JHN 7:33](https://ref.ly/John7:33), [JHN 14:28](https://ref.ly/John14:28), [JHN 16:5](https://ref.ly/John16:5), [JHN 16:10](https://ref.ly/John16:10), [JHN 17:11](https://ref.ly/John17:11), [JHN 17:13](https://ref.ly/John17:13), [JHN 20:17](https://ref.ly/John20:17)

Jesus Christ establishes his kingdom by his ascension
-----------------------------------------------------

### He ascended to send the Holy Spirit

**[JHN 16:7](https://ref.ly/John16:7)** *See also* [JHN 7:39](https://ref.ly/John7:39), [JHN 14:16–14:19](https://ref.ly/John14:16-John14:19), [JHN 14:25–14:26](https://ref.ly/John14:25-John14:26), [JHN 15:26–15:27](https://ref.ly/John15:26-John15:27); [ACT 2:33](https://ref.ly/Acts2:33)

### He ascended to prepare a place for his people

**[JHN 14:2–14:4](https://ref.ly/John14:2-John14:4)**

### He ascended to exaltation and glory

*See also* [LUK 24:26](https://ref.ly/Luke24:26); [ACT 2:33](https://ref.ly/Acts2:33); [EPH 1:20–1:21](https://ref.ly/Eph1:20-Eph1:21); [1PE 3:22](https://ref.ly/1Pet3:22)

### He ascended to exercise his high priestly ministry

**[HEB 4:14](https://ref.ly/Heb4:14)** *See also* [HEB 7:25](https://ref.ly/Heb7:25), [HEB 9:24](https://ref.ly/Heb9:24)

### He ascended so that believers may follow him

**[1TH 4:17](https://ref.ly/1Thess4:17)**

Jesus Christ's ascension indicates the manner of his return
-----------------------------------------------------------

**[ACT 1:11](https://ref.ly/Acts1:11)** *See also* [MAT 24:30](https://ref.ly/Matt24:30) parallels [MRK 13:26](https://ref.ly/Mark13:26), [LUK 21:27](https://ref.ly/Luke21:27); [REV 1:7](https://ref.ly/Rev1:7)
