## 2510: Jesus Christ, baptism of (id: 2510)

In obedience to God's will Jesus Christ was baptised in the River Jordan by John. The event was sealed by the descent of the Holy Spirit and the Father's voice of approval.

John tries to prevent Jesus Christ from being baptised
------------------------------------------------------

**[MAT 3:13–3:14](https://ref.ly/Matt3:13-Matt3:14)** *John was baptising repentant sinners but he knew that Jesus Christ was sinless.*

The necessity of Jesus Christ's baptism
---------------------------------------

**[MAT 3:15](https://ref.ly/Matt3:15)** *See also* [MRK 10:38](https://ref.ly/Mark10:38); [LUK 12:50](https://ref.ly/Luke12:50)

The events surrounding Jesus Christ's baptism
---------------------------------------------

### The baptism itself

**[MRK 1:9](https://ref.ly/Mark1:9)** parallels [MAT 3:13](https://ref.ly/Matt3:13), [LUK 3:21](https://ref.ly/Luke3:21)

### Jesus Christ prays while being baptised

**[LUK 3:21](https://ref.ly/Luke3:21)**

### The Holy Spirit descends on Jesus Christ

**[MRK 1:10](https://ref.ly/Mark1:10)** parallels [MAT 3:16](https://ref.ly/Matt3:16), [LUK 3:22](https://ref.ly/Luke3:22) *The Holy Spirit came upon Jesus Christ to equip him for his ministry which was about to begin and to give him strength at a time of temptation.* *See also* [JHN 1:32–1:34](https://ref.ly/John1:32-John1:34)

### The voice of the Father is heard

**[MAT 3:17](https://ref.ly/Matt3:17)** parallels [MRK 1:11](https://ref.ly/Mark1:11), [LUK 3:22](https://ref.ly/Luke3:22) *These words, which are an allusion to [Ps 2:7](https://ref.ly/Ps2:7) and [Isa 42:1](https://ref.ly/Isa42:1), were repeated at the transfiguration.* *See also* [MAT 17:5](https://ref.ly/Matt17:5) parallels [MRK 9:7](https://ref.ly/Mark9:7), [LUK 9:35](https://ref.ly/Luke9:35)

* **Associated Passages:** Matthew 3:13-14; Matthew 3:15; Mark 10:38; Luke 12:50; Mark 1:9; Matthew 3:13; Luke 3:21; Mark 1:10; Matthew 3:16; Luke 3:22; John 1:32-34; Matthew 3:17; Mark 1:11; Psalms 2:7; Isaiah 42:1; Matthew 17:5; Mark 9:7; Luke 9:35
* **Associated Articles:** 1040: God, fatherhood of (ID: `1040@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 1510: Trinity, the (ID: `1510@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2057: Jesus Christ, obedience of (ID: `2057@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2075: Jesus Christ, sinlessness of (ID: `2075@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2078: Jesus Christ, sonship of (ID: `2078@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2360: Jesus Christ, prayers of (ID: `2360@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2575: Jesus Christ, temptation of (ID: `2575@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 3269: Holy Spirit, in life of Jesus Christ (ID: `3269@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 5196: voice (ID: `5196@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6752: substitution (ID: `6752@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 7903: baptism (ID: `7903@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 2515: Jesus Christ, birth of (id: 2515)

Jesus Christ was born to a poor unmarried Jewish couple in the village of Bethlehem. As Son of God, he was conceived by the Holy Spirit in the womb of his mother Mary.

Jesus Christ's birth is prophesied in the OT
--------------------------------------------

### The prophecy of a coming ruler

**[ISA 9:6–9:7](https://ref.ly/Isa9:6-Isa9:7)**

### The prophecy of a virgin's son

**[ISA 7:14](https://ref.ly/Isa7:14)**

### The prophecy concerning his birthplace

**[MIC 5:2](https://ref.ly/Mic5:2)** *“Bethlehem Ephrathah” is the village where David grew up (“the town of David”).*

Jesus Christ was conceived by the Holy Spirit and born of a virgin
------------------------------------------------------------------

**[MAT 1:18](https://ref.ly/Matt1:18), [MAT 1:23](https://ref.ly/Matt1:23)** *See also* [MAT 1:20](https://ref.ly/Matt1:20); [LUK 1:34–1:35](https://ref.ly/Luke1:34-Luke1:35)

## 2520: Jesus Christ, childhood of (id: 2520)

As an infant Jesus Christ was consecrated in the temple, accompanied by prophetic utterances regarding his future ministry. His childhood was characterised by a growth in wisdom and grace and, in particular, a strong desire to learn of God his Father and to understand the Scriptures.

Jesus Christ was consecrated as an infant
-----------------------------------------

**[LUK 2:22](https://ref.ly/Luke2:22)** *See also* [LUK 2:23–2:24](https://ref.ly/Luke2:23-Luke2:24)

## 2525: Jesus Christ, cross of (id: 2525)

The death of Jesus Christ is of central importance to the Christian faith. Through Christ's death, sinners are reconciled to God and to their fellow human beings. Paul summarises the gospel as “the message of the cross”.

Jesus Christ foretold his death on the cross
--------------------------------------------

**[MAT 20:18–20:19](https://ref.ly/Matt20:18-Matt20:19)** parallels [MRK 10:33–10:34](https://ref.ly/Mark10:33-Mark10:34), [LUK 18:31–18:32](https://ref.ly/Luke18:31-Luke18:32) *See also* [MAT 26:2](https://ref.ly/Matt26:2); [JHN 3:14–3:15](https://ref.ly/John3:14-John3:15), [JHN 8:28](https://ref.ly/John8:28), [JHN 12:32–12:33](https://ref.ly/John12:32-John12:33), [JHN 18:32](https://ref.ly/John18:32)

The facts of Jesus Christ's death on the cross
----------------------------------------------

### Carrying Jesus Christ's cross

**[JHN 19:17](https://ref.ly/John19:17)** *Though Jesus Christ began to carry his cross, the Romans soon forced Simon of Cyrene to continue with it.* *See also* [MAT 27:32](https://ref.ly/Matt27:32) parallels [MRK 15:21](https://ref.ly/Mark15:21), [LUK 23:26](https://ref.ly/Luke23:26)

### Jesus Christ refused the comfort of wine, which would have lessened the pains of his suffering

[MAT 27:34](https://ref.ly/Matt27:34) parallel [MRK 15:23](https://ref.ly/Mark15:23)

### Jesus Christ was nailed to the cross

**[LUK 23:33](https://ref.ly/Luke23:33)** parallels [MAT 27:35](https://ref.ly/Matt27:35), [MRK 15:24–15:25](https://ref.ly/Mark15:24-Mark15:25), [JHN 19:18](https://ref.ly/John19:18)

### Jesus Christ's words from the cross

*See also* [LUK 23:34](https://ref.ly/Luke23:34), [LUK 23:43](https://ref.ly/Luke23:43); [JHN 19:26–19:27](https://ref.ly/John19:26-John19:27); [MAT 27:46](https://ref.ly/Matt27:46) parallel [MRK 15:34](https://ref.ly/Mark15:34); [PSA 22:1](https://ref.ly/Ps22:1); [LUK 23:46](https://ref.ly/Luke23:46); [JHN 19:28–19:30](https://ref.ly/John19:28-John19:30)

### Signs accompanying Jesus Christ's death on the cross

Darkness over the whole land for three hours: [MAT 27:45](https://ref.ly/Matt27:45); ; [MRK 15:33](https://ref.ly/Mark15:33) parallel [LUK 23:44–23:45](https://ref.ly/Luke23:44-Luke23:45); [MAT 27:51](https://ref.ly/Matt27:51) parallels [MRK 15:38](https://ref.ly/Mark15:38), [LUK 23:45](https://ref.ly/Luke23:45); ; [MAT 27:52–27:53](https://ref.ly/Matt27:52-Matt27:53) *the dead come back to life*

## 2530: Jesus Christ, death of (id: 2530)

The death of Jesus Christ by crucifixion is of central importance to the NT. Through the faithful, obedient death of Christ, God grants sinners forgiveness and eternal life. The Christian sacraments of baptism and the Lord's Supper focus upon the death of Christ.

Jesus Christ's death was foretold
---------------------------------

### In time and in eternity

**[REV 13:8](https://ref.ly/Rev13:8)** *See also* [ISA 53:10–53:12](https://ref.ly/Isa53:10-Isa53:12); [ZEC 12:10](https://ref.ly/Zech12:10); [JHN 1:29](https://ref.ly/John1:29), [JHN 1:36](https://ref.ly/John1:36)

### By Jesus Christ himself

**[MAT 16:21](https://ref.ly/Matt16:21)** parallels [MRK 8:31](https://ref.ly/Mark8:31), [LUK 9:22](https://ref.ly/Luke9:22) *See also* [MAT 17:22–17:23](https://ref.ly/Matt17:22-Matt17:23), [MAT 26:12](https://ref.ly/Matt26:12) parallel [JHN 12:7](https://ref.ly/John12:7); [JHN 16:16](https://ref.ly/John16:16), [JHN 16:28](https://ref.ly/John16:28), [JHN 18:4](https://ref.ly/John18:4)

### Jesus Christ willingly planned to give his life

**[JHN 10:11](https://ref.ly/John10:11)** *See also* [JHN 10:15](https://ref.ly/John10:15), [JHN 10:17–10:18](https://ref.ly/John10:17-John10:18), [JHN 13:1](https://ref.ly/John13:1), [JHN 15:13](https://ref.ly/John15:13); [1JN 3:16](https://ref.ly/1John3:16)

Plots to kill Jesus Christ
--------------------------

**[MRK 3:6](https://ref.ly/Mark3:6)** parallel [MAT 12:14](https://ref.ly/Matt12:14) *See also* [MAT 26:4](https://ref.ly/Matt26:4) parallel [MRK 14:1](https://ref.ly/Mark14:1); [LUK 13:31](https://ref.ly/Luke13:31), [LUK 19:47](https://ref.ly/Luke19:47); [JHN 5:18](https://ref.ly/John5:18), [JHN 7:25](https://ref.ly/John7:25), [JHN 8:37](https://ref.ly/John8:37), [JHN 8:40](https://ref.ly/John8:40)

The manner of Jesus Christ's death
----------------------------------

### Jesus Christ died by crucifixion

**[LUK 23:33](https://ref.ly/Luke23:33)** parallels [MAT 27:35](https://ref.ly/Matt27:35), [MRK 15:24–15:25](https://ref.ly/Mark15:24-Mark15:25)

### The moment of death

**[MRK 15:37](https://ref.ly/Mark15:37)** parallels [MAT 27:50](https://ref.ly/Matt27:50), [LUK 23:46](https://ref.ly/Luke23:46), [JHN 19:30](https://ref.ly/John19:30) *See also* [JHN 19:33](https://ref.ly/John19:33)

### Events accompanying Jesus Christ's death

[MAT 27:45](https://ref.ly/Matt27:45) *Darkness descended on the land*; ; [MAT 27:51](https://ref.ly/Matt27:51) *The curtain of the temple was split*; ; [MAT 27:52–27:53](https://ref.ly/Matt27:52-Matt27:53) *The dead emerged from their tombs.*

### Jesus Christ's burial

**[MAT 27:58–27:60](https://ref.ly/Matt27:58-Matt27:60)** parallels [MRK 15:43–15:46](https://ref.ly/Mark15:43-Mark15:46), [LUK 23:51–23:53](https://ref.ly/Luke23:51-Luke23:53), [JHN 19:38–19:42](https://ref.ly/John19:38-John19:42)

The unique character of Jesus Christ's death
--------------------------------------------

### Jesus Christ's body did not decay

**[ACT 2:31](https://ref.ly/Acts2:31)** *See also* [PSA 16:10](https://ref.ly/Ps16:10); [ACT 2:27](https://ref.ly/Acts2:27), [ACT 13:36–13:37](https://ref.ly/Acts13:36-Acts13:37)

### Jesus Christ descended to the dead

**[ROM 1:4](https://ref.ly/Rom1:4)** *See also* [1PE 3:18–3:22](https://ref.ly/1Pet3:18-1Pet3:22)

### Jesus Christ was raised bodily from the dead

**[LUK 24:36–24:40](https://ref.ly/Luke24:36-Luke24:40)** *See also* [JHN 21:12–21:13](https://ref.ly/John21:12-John21:13); [ACT 10:41](https://ref.ly/Acts10:41), [ACT 25:19](https://ref.ly/Acts25:19)

### Death had no power over Jesus Christ

**[ACT 2:24](https://ref.ly/Acts2:24)** *See also* [ROM 6:9–6:10](https://ref.ly/Rom6:9-Rom6:10); [REV 1:18](https://ref.ly/Rev1:18)

### Jesus Christ's death was a unique sacrifice

**[HEB 7:27](https://ref.ly/Heb7:27)** *See also* [1CO 5:7](https://ref.ly/1Cor5:7); [EPH 5:2](https://ref.ly/Eph5:2); [HEB 9:26](https://ref.ly/Heb9:26), [HEB 9:28](https://ref.ly/Heb9:28), [HEB 10:10](https://ref.ly/Heb10:10), [HEB 10:12](https://ref.ly/Heb10:12); [1JN 2:2](https://ref.ly/1John2:2), [1JN 4:10](https://ref.ly/1John4:10)

Achievements of Jesus Christ's death
------------------------------------

### Jesus Christ's death establishes the new covenant

**[LUK 22:20](https://ref.ly/Luke22:20)** parallels [MAT 26:28](https://ref.ly/Matt26:28), [MRK 14:24](https://ref.ly/Mark14:24), [1CO 11:25](https://ref.ly/1Cor11:25) *See also* [HEB 9:15](https://ref.ly/Heb9:15), [HEB 13:20](https://ref.ly/Heb13:20)

### Jesus Christ's death is a victory

**[COL 2:14–2:15](https://ref.ly/Col2:14-Col2:15)** *See also* [HEB 2:9](https://ref.ly/Heb2:9), [HEB 2:14–2:15](https://ref.ly/Heb2:14-Heb2:15); [REV 12:11](https://ref.ly/Rev12:11)

### Jesus Christ's death brings redemption

**[REV 5:9](https://ref.ly/Rev5:9)** *See also* [MRK 10:45](https://ref.ly/Mark10:45) parallel [MAT 20:28](https://ref.ly/Matt20:28); [ACT 20:28](https://ref.ly/Acts20:28); [GAL 3:13](https://ref.ly/Gal3:13); [EPH 1:7](https://ref.ly/Eph1:7); [TIT 2:14](https://ref.ly/Titus2:14); [1PE 1:18–1:19](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:18-1Pet1:19)

### Jesus Christ's death brings forgiveness and cleansing

**[1JN 1:7](https://ref.ly/1John1:7)** *See also* [HEB 9:14](https://ref.ly/Heb9:14); [REV 1:5](https://ref.ly/Rev1:5), [REV 7:14](https://ref.ly/Rev7:14)

### Jesus Christ's death brings sanctification

**[HEB 13:12](https://ref.ly/Heb13:12)** *See also* [HEB 10:14](https://ref.ly/Heb10:14); [1PE 1:2](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:2)

-------------------------------------------------

## 2535: Jesus Christ, family of (id: 2535)

Jesus Christ belonged to a human family and experienced family relationships during his earthly ministry. Such relationships underline the fact of Christ's humanity.

Jesus Christ was born into a family
-----------------------------------

### He is placed in a family tree

[MAT 1:1–1:17](https://ref.ly/Matt1:1-Matt1:17); ; [LUK 1:34–1:37](https://ref.ly/Luke1:34-Luke1:37), [LUK 3:23–3:38](https://ref.ly/Luke3:23-Luke3:38)

### His birth was a natural one

**[LUK 2:5–2:7](https://ref.ly/Luke2:5-Luke2:7)** *Jesus Christ's conception was miraculous, his birth natural.* *See also* [LUK 2:21–2:22](https://ref.ly/Luke2:21-Luke2:22) *see [Lev 12:2–4](https://ref.ly/Lev12:2-Lev12:4) for the instructions concerning purification after childbirth*

### He grew up within a family

**[LUK 2:48](https://ref.ly/Luke2:48)** *See also* [LUK 2:51–2:52](https://ref.ly/Luke2:51-Luke2:52)

Jesus Christ's family is mentioned during his earthly ministry
--------------------------------------------------------------

**[MAT 13:55–13:56](https://ref.ly/Matt13:55-Matt13:56)** parallel [MRK 6:3](https://ref.ly/Mark6:3) *See also* [MAT 12:46–12:47](https://ref.ly/Matt12:46-Matt12:47) parallels [MRK 3:31–3:32](https://ref.ly/Mark3:31-Mark3:32), [LUK 8:19–8:20](https://ref.ly/Luke8:19-Luke8:20); [JHN 2:1](https://ref.ly/John2:1), [JHN 2:12](https://ref.ly/John2:12)

Jesus Christ's natural brothers
-------------------------------

### James

**[GAL 1:19](https://ref.ly/Gal1:19)** *This verse gives support to the traditional view that James, elder at Jerusalem and writer of the NT letter which bears his name was the Lord's brother. (Other references to him include [Ac 15:13](https://ref.ly/Acts15:13); [21:18](https://ref.ly/Acts21:18); [1Co 15:7](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:7); [Jas 1:1](https://ref.ly/Jas1:1).).* *See also* [MAT 13:55](https://ref.ly/Matt13:55) parallel [MRK 6:3](https://ref.ly/Mark6:3)

### Jude

**[JUD 1:1](https://ref.ly/Jude1:1)** *See also* [MAT 13:55](https://ref.ly/Matt13:55) parallel [MRK 6:3](https://ref.ly/Mark6:3) *Jude is understood to be a variation of Judas.*

The nature of Jesus Christ's relationships with his family
----------------------------------------------------------

### He was obedient to and caring towards his parents

**[LUK 2:51](https://ref.ly/Luke2:51)** *See also* [JHN 19:26–19:27](https://ref.ly/John19:26-John19:27)

### The will of his heavenly Father took precedence over the wishes of his natural family

**[JHN 2:3–2:4](https://ref.ly/John2:3-John2:4)** *In John's Gospel, Jesus Christ's “time” (or “hour”) is his cross. Here Christ insists that only his heavenly Father can dictate the course of his ministry.* *See also* [MAT 12:48–12:50](https://ref.ly/Matt12:48-Matt12:50) parallel [MRK 3:33–3:35](https://ref.ly/Mark3:33-Mark3:35); [LUK 2:48–2:49](https://ref.ly/Luke2:48-Luke2:49); [JHN 7:6–7:8](https://ref.ly/John7:6-John7:8)

### His family did not fully understand his ministry

**[JHN 7:3–7:5](https://ref.ly/John7:3-John7:5)** *See also* [MRK 3:21](https://ref.ly/Mark3:21)

### Jesus Christ's natural family were among the first Christians

**[ACT 1:14](https://ref.ly/Acts1:14)** *See also* [1CO 9:5](https://ref.ly/1Cor9:5)

* **Associated Passages:** Matthew 1:1-17; Luke 1:34-37; Luke 3:23-38; Luke 2:5-7; Luke 2:21-22; Leviticus 12:2-4; Luke 2:48; Luke 2:51-52; Matthew 13:55-56; Mark 6:3; Matthew 12:46-47; Mark 3:31-32; Luke 8:19-20; John 2:1; John 2:12; Galatians 1:19; Acts 15:13; Acts 21:18; 1 Corinthians 15:7; James 1:1; Matthew 13:55; Jude 1:1; Luke 2:51; John 19:26-27; John 2:3-4; Matthew 12:48-50; Mark 3:33-35; Luke 2:48-49; John 7:6-8; John 7:3-5; Mark 3:21; Acts 1:14; 1 Corinthians 9:5
* **Associated Articles:** 2033: Jesus Christ, humanity of (ID: `2033@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2057: Jesus Christ, obedience of (ID: `2057@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2515: Jesus Christ, birth of (ID: `2515@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2520: Jesus Christ, childhood of (ID: `2520@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2540: Jesus Christ, genealogy of (ID: `2540@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 5099: Mary, mother of Jesus Christ (ID: `5099@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 5680: family (ID: `5680@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 2540: Jesus Christ, genealogy of (id: 2540)

Jesus Christ's human ancestry is traced back in two separate lines to David and thence back to Adam. Jesus' descent from David is of importance for his Messianic claims.

Jesus Christ is descended from Adam
-----------------------------------

[LUK 3:23–3:38](https://ref.ly/Luke3:23-Luke3:38)

Jesus Christ is descended from Abraham
--------------------------------------

**[GAL 3:16](https://ref.ly/Gal3:16)** *See also* [ACT 3:25–3:26](https://ref.ly/Acts3:25-Acts3:26)

Jesus Christ is descended from Isaac
------------------------------------

[GEN 21:12](https://ref.ly/Gen21:12), [GEN 26:2–26:4](https://ref.ly/Gen26:2-Gen26:4); ; [GAL 3:16](https://ref.ly/Gal3:16)

Jesus Christ is descended from Jacob
------------------------------------

[GEN 28:13–28:14](https://ref.ly/Gen28:13-Gen28:14); ; [MAT 1:2](https://ref.ly/Matt1:2); ; [LUK 3:34](https://ref.ly/Luke3:34)

Jesus Christ is descended from the tribe of Judah
-------------------------------------------------

**[HEB 7:14](https://ref.ly/Heb7:14)** *See also* [RUT 4:18–4:22](https://ref.ly/Ruth4:18-Ruth4:22)

Jesus Christ is descended from Jesse
------------------------------------

**[ISA 11:1](https://ref.ly/Isa11:1)**; **[ROM 15:12](https://ref.ly/Rom15:12)**

Jesus Christ is descended from David
------------------------------------

### Jesus Christ's human lineage

**[MAT 1:1–1:17](https://ref.ly/Matt1:1-Matt1:17)**; **[LUK 2:4](https://ref.ly/Luke2:4)** *See also* [1CH 3:10–3:19](https://ref.ly/1Chr3:10-1Chr3:19); [LUK 3:23–3:31](https://ref.ly/Luke3:23-Luke3:31)

### Jesus Christ as the Son of David

**[REV 22:16](https://ref.ly/Rev22:16)** *See also* [MAT 1:20](https://ref.ly/Matt1:20), [MAT 20:30–20:31](https://ref.ly/Matt20:30-Matt20:31) parallels [MRK 10:47–10:48](https://ref.ly/Mark10:47-Mark10:48), [LUK 18:38–18:39](https://ref.ly/Luke18:38-Luke18:39); [MAT 21:9](https://ref.ly/Matt21:9), [MAT 21:15](https://ref.ly/Matt21:15); [LUK 1:27](https://ref.ly/Luke1:27), [LUK 1:32](https://ref.ly/Luke1:32); [JHN 7:42](https://ref.ly/John7:42)

### Jesus Christ is greater than David

**[MAT 22:41–22:45](https://ref.ly/Matt22:41-Matt22:45)** parallels [MRK 12:35–12:37](https://ref.ly/Mark12:35-Mark12:37), [LUK 20:41–20:44](https://ref.ly/Luke20:41-Luke20:44) *See also* [PSA 110:1](https://ref.ly/Ps110:1); [REV 5:5](https://ref.ly/Rev5:5), [REV 22:16](https://ref.ly/Rev22:16)

### Jesus Christ is greater than Solomon

**[MAT 12:42](https://ref.ly/Matt12:42)** parallel [LUK 11:31](https://ref.ly/Luke11:31)

Jesus Christ as the son of Joseph and Mary
------------------------------------------

**[MAT 13:55](https://ref.ly/Matt13:55)** parallel [MRK 6:3](https://ref.ly/Mark6:3)**[JHN 6:42](https://ref.ly/John6:42)** *See also* [MAT 1:16](https://ref.ly/Matt1:16); [LUK 4:22](https://ref.ly/Luke4:22); [JHN 1:45](https://ref.ly/John1:45)

## 2545: Jesus Christ, opposition to (id: 2545)

Jesus Christ encountered criticism, grumbling and plotting because he was seen as a threat to the religious and political hierarchy, and because he exposed sin.

Opposition by different groups
------------------------------

### By family and friends

**[LUK 4:24–4:29](https://ref.ly/Luke4:24-Luke4:29)** *See also* [MAT 13:55–13:57](https://ref.ly/Matt13:55-Matt13:57) parallel [MRK 6:3–6:4](https://ref.ly/Mark6:3-Mark6:4); [MRK 3:21](https://ref.ly/Mark3:21); [JHN 7:3–7:5](https://ref.ly/John7:3-John7:5)

### By religious leaders

**[MAT 12:14](https://ref.ly/Matt12:14)** parallels [MRK 3:6](https://ref.ly/Mark3:6), [LUK 6:11](https://ref.ly/Luke6:11) *See also* [JHN 11:47–11:53](https://ref.ly/John11:47-John11:53)

### By political leaders

[MAT 2:13–2:14](https://ref.ly/Matt2:13-Matt2:14); ; [LUK 13:31](https://ref.ly/Luke13:31)

Opposition through criticism and accusation
-------------------------------------------

### Criticism of Jesus Christ's choice of company

**[MAT 9:11](https://ref.ly/Matt9:11)** parallels [MRK 2:16](https://ref.ly/Mark2:16), [LUK 5:30](https://ref.ly/Luke5:30) *See also* [LUK 7:39](https://ref.ly/Luke7:39), [LUK 19:7](https://ref.ly/Luke19:7)

### Criticism for breaking with tradition

[MAT 15:1–15:2](https://ref.ly/Matt15:1-Matt15:2) parallel [MRK 7:5](https://ref.ly/Mark7:5) *Though criticism is directed at the disciples, it is really against Jesus Christ*; ; [LUK 10:16](https://ref.ly/Luke10:16), [LUK 11:38](https://ref.ly/Luke11:38)

### Accusations of Sabbath\-breaking

**[JHN 5:16](https://ref.ly/John5:16)** *See also* [MAT 12:2](https://ref.ly/Matt12:2) parallels [MRK 2:24](https://ref.ly/Mark2:24), [LUK 6:2](https://ref.ly/Luke6:2); [MAT 12:10](https://ref.ly/Matt12:10) parallels [MRK 3:2](https://ref.ly/Mark3:2), [LUK 6:7](https://ref.ly/Luke6:7); [LUK 13:14](https://ref.ly/Luke13:14), [LUK 14:1](https://ref.ly/Luke14:1)

### Accusations of blasphemy

**[JHN 10:33](https://ref.ly/John10:33)** *See also* [MAT 9:3](https://ref.ly/Matt9:3) parallels [MRK 2:6–2:7](https://ref.ly/Mark2:6-Mark2:7), [LUK 5:21](https://ref.ly/Luke5:21); [MAT 26:65](https://ref.ly/Matt26:65) parallel [MRK 14:64](https://ref.ly/Mark14:64); [JHN 5:18](https://ref.ly/John5:18), [JHN 10:36](https://ref.ly/John10:36)

### Accusations of being demon\-possessed

**[JHN 10:20](https://ref.ly/John10:20)** *See also* [MAT 12:24](https://ref.ly/Matt12:24) parallels [MRK 3:22](https://ref.ly/Mark3:22), [LUK 11:15](https://ref.ly/Luke11:15); [JHN 7:20](https://ref.ly/John7:20), [JHN 8:48](https://ref.ly/John8:48)

Reasons for opposing Jesus Christ
---------------------------------

### Because of hatred

**[JHN 15:23–15:25](https://ref.ly/John15:23-John15:25)** *See also* [JHN 7:7](https://ref.ly/John7:7), [JHN 8:40](https://ref.ly/John8:40), [JHN 15:18](https://ref.ly/John15:18)

### Because people's minds are closed

**[JHN 8:43–8:44](https://ref.ly/John8:43-John8:44)** *See also* [JHN 8:37](https://ref.ly/John8:37); [2CO 4:4](https://ref.ly/2Cor4:4)

Jesus Christ knew where opposition would lead
---------------------------------------------

**[MAT 16:21](https://ref.ly/Matt16:21)** parallels [MRK 8:31–8:32](https://ref.ly/Mark8:31-Mark8:32), [LUK 9:22](https://ref.ly/Luke9:22) *See also* [MAT 17:22–17:23](https://ref.ly/Matt17:22-Matt17:23) parallel [MRK 9:31](https://ref.ly/Mark9:31); [MAT 20:17–20:19](https://ref.ly/Matt20:17-Matt20:19) parallels [MRK 10:32–10:34](https://ref.ly/Mark10:32-Mark10:34), [LUK 18:31–18:32](https://ref.ly/Luke18:31-Luke18:32); [LUK 9:44](https://ref.ly/Luke9:44)

Unsuccessful opposition before the crucifixion
----------------------------------------------

### Early attempts to arrest Jesus Christ

**[JHN 10:39](https://ref.ly/John10:39)** *See also* [JHN 7:30](https://ref.ly/John7:30), [JHN 7:32](https://ref.ly/John7:32), [JHN 7:44](https://ref.ly/John7:44)

### Attempts on Jesus Christ's life

**[JHN 8:59](https://ref.ly/John8:59)** *See also* [LUK 4:28–4:30](https://ref.ly/Luke4:28-Luke4:30); [JHN 7:19](https://ref.ly/John7:19), [JHN 10:31](https://ref.ly/John10:31)

Opposition that led to the crucifixion
--------------------------------------

### Plots by the Jewish leaders

**[MAT 26:3–26:4](https://ref.ly/Matt26:3-Matt26:4)** parallels [MRK 14:1–14:2](https://ref.ly/Mark14:1-Mark14:2), [LUK 22:2](https://ref.ly/Luke22:2) *See also* [MAT 21:46](https://ref.ly/Matt21:46) parallels [MRK 12:12](https://ref.ly/Mark12:12), [LUK 20:19](https://ref.ly/Luke20:19); [JHN 11:57](https://ref.ly/John11:57)

### The chief priests stirred up the crowd

**[MAT 27:20–27:23](https://ref.ly/Matt27:20-Matt27:23)** parallels [MRK 15:11–15:14](https://ref.ly/Mark15:11-Mark15:14), [LUK 23:21](https://ref.ly/Luke23:21) *See also* [JHN 19:15](https://ref.ly/John19:15)

**[MAT 27:26](https://ref.ly/Matt27:26)** parallels [MRK 15:15](https://ref.ly/Mark15:15), [LUK 23:24–23:25](https://ref.ly/Luke23:24-Luke23:25) *See also* [LUK 23:7–23:12](https://ref.ly/Luke23:7-Luke23:12); [JHN 19:16](https://ref.ly/John19:16); [ACT 4:25–4:27](https://ref.ly/Acts4:25-Acts4:27); [PSA 2:1–2:2](https://ref.ly/Ps2:1-Ps2:2)

## 2555: Jesus Christ, resurrection appearances of (id: 2555)

Jesus Christ appeared to various groups and individuals on several occasions after his death, prior to his ascension into heaven.

The resurrection appearances of Jesus Christ on the third day
-------------------------------------------------------------

### To Mary Magdalene

**[JHN 20:10–20:18](https://ref.ly/John20:10-John20:18)** *See also* [MRK 16:9–16:11](https://ref.ly/Mark16:9-Mark16:11)

[MAT 28:1–28:10](https://ref.ly/Matt28:1-Matt28:10) parallels [MRK 16:1–16:8](https://ref.ly/Mark16:1-Mark16:8), [LUK 24:1–24:12](https://ref.ly/Luke24:1-Luke24:12)

### To Peter

[LUK 24:34](https://ref.ly/Luke24:34); ; [1CO 15:5](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:5)

### To the two travellers to Emmaus

[MRK 16:12–16:13](https://ref.ly/Mark16:12-Mark16:13); ; [LUK 24:13–24:16](https://ref.ly/Luke24:13-Luke24:16), [LUK 24:30–24:32](https://ref.ly/Luke24:30-Luke24:32)

### To the disciples in the upper room

**[MRK 16:14](https://ref.ly/Mark16:14)** parallels [LUK 24:36](https://ref.ly/Luke24:36), [JHN 20:19](https://ref.ly/John20:19)

Further appearances of Jesus Christ
-----------------------------------

### To the disciples in the upper room

*See also* [JHN 20:26](https://ref.ly/John20:26); [1CO 15:5](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:5)

### Other appearances

[MRK 16:19](https://ref.ly/Mark16:19); ; [LUK 24:50–24:51](https://ref.ly/Luke24:50-Luke24:51); ; [ACT 1:9](https://ref.ly/Acts1:9)

Jesus Christ's resurrection body
--------------------------------

### It was different from his pre\-crucifixion body

**[JHN 20:26](https://ref.ly/John20:26)** *This suggests that the resurrected body of Jesus Christ was not restricted by natural laws: closed doors provided no barrier to Jesus Christ's bodily appearance to his disciples.* *See also* [MRK 16:12](https://ref.ly/Mark16:12) *The failure to recognise Jesus Christ may be an indication of his changed appearance but also might emphasise the disciples' own sorrow and lack of faith*; [JHN 20:14](https://ref.ly/John20:14), [JHN 20:19](https://ref.ly/John20:19) parallel [LUK 24:36](https://ref.ly/Luke24:36)

### It was a body of flesh and blood

**[LUK 24:39](https://ref.ly/Luke24:39)** *See also* [LUK 24:42–24:43](https://ref.ly/Luke24:42-Luke24:43); [JHN 20:20](https://ref.ly/John20:20)

Jesus Christ foretold his resurrection appearances
--------------------------------------------------

**[JHN 16:16](https://ref.ly/John16:16)**

## 2560: Jesus Christ, resurrection of (id: 2560)

True Christian preaching is centred on the fact that God raised Jesus Christ from the dead so that believers may have victory over sin and death and receive the blessings of eternal life.

The resurrection of Jesus Christ is foretold
--------------------------------------------

### In Scripture

**[1CO 15:3–15:4](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:3-1Cor15:4)** *See also* [PSA 16:10](https://ref.ly/Ps16:10), [PSA 49:15](https://ref.ly/Ps49:15); [ISA 53:10–53:12](https://ref.ly/Isa53:10-Isa53:12); [HOS 6:2](https://ref.ly/Hos6:2); [LUK 24:46](https://ref.ly/Luke24:46); [ACT 2:29–2:31](https://ref.ly/Acts2:29-Acts2:31), [ACT 26:22–26:23](https://ref.ly/Acts26:22-Acts26:23)

### By Jesus Christ

**[MAT 16:21](https://ref.ly/Matt16:21)** parallels [MRK 8:31](https://ref.ly/Mark8:31), [LUK 9:22](https://ref.ly/Luke9:22) *See also* [MAT 12:40](https://ref.ly/Matt12:40) *the sign of Jonah*; [MAT 17:9](https://ref.ly/Matt17:9) parallel [MRK 9:9](https://ref.ly/Mark9:9) *the transfiguration*; [MAT 17:22–17:23](https://ref.ly/Matt17:22-Matt17:23) parallel [MRK 9:31](https://ref.ly/Mark9:31); [MAT 20:18–20:19](https://ref.ly/Matt20:18-Matt20:19) parallels [MRK 10:33–10:34](https://ref.ly/Mark10:33-Mark10:34), [LUK 18:31–18:33](https://ref.ly/Luke18:31-Luke18:33); [MAT 26:32](https://ref.ly/Matt26:32) parallel [MRK 14:28](https://ref.ly/Mark14:28); [JHN 2:19–2:22](https://ref.ly/John2:19-John2:22) *Jesus Christ clears the temple*; [JHN 16:16](https://ref.ly/John16:16)

The resurrection is preached by the apostles
--------------------------------------------

**[ACT 4:33](https://ref.ly/Acts4:33)** *See also* [ACT 2:24–2:32](https://ref.ly/Acts2:24-Acts2:32), [ACT 10:40–10:41](https://ref.ly/Acts10:40-Acts10:41), [ACT 17:2–17:3](https://ref.ly/Acts17:2-Acts17:3), [ACT 17:18](https://ref.ly/Acts17:18), [ACT 17:31](https://ref.ly/Acts17:31)

---------------------------------

---------------------------------

**[1CO 15:17](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:17)** *See also* [JHN 20:9](https://ref.ly/John20:9)

------------------------------------------

### God's power is demonstrated

**[ROM 1:4](https://ref.ly/Rom1:4)** *See also* [ACT 13:33](https://ref.ly/Acts13:33)

The benefits of Jesus Christ's resurrection for believers
---------------------------------------------------------

### It is the foundation of salvation

**[ROM 4:25](https://ref.ly/Rom4:25)** *See also* [JHN 11:25–11:26](https://ref.ly/John11:25-John11:26); [ROM 10:9](https://ref.ly/Rom10:9); [1PE 1:21](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:21), [1PE 3:21](https://ref.ly/1Pet3:21)

## 2565: Jesus Christ, second coming of (id: 2565)

Jesus Christ will return visibly and in glory at the end of history to raise the dead, judge the world, destroy all evil and opposition to God and consummate his kingdom. Believers are encouraged to be prepared for his return, waiting with eagerness and joy.

The second coming is foretold
-----------------------------

### In the OT

**[DAN 7:13–7:14](https://ref.ly/Dan7:13-Dan7:14)** *See also* [PSA 72:2–72:4](https://ref.ly/Ps72:2-Ps72:4); [ISA 2:2–2:4](https://ref.ly/Isa2:2-Isa2:4) parallel [MIC 4:1–4:3](https://ref.ly/Mic4:1-Mic4:3); [ISA 11:4–11:9](https://ref.ly/Isa11:4-Isa11:9), [ISA 40:5](https://ref.ly/Isa40:5)

### By Jesus Christ

**[MAT 24:30](https://ref.ly/Matt24:30)** parallels [MRK 13:26](https://ref.ly/Mark13:26), [LUK 21:27](https://ref.ly/Luke21:27) *See also* [MAT 16:27](https://ref.ly/Matt16:27), [MAT 25:31](https://ref.ly/Matt25:31); [MRK 14:62](https://ref.ly/Mark14:62); [LUK 12:40](https://ref.ly/Luke12:40); [JHN 14:3](https://ref.ly/John14:3), [JHN 14:28](https://ref.ly/John14:28)

### By the angels at Jesus Christ's ascension

**[ACT 1:11](https://ref.ly/Acts1:11)**

### By the apostles

**[PHP 3:20](https://ref.ly/Phil3:20)** *See also* [ACT 3:20–3:21](https://ref.ly/Acts3:20-Acts3:21); [1CO 1:7](https://ref.ly/1Cor1:7), [1CO 11:26](https://ref.ly/1Cor11:26); [1TH 1:10](https://ref.ly/1Thess1:10), [1TH 3:13](https://ref.ly/1Thess3:13), [1TH 4:16](https://ref.ly/1Thess4:16); [2TH 1:7–1:10](https://ref.ly/2Thess1:7-2Thess1:10); [HEB 9:28](https://ref.ly/Heb9:28)

NT terms for the second coming
------------------------------

### \`\`Parousia''

Meaning literally `presence'' or`coming'', the term was used in the NT world of a royal visit: [MAT 24:3](https://ref.ly/Matt24:3); ; [JAS 5:7–5:8](https://ref.ly/Jas5:7-Jas5:8); ; [2PE 3:4](https://ref.ly/2Pet3:4); ; [1JN 2:28](https://ref.ly/1John2:28)

### \`\`Apocalypsis''

Meaning literally `unveiling'',`apocalypsis'' suggests that the second coming will make visible that which is already true of Jesus Christ but presently hidden from human sight: [LUK 17:30](https://ref.ly/Luke17:30); ; [1CO 1:7](https://ref.ly/1Cor1:7); ; [2TH 1:7](https://ref.ly/2Thess1:7); ; [1PE 1:7](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:7), [1PE 4:13](https://ref.ly/1Pet4:13)

### \`\`Epiphaneia''

Meaning literally `appearing'' or`manifestation'', the term suggests coming out into view from a hidden background: [2TH 2:8](https://ref.ly/2Thess2:8); ; [1TI 6:14](https://ref.ly/1Tim6:14); ; [2TI 4:1](https://ref.ly/2Tim4:1); ; [TIT 2:13](https://ref.ly/Titus2:13)

Events that will precede the second coming
------------------------------------------

### The universal preaching of the gospel

**[MAT 24:14](https://ref.ly/Matt24:14)** parallel [MRK 13:10](https://ref.ly/Mark13:10) *See also* [MAT 28:19–28:20](https://ref.ly/Matt28:19-Matt28:20); [ACT 1:7–1:8](https://ref.ly/Acts1:7-Acts1:8)

### The persecution of believers

**[MAT 24:9](https://ref.ly/Matt24:9)** parallels [MRK 13:9](https://ref.ly/Mark13:9), [LUK 21:12](https://ref.ly/Luke21:12) *See also* [MAT 24:21](https://ref.ly/Matt24:21) parallel [MRK 13:19](https://ref.ly/Mark13:19); [MAT 24:22](https://ref.ly/Matt24:22) parallel [MRK 13:20](https://ref.ly/Mark13:20); [MRK 13:12–13:13](https://ref.ly/Mark13:12-Mark13:13) parallels [MAT 24:12–24:13](https://ref.ly/Matt24:12-Matt24:13), [LUK 21:16–21:17](https://ref.ly/Luke21:16-Luke21:17); [2TI 3:1](https://ref.ly/2Tim3:1); [REV 7:14](https://ref.ly/Rev7:14)

### Apostasy, nominal religion and godlessness

**[1TI 4:1](https://ref.ly/1Tim4:1)** *See also* [MAT 24:10](https://ref.ly/Matt24:10); [2TI 3:1–3:5](https://ref.ly/2Tim3:1-2Tim3:5); [2PE 3:3–3:4](https://ref.ly/2Pet3:3-2Pet3:4)

### The revelation of the antichrist

**[1JN 2:18](https://ref.ly/1John2:18)** *The antichrist is a name given to the one who will lead opposition to God's kingdom. It appears to refer to an individual but may denote a corporate movement.* *See also* [DAN 7:20–7:22](https://ref.ly/Dan7:20-Dan7:22); [2TH 2:3–2:4](https://ref.ly/2Thess2:3-2Thess2:4); [1JN 4:3](https://ref.ly/1John4:3); [REV 13:1–13:10](https://ref.ly/Rev13:1-Rev13:10)

### The appearance of false Christs and false prophets

**[MAT 24:24](https://ref.ly/Matt24:24)** parallel [MRK 13:22](https://ref.ly/Mark13:22) *See also* [MAT 7:15](https://ref.ly/Matt7:15), [MAT 24:5](https://ref.ly/Matt24:5) parallels [MRK 13:6](https://ref.ly/Mark13:6), [LUK 21:8](https://ref.ly/Luke21:8); [MAT 24:11](https://ref.ly/Matt24:11); [LUK 17:23](https://ref.ly/Luke17:23); [2JN 1:7](https://ref.ly/2John1:7)

### Wars and rumours of wars

**[MAT 24:6–24:7](https://ref.ly/Matt24:6-Matt24:7)** parallels [MRK 13:7–13:8](https://ref.ly/Mark13:7-Mark13:8), [LUK 21:9–21:10](https://ref.ly/Luke21:9-Luke21:10)

### Famines and earthquakes

**[MAT 24:7–24:8](https://ref.ly/Matt24:7-Matt24:8)** parallels [MRK 13:8](https://ref.ly/Mark13:8), [LUK 21:11](https://ref.ly/Luke21:11)

### Cosmic changes

**[MAT 24:29](https://ref.ly/Matt24:29)** parallels [MRK 13:24](https://ref.ly/Mark13:24), [LUK 21:25–21:26](https://ref.ly/Luke21:25-Luke21:26)

The timing of the second coming
-------------------------------

### At God's appointed time

**[ACT 3:20–3:21](https://ref.ly/Acts3:20-Acts3:21)** *See also* [MAT 24:36](https://ref.ly/Matt24:36) parallel [MRK 13:32](https://ref.ly/Mark13:32); [LUK 17:20–17:30](https://ref.ly/Luke17:20-Luke17:30); [ACT 1:7](https://ref.ly/Acts1:7); [2PE 3:9](https://ref.ly/2Pet3:9)

### Unexpectedly

**[1TH 5:1–5:2](https://ref.ly/1Thess5:1-1Thess5:2)** *See also* [MAT 24:27](https://ref.ly/Matt24:27) parallel [LUK 17:24](https://ref.ly/Luke17:24); [MAT 24:43–24:44](https://ref.ly/Matt24:43-Matt24:44) parallel [LUK 12:39–12:40](https://ref.ly/Luke12:39-Luke12:40); [2PE 3:10](https://ref.ly/2Pet3:10); [REV 3:3](https://ref.ly/Rev3:3), [REV 16:15](https://ref.ly/Rev16:15)

### After a delay

**[MAT 25:5](https://ref.ly/Matt25:5)** *Part of a parable concerning the coming of Jesus Christ who is represented by the bridegroom.* *See also* [MAT 25:19](https://ref.ly/Matt25:19); [2PE 3:3–3:9](https://ref.ly/2Pet3:3-2Pet3:9)

### Imminently

**[MAT 24:30–24:34](https://ref.ly/Matt24:30-Matt24:34)** parallels [MRK 13:26–13:30](https://ref.ly/Mark13:26-Mark13:30), [LUK 21:27–21:32](https://ref.ly/Luke21:27-Luke21:32) *See also* [JHN 21:22](https://ref.ly/John21:22); [ROM 13:11–13:12](https://ref.ly/Rom13:11-Rom13:12); [JAS 5:8–5:9](https://ref.ly/Jas5:8-Jas5:9); [REV 3:11](https://ref.ly/Rev3:11), [REV 22:7](https://ref.ly/Rev22:7), [REV 22:20](https://ref.ly/Rev22:20)

The manner of the second coming
-------------------------------

### Jesus Christ's personal return

**[ACT 1:11](https://ref.ly/Acts1:11)** *See also* [ACT 3:20](https://ref.ly/Acts3:20); [1TH 4:16](https://ref.ly/1Thess4:16); [HEB 9:28](https://ref.ly/Heb9:28)

**[REV 1:7](https://ref.ly/Rev1:7)** *See also* [MAT 24:30](https://ref.ly/Matt24:30) parallels [MRK 13:26](https://ref.ly/Mark13:26), [LUK 21:27](https://ref.ly/Luke21:27); [MAT 26:64](https://ref.ly/Matt26:64); [ACT 1:9](https://ref.ly/Acts1:9)

### With the sound of a trumpet

[MAT 24:31](https://ref.ly/Matt24:31); ; [1CO 15:52](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:52); ; [1TH 4:16](https://ref.ly/1Thess4:16)

### With angels

[MAT 16:27](https://ref.ly/Matt16:27), [MAT 24:31](https://ref.ly/Matt24:31); ; [2TH 1:7](https://ref.ly/2Thess1:7)

The purpose of the second coming
--------------------------------

### To raise the dead

**[1CO 15:22–15:23](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:22-1Cor15:23)** *See also* [JHN 5:28–5:29](https://ref.ly/John5:28-John5:29); [1CO 15:52](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:52); [1TH 4:16](https://ref.ly/1Thess4:16)

### To judge all people

**[PSA 96:13](https://ref.ly/Ps96:13)** *See also* [PSA 98:9](https://ref.ly/Ps98:9); [MAT 16:27](https://ref.ly/Matt16:27), [MAT 25:31–25:32](https://ref.ly/Matt25:31-Matt25:32); [2TI 4:1](https://ref.ly/2Tim4:1); [REV 20:11–20:15](https://ref.ly/Rev20:11-Rev20:15), [REV 22:12](https://ref.ly/Rev22:12)

### To judge the wicked

**[2TH 1:7–1:10](https://ref.ly/2Thess1:7-2Thess1:10)** *See also* [MAT 24:51](https://ref.ly/Matt24:51); [ROM 2:5](https://ref.ly/Rom2:5); [2PE 3:7](https://ref.ly/2Pet3:7); [JUD 1:15](https://ref.ly/Jude1:15)

### To separate the wicked from the righteous

**[MAT 25:31–25:32](https://ref.ly/Matt25:31-Matt25:32)** *See also* [MAT 24:40–24:41](https://ref.ly/Matt24:40-Matt24:41) parallel [LUK 17:34–17:35](https://ref.ly/Luke17:34-Luke17:35)

### To destroy all evil and opposition to God's kingdom

**[2TH 2:8](https://ref.ly/2Thess2:8)** *See also* [1CO 15:24–15:26](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:24-1Cor15:26); [REV 20:10](https://ref.ly/Rev20:10), [REV 20:14](https://ref.ly/Rev20:14)

### To reward believers

[MAT 24:46–24:47](https://ref.ly/Matt24:46-Matt24:47); ; [LUK 12:37](https://ref.ly/Luke12:37); ; [2TI 4:8](https://ref.ly/2Tim4:8); ; [1PE 5:4](https://ref.ly/1Pet5:4); ; [1JN 3:1](https://ref.ly/1John3:1)

### To gather the church together

[JHN 14:3](https://ref.ly/John14:3); ; [1TH 4:17](https://ref.ly/1Thess4:17); ; [2TH 2:1](https://ref.ly/2Thess2:1)

### To bring final salvation

[LUK 21:28](https://ref.ly/Luke21:28); ; [HEB 9:28](https://ref.ly/Heb9:28)

### To transform the saints into his likeness

[1CO 15:51–15:52](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:51-1Cor15:52); ; [PHP 3:20–3:21](https://ref.ly/Phil3:20-Phil3:21); ; [COL 3:4](https://ref.ly/Col3:4)

### To end the present age

[MAT 24:3](https://ref.ly/Matt24:3); ; [1CO 15:24](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:24); ; [2PE 3:10](https://ref.ly/2Pet3:10), [2PE 3:12](https://ref.ly/2Pet3:12)

### To restore and renew all things

[ACT 3:21](https://ref.ly/Acts3:21); ; [2PE 3:13](https://ref.ly/2Pet3:13); ; [REV 21:1–21:5](https://ref.ly/Rev21:1-Rev21:5)

Reactions at Jesus Christ's second coming
-----------------------------------------

[MAT 24:30](https://ref.ly/Matt24:30) *all peoples will mourn*; ; [2TH 1:10](https://ref.ly/2Thess1:10) *His people will marvel.*

-------------------------------------------------------

**[MAT 24:42–24:44](https://ref.ly/Matt24:42-Matt24:44)** *See also* [MAT 25:10](https://ref.ly/Matt25:10); [MRK 13:35](https://ref.ly/Mark13:35); [LUK 12:35–12:36](https://ref.ly/Luke12:35-Luke12:36)

### They must eagerly expect his coming

**[1CO 1:7](https://ref.ly/1Cor1:7)** *See also* [LUK 21:28](https://ref.ly/Luke21:28); [PHP 3:20](https://ref.ly/Phil3:20); [TIT 2:13](https://ref.ly/Titus2:13)

### They must endure suffering with patient endurance

## 2570: Jesus Christ, suffering of (id: 2570)

Jesus Christ's life was characterised by suffering, though the worst experiences were reserved for his final days. His sufferings are both redemptive and an example to believers.

Jesus Christ's sufferings foretold
----------------------------------

### In the OT

[PSA 22:6–22:8](https://ref.ly/Ps22:6-Ps22:8), [PSA 22:16–22:18](https://ref.ly/Ps22:16-Ps22:18); ; [ISA 50:6](https://ref.ly/Isa50:6), [ISA 52:13–53:12](https://ref.ly/Isa52:13-Isa53:12); ; [ZEC 9:9–9:10](https://ref.ly/Zech9:9-Zech9:10), [ZEC 12:10](https://ref.ly/Zech12:10), [ZEC 13:7](https://ref.ly/Zech13:7); ; [1PE 1:11](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:11)

### In Jesus Christ's predictions

**[MAT 16:21](https://ref.ly/Matt16:21)** parallels [MRK 8:31](https://ref.ly/Mark8:31), [LUK 9:22](https://ref.ly/Luke9:22) *See also* [MAT 20:17–20:19](https://ref.ly/Matt20:17-Matt20:19) parallels [MRK 10:32–10:34](https://ref.ly/Mark10:32-Mark10:34), [LUK 18:31–18:32](https://ref.ly/Luke18:31-Luke18:32); [JHN 12:32–12:33](https://ref.ly/John12:32-John12:33)

Jesus Christ's suffering during his lifetime
--------------------------------------------

### As a child

[MAT 2:13–2:15](https://ref.ly/Matt2:13-Matt2:15)

### Because of his family

**[MRK 3:20–3:21](https://ref.ly/Mark3:20-Mark3:21)** *See also* [JHN 7:3–7:5](https://ref.ly/John7:3-John7:5)

### Because of the crowds' unbelief

**[MRK 9:19](https://ref.ly/Mark9:19)** parallels [MAT 17:17](https://ref.ly/Matt17:17), [LUK 9:41](https://ref.ly/Luke9:41) *See also* [MAT 12:39](https://ref.ly/Matt12:39) parallel [LUK 11:29](https://ref.ly/Luke11:29); [MRK 8:11–8:12](https://ref.ly/Mark8:11-Mark8:12)

### Because of the disciples' slowness

**[MRK 8:17–8:21](https://ref.ly/Mark8:17-Mark8:21)** parallel [MAT 16:8–16:11](https://ref.ly/Matt16:8-Matt16:11)

### Because of the religious leaders

**[MAT 12:14](https://ref.ly/Matt12:14)** parallels [MRK 3:6](https://ref.ly/Mark3:6), [LUK 6:11](https://ref.ly/Luke6:11) *See also* [JHN 5:18](https://ref.ly/John5:18), [JHN 7:1](https://ref.ly/John7:1), [JHN 8:48](https://ref.ly/John8:48)

### Because of human suffering

**[LUK 19:41](https://ref.ly/Luke19:41)** *See also* [MRK 7:34](https://ref.ly/Mark7:34); [LUK 7:13](https://ref.ly/Luke7:13); [JHN 11:33–11:35](https://ref.ly/John11:33-John11:35)

Jesus Christ's suffering at the time of his death
-------------------------------------------------

### He was inwardly troubled

**[JHN 12:27](https://ref.ly/John12:27)** *See also* [MAT 26:36–26:42](https://ref.ly/Matt26:36-Matt26:42) parallels [MRK 14:32–14:39](https://ref.ly/Mark14:32-Mark14:39), [LUK 22:40–22:44](https://ref.ly/Luke22:40-Luke22:44); [JHN 13:21](https://ref.ly/John13:21)

### He was betrayed

[MAT 26:21–26:25](https://ref.ly/Matt26:21-Matt26:25) parallels [MRK 14:17–14:21](https://ref.ly/Mark14:17-Mark14:21), [LUK 22:21–22:23](https://ref.ly/Luke22:21-Luke22:23); ; [MAT 26:47–26:49](https://ref.ly/Matt26:47-Matt26:49) parallels [MRK 14:43–14:45](https://ref.ly/Mark14:43-Mark14:45), [LUK 22:47–22:48](https://ref.ly/Luke22:47-Luke22:48), [JHN 18:2–18:5](https://ref.ly/John18:2-John18:5); ; [JHN 13:18–13:30](https://ref.ly/John13:18-John13:30)

### He was humiliated

**[MAT 27:27–27:30](https://ref.ly/Matt27:27-Matt27:30)** parallel [MRK 15:16–15:19](https://ref.ly/Mark15:16-Mark15:19) *See also* [MAT 26:67–26:68](https://ref.ly/Matt26:67-Matt26:68) parallels [MRK 14:65](https://ref.ly/Mark14:65), [LUK 22:63–22:65](https://ref.ly/Luke22:63-Luke22:65); [MAT 27:26](https://ref.ly/Matt27:26) parallels [MRK 15:15](https://ref.ly/Mark15:15), [LUK 23:22](https://ref.ly/Luke23:22); [LUK 23:11](https://ref.ly/Luke23:11); [JHN 18:22](https://ref.ly/John18:22), [JHN 19:1](https://ref.ly/John19:1)

### He was crucified

**[LUK 23:33](https://ref.ly/Luke23:33)** parallels [MAT 27:35](https://ref.ly/Matt27:35), [MRK 15:25](https://ref.ly/Mark15:25), [JHN 19:18](https://ref.ly/John19:18)

### He suffered separation from God

**[MAT 27:46](https://ref.ly/Matt27:46)** parallels [MRK 15:34](https://ref.ly/Mark15:34), [LUK 23:46](https://ref.ly/Luke23:46) *See also* [PSA 22:1](https://ref.ly/Ps22:1)

Jesus Christ's attitude to his suffering
----------------------------------------

### He did not retaliate in his suffering

**[1PE 2:23](https://ref.ly/1Pet2:23)** *See also* [MAT 27:12–27:14](https://ref.ly/Matt27:12-Matt27:14) parallel [MRK 15:3–15:5](https://ref.ly/Mark15:3-Mark15:5); [LUK 23:34](https://ref.ly/Luke23:34)

### He grew through the experience of suffering

**[HEB 5:8](https://ref.ly/Heb5:8)** *See also* [HEB 2:10](https://ref.ly/Heb2:10)

Jesus Christ's sufferings were necessary for salvation
------------------------------------------------------

**[LUK 24:26–24:27](https://ref.ly/Luke24:26-Luke24:27)** *See also* [LUK 24:46–24:47](https://ref.ly/Luke24:46-Luke24:47); [ACT 3:18](https://ref.ly/Acts3:18), [ACT 17:3](https://ref.ly/Acts17:3), [ACT 26:23](https://ref.ly/Acts26:23)

### Jesus Christ suffered as a unique sacrifice

[HEB 7:27](https://ref.ly/Heb7:27), [HEB 9:25–9:26](https://ref.ly/Heb9:25-Heb9:26)

The Christian experience of suffering
-------------------------------------

### Believers share in Jesus Christ's sufferings

**[2CO 1:5](https://ref.ly/2Cor1:5)** *See also* [MAT 25:34–25:40](https://ref.ly/Matt25:34-Matt25:40); [ACT 9:4–9:5](https://ref.ly/Acts9:4-Acts9:5) parallels [ACT 22:7–22:8](https://ref.ly/Acts22:7-Acts22:8), [ACT 26:15](https://ref.ly/Acts26:15); [ROM 8:17](https://ref.ly/Rom8:17); [PHP 3:10](https://ref.ly/Phil3:10); [1PE 4:13](https://ref.ly/1Pet4:13)

### Jesus Christ's sufferings are an example for believers

**[1PE 2:21](https://ref.ly/1Pet2:21)** *See also* [JHN 16:18–16:20](https://ref.ly/John16:18-John16:20); [PHP 2:5–2:7](https://ref.ly/Phil2:5-Phil2:7)

## 2575: Jesus Christ, temptation of (id: 2575)

Repeated yet unsuccessful efforts made by Satan and by human beings to deflect Jesus Christ from his Father's will.

The wilderness temptations
--------------------------

**[MRK 1:13](https://ref.ly/Mark1:13)**

### Tempted to turn stones into bread

**[MAT 4:2–4:3](https://ref.ly/Matt4:2-Matt4:3)** parallel [LUK 4:2–4:3](https://ref.ly/Luke4:2-Luke4:3)

### Tempted to abuse miraculous power

**[MAT 4:5–4:6](https://ref.ly/Matt4:5-Matt4:6)** parallel [LUK 4:9–4:11](https://ref.ly/Luke4:9-Luke4:11) *See also* [MAT 12:38](https://ref.ly/Matt12:38), [MAT 16:1](https://ref.ly/Matt16:1) parallel [MRK 8:11](https://ref.ly/Mark8:11); [LUK 11:16](https://ref.ly/Luke11:16); [JHN 2:18](https://ref.ly/John2:18)

### Tempted by the offer of an easy route to power

**[MAT 4:8–4:9](https://ref.ly/Matt4:8-Matt4:9)** parallel [LUK 4:5–4:7](https://ref.ly/Luke4:5-Luke4:7)

### Tempted to doubt he was God's Son

**[MAT 4:3](https://ref.ly/Matt4:3)** parallel [LUK 4:3](https://ref.ly/Luke4:3) *See also* [MAT 4:6](https://ref.ly/Matt4:6) parallel [LUK 4:9](https://ref.ly/Luke4:9); [MAT 27:40](https://ref.ly/Matt27:40)

Temptation continued throughout Jesus Christ's life
---------------------------------------------------

**[LUK 22:28](https://ref.ly/Luke22:28)** *Trials can include temptations.*

### Opponents tempted Jesus Christ with trick questions

*See also* [MAT 22:15](https://ref.ly/Matt22:15) parallels [MRK 12:13](https://ref.ly/Mark12:13), [LUK 20:20](https://ref.ly/Luke20:20)

### Jesus Christ tempted to sidestep the cross

**[MAT 16:21–16:23](https://ref.ly/Matt16:21-Matt16:23)** parallel [MRK 8:32–8:33](https://ref.ly/Mark8:32-Mark8:33) *See also* [MAT 26:39–26:44](https://ref.ly/Matt26:39-Matt26:44) parallels [MRK 14:35–14:41](https://ref.ly/Mark14:35-Mark14:41), [LUK 22:41–22:44](https://ref.ly/Luke22:41-Luke22:44); [MAT 27:40](https://ref.ly/Matt27:40) parallel [MRK 15:30](https://ref.ly/Mark15:30)

Jesus Christ steadfastly resisted temptation
--------------------------------------------

### Jesus Christ resisted temptation by trusting God's word

**[MAT 4:4](https://ref.ly/Matt4:4)** parallel [LUK 4:4](https://ref.ly/Luke4:4) *See also* [MAT 4:7](https://ref.ly/Matt4:7) parallel [LUK 4:12](https://ref.ly/Luke4:12); [MAT 4:10](https://ref.ly/Matt4:10) parallel [LUK 4:8](https://ref.ly/Luke4:8)

### Jesus Christ resisted temptation by obeying his Father

**[HEB 5:7–5:8](https://ref.ly/Heb5:7-Heb5:8)** *See also* [MAT 26:39](https://ref.ly/Matt26:39) parallels [MRK 14:36](https://ref.ly/Mark14:36), [LUK 22:42](https://ref.ly/Luke22:42); [MAT 26:42](https://ref.ly/Matt26:42)

Results of Jesus Christ's temptations
-------------------------------------

### Satan left Jesus Christ alone

**[MAT 4:11](https://ref.ly/Matt4:11)** parallel [LUK 4:13](https://ref.ly/Luke4:13)

### Jesus Christ remained sinless

**[HEB 4:15](https://ref.ly/Heb4:15)** *Refers to Jesus Christ as high priest and as sacrificial lamb.* *See also* [JHN 8:46](https://ref.ly/John8:46); [1PE 2:22](https://ref.ly/1Pet2:22)

### Jesus Christ helps those who are being tempted

**[HEB 2:18](https://ref.ly/Heb2:18)** *See also* [HEB 4:14–4:16](https://ref.ly/Heb4:14-Heb4:16)

## 2580: Jesus Christ, transfiguration of (id: 2580)

The revelation of the glory of Jesus Christ, shortly before his death, at which his disciples caught sight of him in his full majesty. The transfiguration brought home to the disciples that Jesus Christ is the Son of God.

The glory of Jesus Christ is revealed at the transfiguration
------------------------------------------------------------

### Jesus Christ prepares for his glory to be revealed

**[LUK 9:28](https://ref.ly/Luke9:28)** parallels [MAT 17:1](https://ref.ly/Matt17:1), [MRK 9:2](https://ref.ly/Mark9:2)

### Jesus Christ is visibly transfigured

**[MAT 17:2](https://ref.ly/Matt17:2)** parallels [MRK 9:2–9:3](https://ref.ly/Mark9:2-Mark9:3), [LUK 9:29](https://ref.ly/Luke9:29) *The transfiguration was a glimpse of Jesus Christ's glory whereby his physical appearance was visibly changed.*

### The disciples are eye\-witnesses of Jesus Christ's glory

**[MAT 17:6](https://ref.ly/Matt17:6)** *See also* [MRK 9:9](https://ref.ly/Mark9:9); [LUK 9:32](https://ref.ly/Luke9:32); [JHN 1:14](https://ref.ly/John1:14); [2PE 1:16](https://ref.ly/2Pet1:16)

Moses and Elijah appear at the transfiguration
----------------------------------------------

**[LUK 9:30–9:31](https://ref.ly/Luke9:30-Luke9:31)** parallels [MAT 17:3](https://ref.ly/Matt17:3), [MRK 9:4](https://ref.ly/Mark9:4) *“departure” refers to Jesus Christ's death.*

God's voice is heard at the transfiguration
-------------------------------------------

**[MAT 17:5](https://ref.ly/Matt17:5)** parallels [MRK 9:7](https://ref.ly/Mark9:7), [LUK 9:35](https://ref.ly/Luke9:35) *God the Father's voice is heard authenticating Jesus Christ's ministry.* *See also* [MAT 3:17](https://ref.ly/Matt3:17) parallels [MRK 1:11](https://ref.ly/Mark1:11), [LUK 3:22](https://ref.ly/Luke3:22); [2PE 1:17–1:18](https://ref.ly/2Pet1:17-2Pet1:18)

The disciples' response to the transfiguration
----------------------------------------------

### Peter's wish to build shelters

[MAT 17:4](https://ref.ly/Matt17:4) parallels [MRK 9:5–9:6](https://ref.ly/Mark9:5-Mark9:6), [LUK 9:33](https://ref.ly/Luke9:33)

### Fear

[MAT 17:6–17:7](https://ref.ly/Matt17:6-Matt17:7); ; [MRK 9:6](https://ref.ly/Mark9:6); ; [LUK 9:34](https://ref.ly/Luke9:34)

### Questioning and confusion

[MAT 17:10](https://ref.ly/Matt17:10) parallel [MRK 9:10–9:11](https://ref.ly/Mark9:10-Mark9:11)

### They keep to themselves what they have seen and heard

**[LUK 9:36](https://ref.ly/Luke9:36)** parallels [MAT 17:9–17:10](https://ref.ly/Matt17:9-Matt17:10), [MRK 9:9–9:10](https://ref.ly/Mark9:9-Mark9:10) *These verses reiterate that Jesus Christ's full glory was hidden from the world until his resurrection.*

## 2585: Jesus Christ, trial of (id: 2585)

Jesus Christ, falsely accused of blasphemy towards God and treason towards Rome, humbly endured his trial as a fulfilment of the purposes of God.

The preliminary hearing before Annas
------------------------------------

*See also* [JHN 18:12–18:14](https://ref.ly/John18:12-John18:14) *Annas, though deposed from office by the Romans, was probably still regarded by many as the true high priest*; [JHN 18:19–18:23](https://ref.ly/John18:19-John18:23)

The trial before Caiaphas and the Sanhedrin
-------------------------------------------

### Jesus Christ is sent to the ruling high priest

[MAT 26:57](https://ref.ly/Matt26:57) parallels [MRK 14:53](https://ref.ly/Mark14:53), [JHN 18:24](https://ref.ly/John18:24); ; [LUK 22:54](https://ref.ly/Luke22:54)

### False evidence is sought

**[MAT 26:59–26:60](https://ref.ly/Matt26:59-Matt26:60)** parallel [MRK 14:55–14:56](https://ref.ly/Mark14:55-Mark14:56) *The Sanhedrin was the high court of the Jews and consisted of 71 chief priests, elders and teachers of the law, including the high priest who presided.*

### False accusations are made

*See also* [MAT 26:60–26:61](https://ref.ly/Matt26:60-Matt26:61) parallel [MRK 14:57–14:59](https://ref.ly/Mark14:57-Mark14:59) *A person could only be convicted on the evidence of two or more witnesses.*

Jesus Christ's trial centres upon his Messianic claims
------------------------------------------------------

### Jesus declares himself to be the Christ

**[MAT 26:63–26:64](https://ref.ly/Matt26:63-Matt26:64)** parallel [MRK 14:61–14:62](https://ref.ly/Mark14:61-Mark14:62) *See also* [LUK 22:66–22:70](https://ref.ly/Luke22:66-Luke22:70)

### Jesus Christ is charged with blasphemy

[MAT 26:65–26:66](https://ref.ly/Matt26:65-Matt26:66) parallel [MRK 14:63–14:64](https://ref.ly/Mark14:63-Mark14:64); ; [MAT 27:1](https://ref.ly/Matt27:1) parallel [MRK 15:1](https://ref.ly/Mark15:1) *The Sanhedrin decided that Jesus Christ deserved death but charged him with treason rather than blasphemy.*

### Jesus is mocked as the Christ

[MAT 26:67–26:68](https://ref.ly/Matt26:67-Matt26:68) parallels [MRK 14:65](https://ref.ly/Mark14:65), [LUK 22:63–22:65](https://ref.ly/Luke22:63-Luke22:65)

The trial before Pilate
-----------------------

### The Sanhedrin hand Jesus Christ over to Pilate

[MAT 27:2](https://ref.ly/Matt27:2) parallel [MRK 15:1](https://ref.ly/Mark15:1); ; [LUK 23:1](https://ref.ly/Luke23:1); ; [JHN 18:28–18:32](https://ref.ly/John18:28-John18:32)

### Jesus Christ accepts the title of king

**[JHN 18:36–18:37](https://ref.ly/John18:36-John18:37)** *See also* [MAT 27:11](https://ref.ly/Matt27:11) parallel [MRK 15:2](https://ref.ly/Mark15:2); [LUK 23:2–23:3](https://ref.ly/Luke23:2-Luke23:3); [JHN 19:9–19:12](https://ref.ly/John19:9-John19:12); [1TI 6:13](https://ref.ly/1Tim6:13)

### Pilate decides Jesus Christ is innocent

**[LUK 23:4](https://ref.ly/Luke23:4)** *See also* [LUK 23:14–23:15](https://ref.ly/Luke23:14-Luke23:15), [LUK 23:22](https://ref.ly/Luke23:22); [JHN 18:38](https://ref.ly/John18:38), [JHN 19:4–19:6](https://ref.ly/John19:4-John19:6); [ACT 13:28](https://ref.ly/Acts13:28)

### Pilate sends Jesus Christ to Herod

[LUK 23:5–23:10](https://ref.ly/Luke23:5-Luke23:10)

### Herod sends Jesus Christ back to Pilate

[LUK 23:11–23:12](https://ref.ly/Luke23:11-Luke23:12)

### Pilate seeks to release Jesus Christ

**[JHN 19:12](https://ref.ly/John19:12)** *See also* [MAT 27:15–27:18](https://ref.ly/Matt27:15-Matt27:18) parallel [MRK 15:6–15:10](https://ref.ly/Mark15:6-Mark15:10) *Pilate appeals to the crowd on the basis of Jesus Christ's kingship*; [MAT 27:19](https://ref.ly/Matt27:19) *Pilate is warned by his wife not to get involved*; [LUK 23:16](https://ref.ly/Luke23:16), [LUK 23:20](https://ref.ly/Luke23:20), [LUK 23:22](https://ref.ly/Luke23:22); [JHN 18:38–18:39](https://ref.ly/John18:38-John18:39), [JHN 19:6](https://ref.ly/John19:6), [JHN 19:15](https://ref.ly/John19:15)

### The crowd demand the release of Barabbas and the crucifixion of Jesus Christ

**[MAT 27:20](https://ref.ly/Matt27:20)** parallel [MRK 15:11](https://ref.ly/Mark15:11) *See also* [MAT 27:21–27:23](https://ref.ly/Matt27:21-Matt27:23) parallel [MRK 15:12–15:14](https://ref.ly/Mark15:12-Mark15:14); [LUK 23:18](https://ref.ly/Luke23:18), [LUK 23:21](https://ref.ly/Luke23:21), [LUK 23:23](https://ref.ly/Luke23:23); [JHN 18:40](https://ref.ly/John18:40), [JHN 19:6–19:7](https://ref.ly/John19:6-John19:7), [JHN 19:12](https://ref.ly/John19:12), [JHN 19:15](https://ref.ly/John19:15)

### The crowd's demands prevail

**[MRK 15:15](https://ref.ly/Mark15:15)** parallel [MAT 27:26](https://ref.ly/Matt27:26) *See also* [MAT 27:24](https://ref.ly/Matt27:24) *Pilate denies responsibility*; [MAT 27:25](https://ref.ly/Matt27:25); [LUK 23:23–23:25](https://ref.ly/Luke23:23-Luke23:25); [JHN 19:16](https://ref.ly/John19:16); [ACT 3:13–3:14](https://ref.ly/Acts3:13-Acts3:14) *The emphasis is on the people's responsibility.*

### Jesus Christ is mocked as king

**[JHN 19:2–19:3](https://ref.ly/John19:2-John19:3)** *See also* [MAT 27:27–27:31](https://ref.ly/Matt27:27-Matt27:31) parallel [MRK 15:16–15:20](https://ref.ly/Mark15:16-Mark15:20); [JHN 19:15](https://ref.ly/John19:15)

Jesus Christ's response to his trial
------------------------------------

**[ISA 53:7](https://ref.ly/Isa53:7)** *See also* [MAT 26:62–26:63](https://ref.ly/Matt26:62-Matt26:63) parallel [MRK 14:60–14:61](https://ref.ly/Mark14:60-Mark14:61); [MAT 27:12](https://ref.ly/Matt27:12), [MAT 27:14](https://ref.ly/Matt27:14) parallel [MRK 15:5](https://ref.ly/Mark15:5); [LUK 23:9](https://ref.ly/Luke23:9); [JHN 19:9](https://ref.ly/John19:9); [ACT 8:32–8:35](https://ref.ly/Acts8:32-Acts8:35); [1PE 2:23](https://ref.ly/1Pet2:23)

## 2590: Jesus Christ, triumphal entry of (id: 2590)

Jesus Christ rode into Jerusalem on a colt, royally yet humbly, to the rejoicing of his followers, but provoking opposition from the Jewish religious leaders.

The colt used in Jesus Christ's entry into Jerusalem
----------------------------------------------------

### Jesus Christ's instructions to his disciples

**[LUK 19:29–19:31](https://ref.ly/Luke19:29-Luke19:31)** parallels [MAT 21:1–21:3](https://ref.ly/Matt21:1-Matt21:3), [MRK 11:1–11:3](https://ref.ly/Mark11:1-Mark11:3)

-----------------------------------

----------------------------------------------------------------

## 2595: incarnation (id: 2595)

The assuming by God of human nature in the person of Jesus Christ. The incarnation is the fixed and permanent physical dwelling of God in his world, as opposed to the temporary manifestation of the divine presence and power in a theophany.

God the Son assumed human nature
--------------------------------

**[JHN 1:14](https://ref.ly/John1:14)** *See also* [JHN 1:9](https://ref.ly/John1:9), [JHN 8:56](https://ref.ly/John8:56); [1TI 3:16](https://ref.ly/1Tim3:16); [1JN 1:1–1:2](https://ref.ly/1John1:1-1John1:2), [1JN 4:2](https://ref.ly/1John4:2); [2JN 1:7](https://ref.ly/2John1:7)

Jesus Christ's incarnation involved a supernatural conception
-------------------------------------------------------------

**[LUK 1:35](https://ref.ly/Luke1:35)** *See also* [ISA 9:6](https://ref.ly/Isa9:6); [MAT 1:18](https://ref.ly/Matt1:18); [JHN 14:9](https://ref.ly/John14:9) *The incarnation was such that the Son was the exact representation of the Father*; [ROM 1:4](https://ref.ly/Rom1:4); [COL 1:15](https://ref.ly/Col1:15), [COL 1:19](https://ref.ly/Col1:19); [HEB 1:2–1:3](https://ref.ly/Heb1:2-Heb1:3)
